import { useState } from 'react';
import { useAuthStore } from '@/stores/authStore';
import { User, ActionPassword } from '@/types/auth';
import { X, Plus, Trash2, Save, Shield, Key, Users, Activity } from 'lucide-react';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { Input } from '@/components/ui/input';
import { Label } from '@/components/ui/label';
import { Switch } from '@/components/ui/switch';
import { Tabs, TabsContent, TabsList, TabsTrigger } from '@/components/ui/tabs';
import { Badge } from '@/components/ui/badge';
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';

export function AdminPanel() {
  const isAdminRoute = useAuthStore((s) => s.isAdminRoute);
  const adminLogin = useAuthStore((s) => s.adminLogin);
  const adminLogout = useAuthStore((s) => s.adminLogout);
  const users = useAuthStore((s) => s.users);
  const createUser = useAuthStore((s) => s.createUser);
  const updateUser = useAuthStore((s) => s.updateUser);
  const deleteUser = useAuthStore((s) => s.deleteUser);
  const setActionPassword = useAuthStore((s) => s.setActionPassword);

  const [adminPassword, setAdminPassword] = useState('');
  const [loginError, setLoginError] = useState('');
  
  const [newUser, setNewUser] = useState({ username: '', password: '', role: 'user' as const });
  const [editingUser, setEditingUser] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [actionPasswords, setActionPasswords] = useState({
    delete: { password: '', required: false },
    format: { password: '', required: false },
    rename: { password: '', required: false },
    dfol: { password: '', required: false },
  });

  if (!isAdminRoute) {
    return (
      <div className="min-h-screen flex items-center justify-center bg-background">
        <div className="w-full max-w-md p-6 bg-card border border-border rounded-lg shadow-lg">
          <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-6">
            <Shield className="w-6 h-6 text-primary" />
            <h1 className="text-xl font-bold">Admin Access</h1>
          </div>
          
          <div className="space-y-4">
            <div>
              <Label>Admin Password</Label>
              <Input
                type="password"
                value={adminPassword}
                onChange={(e) => setAdminPassword(e.target.value)}
                placeholder="Enter admin password"
              />
            </div>
            
            {loginError && (
              <p className="text-sm text-destructive">{loginError}</p>
            )}
            
            <Button 
              className="w-full" 
              onClick={() => {
                if (adminLogin(adminPassword)) {
                  setLoginError('');
                } else {
                  setLoginError('Invalid password');
                }
              }}
            >
              Login
            </Button>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    );
  }

  const handleCreateUser = async () => {
    try {
      await createUser(newUser.username, newUser.password, newUser.role);
      setNewUser({ username: '', password: '', role: 'user' });
    } catch (error) {
      alert((error as Error).message);
    }
  };

  const handleSaveActionPasswords = () => {
    Object.entries(actionPasswords).forEach(([action, config]) => {
      if (config.password) {
        setActionPassword(action, config.password, config.required);
      }
    });
    alert('Action passwords saved');
  };

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen bg-background p-6">
      <div className="max-w-6xl mx-auto">
        {/* Header */}
        <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-6">
          <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
            <Shield className="w-8 h-8 text-primary" />
            <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold">Admin Panel</h1>
          </div>
          <Button variant="outline" onClick={adminLogout}>
            <X className="w-4 h-4 mr-2" />
            Logout
          </Button>
        </div>

        <Tabs defaultValue="users">
          <TabsList className="mb-6">
            <TabsTrigger value="users" className="gap-2">
              <Users className="w-4 h-4" />
              Users
            </TabsTrigger>
            <TabsTrigger value="security" className="gap-2">
              <Key className="w-4 h-4" />
              Security
            </TabsTrigger>
            <TabsTrigger value="logs" className="gap-2">
              <Activity className="w-4 h-4" />
              System Logs
            </TabsTrigger>
          </TabsList>

          {/* Users Tab */}
          <TabsContent value="users" className="space-y-6">
            {/* Create User */}
            <div className="p-4 border border-border rounded-lg bg-card">
              <h3 className="font-semibold mb-4">Create New User</h3>
              <div className="grid grid-cols-3 gap-4">
                <div>
                  <Label>Username</Label>
                  <Input
                    value={newUser.username}
                    onChange={(e) => setNewUser({ ...newUser, username: e.target.value })}
                    placeholder="username"
                  />
                </div>
                <div>
                  <Label>Password</Label>
                  <Input
                    type="password"
                    value={newUser.password}
                    onChange={(e) => setNewUser({ ...newUser, password: e.target.value })}
                    placeholder="password"
                  />
                </div>
                <div>
                  <Label>Role</Label>
                  <select
                    value={newUser.role}
                    onChange={(e) => setNewUser({ ...newUser, role: e.target.value as any })}
                    className="w-full h-10 px-3 rounded-md border bg-background"
                  >
                    <option value="user">User</option>
                    <option value="admin">Admin</option>
                  </select>
                </div>
              </div>
              <Button className="mt-4" onClick={handleCreateUser}>
                <Plus className="w-4 h-4 mr-2" />
                Create User
              </Button>
            </div>

            {/* User List */}
            <div className="border border-border rounded-lg bg-card">
              <table className="w-full">
                <thead className="bg-muted">
                  <tr>
                    <th className="px-4 py-2 text-left text-sm font-medium">Username</th>
                    <th className="px-4 py-2 text-left text-sm font-medium">Role</th>
                    <th className="px-4 py-2 text-left text-sm font-medium">Status</th>
                    <th className="px-4 py-2 text-left text-sm font-medium">Last Login</th>
                    <th className="px-4 py-2 text-right text-sm font-medium">Actions</th>
                  </tr>
                </thead>
                <tbody className="divide-y divide-border">
                  {users.map((user) => (
                    <tr key={user.id} className={cn(!user.isActive && "opacity-50")}>
                      <td className="px-4 py-3">{user.username}</td>
                      <td className="px-4 py-3">
                        <Badge variant={user.role === 'admin' ? 'default' : 'secondary'}>
                          {user.role}
                        </Badge>
                      </td>
                      <td className="px-4 py-3">
                        <Badge variant={user.isActive ? 'outline' : 'destructive'}>
                          {user.isActive ? 'Active' : 'Inactive'}
                        </Badge>
                      </td>
                      <td className="px-4 py-3 text-sm text-muted-foreground">
                        {user.lastLogin?.toLocaleString() || 'Never'}
                      </td>
                      <td className="px-4 py-3 text-right">
                        <Button
                          variant="ghost"
                          size="sm"
                          onClick={() => deleteUser(user.id)}
                        >
                          <Trash2 className="w-4 h-4 text-destructive" />
                        </Button>
                      </td>
                    </tr>
                  ))}
                </tbody>
              </table>
            </div>
          </TabsContent>

          {/* Security Tab */}
          <TabsContent value="security" className="space-y-6">
            <div className="p-4 border border-border rounded-lg bg-card">
              <h3 className="font-semibold mb-4">Action Passwords</h3>
              <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground mb-4">
                Require additional passwords for sensitive operations
              </p>

              <div className="space-y-4">
                {(['delete', 'format', 'rename', 'dfol'] as const).map((action) => (
                  <div key={action} className="flex items-center justify-between p-3 border rounded-lg">
                    <div className="flex items-center gap-4">
                      <Switch
                        checked={actionPasswords[action].required}
                        onCheckedChange={(checked) => 
                          setActionPasswords({
                            ...actionPasswords,
                            [action]: { ...actionPasswords[action], required: checked }
                          })
                        }
                      />
                      <span className="font-medium capitalize">{action}</span>
                    </div>
                    
                    {actionPasswords[action].required && (
                      <Input
                        type="password"
                        placeholder={`${action} password`}
                        value={actionPasswords[action].password}
                        onChange={(e) => 
                          setActionPasswords({
                            ...actionPasswords,
                            [action]: { ...actionPasswords[action], password: e.target.value }
                          })
                        }
                        className="w-48"
                      />
                    )}
                  </div>
                ))}
              </div>

              <Button className="mt-4" onClick={handleSaveActionPasswords}>
                <Save className="w-4 h-4 mr-2" />
                Save Security Settings
              </Button>
            </div>
          </TabsContent>

          {/* Logs Tab */}
          <TabsContent value="logs">
            <div className="p-4 border border-border rounded-lg bg-card">
              <h3 className="font-semibold mb-4">System Logs</h3>
              <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">
                View and export system-wide logs
              </p>
              {/* Log viewer implementation */}
            </div>
          </TabsContent>
        </Tabs>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
import {
  DropdownMenu,
  DropdownMenuContent,
  DropdownMenuItem,
  DropdownMenuSeparator,
  DropdownMenuSub,
  DropdownMenuSubContent,
  DropdownMenuSubTrigger,
  DropdownMenuTrigger,
} from "@/components/ui/dropdown-menu";
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { 
  MoreVertical, 
  FolderDown, 
  FileText, 
  FileCode, 
  Archive,
  Check,
  TreePine,
  Pencil,
  Trash2
} from 'lucide-react';
import { useDFOLStore, useIsDFOLMode } from '@/stores/dfolStore';
import { DFOLItem, DFOLMode } from '@/types/dfol';

interface DFOLMenuProps {
  item: any;
  sourceType: 'storage' | 'drive' | 'github' | 'terminal';
  panelId: string;
  onRename?: () => void;
  onDelete?: () => void;
  onTreeView?: () => void;
}

export function DFOLMenu({ item, sourceType, panelId, onRename, onDelete, onTreeView }: DFOLMenuProps) {
  const isDFOLMode = useIsDFOLMode();
  const enterDFOLMode = useDFOLStore((s) => s.enterDFOLMode);
  const selectItem = useDFOLStore((s) => s.selectItem);
  const selectedItems = useDFOLStore((s) => s.selectedItems);
  
  const isSelected = selectedItems.some(i => i.id === (item.id || item.name));
  const selectedItem = selectedItems.find(i => i.id === (item.id || item.name));

  const handleDFOLSelect = (operations: DFOLMode[]) => {
    if (!isDFOLMode) {
      enterDFOLMode();
    }
    
    const dfolItem: DFOLItem = {
      id: item.id || item.name,
      name: item.name,
      sourceType,
      panelId,
      path: item.path || item.name,
      type: item.kind === 'directory' || item.type === 'directory' ? 'directory' : 'file',
      size: item.size || 0,
      handle: item.handle,
      operations,
    };
    
    selectItem(dfolItem, operations);
  };

  return (
    <DropdownMenu>
      <DropdownMenuTrigger asChild>
        <Button variant="ghost" size="icon" className="h-6 w-6">
          <MoreVertical className="w-4 h-4" />
        </Button>
      </DropdownMenuTrigger>
      
      <DropdownMenuContent align="end" className="w-56">
        {/* Standard Actions */}
        <DropdownMenuItem onClick={onTreeView}>
          <TreePine className="w-4 h-4 mr-2" />
          View Tree
        </DropdownMenuItem>
        
        <DropdownMenuItem onClick={onRename}>
          <Pencil className="w-4 h-4 mr-2" />
          Rename
        </DropdownMenuItem>
        
        <DropdownMenuSeparator />
        
        {/* DFOL Section */}
        <DropdownMenuSub>
          <DropdownMenuSubTrigger className={isSelected ? "bg-primary/10" : ""}>
            <FolderDown className="w-4 h-4 mr-2" />
            DFOL Dump
            {isSelected && <Check className="w-3 h-3 ml-auto" />}
          </DropdownMenuSubTrigger>
          
          <DropdownMenuSubContent className="w-48">
            <DropdownMenuItem onClick={() => handleDFOLSelect(['folder'])}>
              <FolderDown className="w-4 h-4 mr-2" />
              Folder Dump
            </DropdownMenuItem>
            
            <DropdownMenuItem onClick={() => handleDFOLSelect(['txt'])}>
              <FileText className="w-4 h-4 mr-2" />
              TXT Dump
            </DropdownMenuItem>
            
            <DropdownMenuItem onClick={() => handleDFOLSelect(['pdf'])}>
              <FileCode className="w-4 h-4 mr-2" />
              PDF Dump
            </DropdownMenuItem>
            
            <DropdownMenuItem onClick={() => handleDFOLSelect(['compress'])}>
              <Archive className="w-4 h-4 mr-2" />
              Compress
            </DropdownMenuItem>
            
            <DropdownMenuSeparator />
            
            <DropdownMenuItem onClick={() => handleDFOLSelect(['folder', 'txt', 'compress'])}>
              <Check className="w-4 h-4 mr-2" />
              All Operations
            </DropdownMenuItem>
          </DropdownMenuSubContent>
        </DropdownMenuSub>
        
        <DropdownMenuSeparator />
        
        <DropdownMenuItem onClick={onDelete} className="text-destructive">
          <Trash2 className="w-4 h-4 mr-2" />
          Delete
        </DropdownMenuItem>
      </DropdownMenuContent>
    </DropdownMenu>
  );
}

import { Zap } from 'lucide-react';

export function DFOLModeIndicator({ isActive = false }: { isActive?: boolean }) {
  if (!isActive) return null;
  return (
    <div className="fixed top-4 right-4 z-50 flex items-center gap-2 px-3 py-1.5 rounded-full text-xs font-medium bg-yellow-500/10 text-yellow-600 border">
      <Zap className="w-3 h-3" />DFOL Mode
    </div>
  );
}

FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/prakash-app/src/components/DFOL/ExecutePanel.tsx
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
import { useDFOLStore, useDFOLOperations, useDFOLGlobalProgress, useDFOLIsExecuting } from '@/stores/dfolStore';
import { X, Play, Pause, RotateCcw, Check, AlertCircle, FolderDown, FileText, FileCode, Archive } from 'lucide-react';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { Progress } from '@/components/ui/progress';
import { Badge } from '@/components/ui/badge';
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';
import { ScrollArea } from '@/components/ui/scroll-area';

const modeIcons: Record<string, React.ReactNode> = {
  folder: <FolderDown className="w-4 h-4" />,
  txt: <FileText className="w-4 h-4" />,
  pdf: <FileCode className="w-4 h-4" />,
  compress: <Archive className="w-4 h-4" />,
};

export function ExecutePanel() {
  const showExecutePanel = useDFOLStore((s) => s.showExecutePanel);
  const hideExecutePanel = useDFOLStore((s) => s.hideExecutePanel);
  const operations = useDFOLOperations();
  const globalProgress = useDFOLGlobalProgress();
  const isExecuting = useDFOLIsExecuting();
  const stats = useDFOLStore((s) => s.getOperationStats());
  
  if (!showExecutePanel) return null;

  return (
    <div className="fixed inset-0 z-50 flex items-center justify-center bg-black/50 p-4">
      <div className="w-full max-w-3xl max-h-[85vh] bg-background rounded-lg shadow-2xl flex flex-col overflow-hidden">
        {/* Header */}
        <div className="flex items-center justify-between p-4 border-b border-border bg-card">
          <div>
            <h2 className="text-lg font-semibold flex items-center gap-2">
              <Play className="w-5 h-5 text-primary" />
              DFOL Execution
            </h2>
            <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">
              Output: {useDFOLStore.getState().outputDirectory}
            </p>
          </div>
          
          <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
            {!isExecuting && stats.completed > 0 && (
              <Button variant="outline" size="sm" onClick={() => useDFOLStore.getState().executeOperations()}>
                <RotateCcw className="w-4 h-4 mr-2" />
                Retry Failed
              </Button>
            )}
            <Button variant="ghost" size="icon" onClick={hideExecutePanel}>
              <X className="w-4 h-4" />
            </Button>
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* Global Progress */}
        <div className="p-4 border-b border-border bg-muted/50">
          <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-2">
            <span className="text-sm font-medium">Overall Progress</span>
            <span className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">{Math.round(globalProgress)}%</span>
          </div>
          <Progress value={globalProgress} className="h-2" />
          
          <div className="flex items-center gap-4 mt-3 text-xs">
            <Badge variant="secondary">Total: {stats.total}</Badge>
            <Badge variant="outline" className="text-yellow-600">Pending: {stats.pending}</Badge>
            <Badge variant="outline" className="text-blue-600">Running: {stats.running}</Badge>
            <Badge variant="outline" className="text-green-600">Completed: {stats.completed}</Badge>
            <Badge variant="destructive">Failed: {stats.failed}</Badge>
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* Operations List */}
        <ScrollArea className="flex-1 p-4">
          <div className="space-y-2">
            {operations.map((op) => (
              <div
                key={op.id}
                className={cn(
                  "flex items-center gap-3 p-3 rounded-lg border transition-colors",
                  op.status === 'running' && "bg-primary/5 border-primary/20",
                  op.status === 'completed' && "bg-green-50 border-green-200",
                  op.status === 'failed' && "bg-destructive/5 border-destructive/20",
                  op.status === 'pending' && "bg-muted border-border"
                )}
              >
                {/* Status Icon */}
                <div className={cn(
                  "w-8 h-8 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center shrink-0",
                  op.status === 'completed' && "bg-green-100 text-green-600",
                  op.status === 'failed' && "bg-destructive/10 text-destructive",
                  op.status === 'running' && "bg-primary/10 text-primary",
                  op.status === 'pending' && "bg-muted text-muted-foreground"
                )}>
                  {op.status === 'completed' && <Check className="w-4 h-4" />}
                  {op.status === 'failed' && <AlertCircle className="w-4 h-4" />}
                  {op.status === 'running' && (
                    <div className="w-4 h-4 border-2 border-primary border-t-transparent rounded-full animate-spin" />
                  )}
                  {op.status === 'pending' && <span className="text-xs">•</span>}
                </div>

                {/* Content */}
                <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
                  <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                    {modeIcons[op.mode]}
                    <span className="font-medium text-sm">{op.itemId}</span>
                    <Badge variant="outline" className="text-xs capitalize">
                      {op.mode}
                    </Badge>
                  </div>
                  
                  <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground truncate">
                    {op.message}
                  </p>
                  
                  {op.status === 'running' && (
                    <Progress value={op.progress} className="h-1 mt-2" />
                  )}
                  
                  {op.result && (
                    <p className="text-xs text-green-600 mt-1">
                      ✓ {formatBytes(op.result.size)} → {op.result.outputPath}
                    </p>
                  )}
                  
                  {op.error && (
                    <p className="text-xs text-destructive mt-1">
                      ✗ {op.error}
                    </p>
                  )}
                </div>

                {/* Progress % */}
                <div className="text-sm font-medium w-12 text-right">
                  {op.status === 'running' ? `${op.progress}%` : 
                   op.status === 'completed' ? '100%' : '-'}
                </div>
              </div>
            ))}
          </div>
        </ScrollArea>

        {/* Footer */}
        <div className="p-4 border-t border-border bg-card">
          <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
            <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">
              {isExecuting ? 'Processing...' : 'Execution complete'}
            </p>
            <Button onClick={hideExecutePanel} disabled={isExecuting}>
              {isExecuting ? 'Running...' : 'Close'}
            </Button>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

function formatBytes(bytes?: number): string {
  if (!bytes) return '-';
  const units = ['B', 'KB', 'MB', 'GB'];
  let size = bytes;
  let unitIndex = 0;
  while (size >= 1024 && unitIndex < units.length - 1) {
    size /= 1024;
    unitIndex++;
  }
  return `${size.toFixed(1)} ${units[unitIndex]}`;
}

import { useDFOLStore, useDFOLNotifications } from '@/stores/dfolStore';
import { X, Check, AlertCircle, Info, Bell } from 'lucide-react';
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';
import { useEffect } from 'react';

export function NotificationPanel() {
  const notifications = useDFOLNotifications();
  const dismissNotification = useDFOLStore((s) => s.dismissNotification);

  if (notifications.length === 0) return null;

  return (
    <div className="fixed top-4 right-4 z-50 flex flex-col gap-2 max-w-sm">
      {notifications.map((notif) => (
        <div
          key={notif.id}
          className={cn(
            "flex items-start gap-3 p-4 rounded-lg shadow-lg border animate-in slide-in-from-right",
            notif.type === 'success' && "bg-green-50 border-green-200 text-green-800",
            notif.type === 'error' && "bg-destructive/10 border-destructive/20 text-destructive",
            notif.type === 'warning' && "bg-yellow-50 border-yellow-200 text-yellow-800",
            notif.type === 'info' && "bg-blue-50 border-blue-200 text-blue-800"
          )}
        >
          <div className="shrink-0 mt-0.5">
            {notif.type === 'success' && <Check className="w-5 h-5" />}
            {notif.type === 'error' && <AlertCircle className="w-5 h-5" />}
            {notif.type === 'warning' && <Bell className="w-5 h-5" />}
            {notif.type === 'info' && <Info className="w-5 h-5" />}
          </div>
          
          <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
            <p className="text-sm font-medium">{notif.message}</p>
            {notif.operationId && (
              <p className="text-xs opacity-75 mt-1">
                Operation: {notif.operationId.slice(0, 8)}...
              </p>
            )}
          </div>
          
          <button
            onClick={() => dismissNotification(notif.id)}
            className="shrink-0 opacity-50 hover:opacity-100"
          >
            <X className="w-4 h-4" />
          </button>
        </div>
      ))}
    </div>
  );
}

import { X, Plus, Trash2, Save, Lock, Unlock, Zap, Gauge, Turtle } from 'lucide-react';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { Input } from '@/components/ui/input';

import { useState } from 'react';
import { DFOLProfile } from '@/types/dfol';
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';

export function ProfilePanel() {
  const showProfilePanel = useDFOLStore((s) => s.showProfilePanel);
  const hideProfilePanel = useDFOLStore((s) => s.hideProfilePanel);
  const profiles = useDFOLProfiles();
  const activeProfile = useDFOLActiveProfile();
  const setActiveProfile = useDFOLStore((s) => s.setActiveProfile);
  const addCustomProfile = useDFOLStore((s) => s.addCustomProfile);
  const removeCustomProfile = useDFOLStore((s) => s.removeCustomProfile);
  
  const [isCreating, setIsCreating] = useState(false);
  const [newProfile, setNewProfile] = useState<Partial<DFOLProfile>>({
    format: 'zip',
    compressionLevel: 'normal',
    encryptFilenames: false,
  });

  if (!showProfilePanel) return null;

  const handleSaveProfile = () => {
    if (!newProfile.name) return;
    
    const profile: DFOLProfile = {
      id: `custom-${Date.now()}`,
      name: newProfile.name,
      format: newProfile.format as any,
      compressionLevel: newProfile.compressionLevel as any,
      encryptFilenames: newProfile.encryptFilenames || false,
      password: newProfile.password,
      splitSize: newProfile.splitSize,
    };
    
    addCustomProfile(profile);
    setIsCreating(false);
    setNewProfile({ format: 'zip', compressionLevel: 'normal', encryptFilenames: false });
  };

  const getCompressionIcon = (level: string) => {
    switch (level) {
      case 'store': return <Unlock className="w-4 h-4" />;
      case 'fast': return <Zap className="w-4 h-4" />;
      case 'normal': return <Gauge className="w-4 h-4" />;
      case 'maximum': return <Turtle className="w-4 h-4" />;
      default: return <Gauge className="w-4 h-4" />;
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="fixed inset-0 z-50 flex items-center justify-center bg-black/50 p-4">
      <div className="w-full max-w-2xl max-h-[80vh] bg-background rounded-lg shadow-2xl flex flex-col overflow-hidden">
        {/* Header */}
        <div className="flex items-center justify-between p-4 border-b border-border">
          <h2 className="text-lg font-semibold">Compression Profiles</h2>
          <Button variant="ghost" size="icon" onClick={hideProfilePanel}>
            <X className="w-4 h-4" />
          </Button>
        </div>

        {/* Content */}
        <div className="flex-1 overflow-auto p-4 space-y-4">
          {/* Existing Profiles */}

              <Plus className="w-4 h-4 mr-2" />
              Create Custom Profile
            </Button>
          )}

      </div>

FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/prakash-app/src/components/DragDrop/DragDropItem.tsx
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';
import { Check, GripVertical } from 'lucide-react';
import { useDragDrop } from './useDragDrop';
import { SourceType } from '@/types/dragDrop';

interface DragDropItemProps {
  children: React.ReactNode;
  item: any;
  id: string;
  sourceType: SourceType;
  panelId: string;
  className?: string;
  onDrop?: (items: any[], operation: 'copy' | 'move') => void;
}

export function DragDropItem({
  children,
  item,
  id,
  sourceType,
  panelId,
  className,
  onDrop,
}: DragDropItemProps) {
  const {
    setRef,
    isSelected,
    isDragging,
    isOver,
    canDrop,
    isPressed,
    isDragMode,
    toggleSelection,
    handlers,
  } = useDragDrop({ item, id, sourceType, panelId, onDrop });

  return (
    <div
      ref={setRef}
      className={cn(
        "relative transition-all",
        isSelected && "ring-2 ring-primary bg-primary/5",
        isDragging && "opacity-50",
        isOver && canDrop && "bg-accent/50 ring-2 ring-accent",
        isPressed && "scale-95",
        className
      )}
      {...handlers}
    >
      {/* Selection checkbox */}
      {isDragMode && (
        <div 
          className="absolute top-2 left-2 z-10"
          onClick={(e) => {
            e.stopPropagation();
            toggleSelection();
          }}
        >
          <div className={cn(
            "w-5 h-5 rounded border-2 flex items-center justify-center cursor-pointer",
            isSelected 
              ? "bg-primary border-primary text-primary-foreground" 
              : "border-muted-foreground bg-background"
          )}>
            {isSelected && <Check className="w-3 h-3" />}
          </div>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* Drag handle indicator */}
      {isDragMode && isSelected && (
        <div className="absolute top-2 right-2 z-10 p-1 bg-primary/10 rounded cursor-move">
          <GripVertical className="w-4 h-4 text-primary" />
        </div>
      )}

      {children}
    </div>
  );
}

FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/prakash-app/src/components/DragDrop/DropHandler.tsx
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
import { useEffect } from 'react';
import { useDragDropStore, usePendingOperation, useTargetPanel, useSelectedItems, useDragSourcePanel } from '@/stores/dragDropStore';
import { usePanelStore } from '@/stores/panelStore';
import { fileSystemBackend } from '@/lib/fileSystemBackend';
import { githubApi } from '@/lib/githubApi';
import { webcontainerApi } from '@/lib/webcontainerApi';

// This component handles the actual copy/move operations when confirmed
export function DropHandler() {
  const showConfirm = useDragDropStore((s) => s.showConfirmDialog);
  const pendingOperation = usePendingOperation();
  const targetPanel = useTargetPanel();
  const sourcePanel = useDragSourcePanel();
  const selectedItems = useSelectedItems();

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!showConfirm && pendingOperation && targetPanel && sourcePanel) {
      executeOperation();
    }
  }, [showConfirm, pendingOperation, targetPanel, sourcePanel]);

  const executeOperation = async () => {
    const targetPanelState = usePanelStore.getState().getPanel(targetPanel!);
    
    if (!targetPanelState) return;

    console.log(`Executing ${pendingOperation} from ${sourcePanel} to ${targetPanel}`);

    for (const item of selectedItems) {
      try {
        switch (targetPanelState.source) {
          case 'storage':
            await handleStorageDrop(item, pendingOperation!);
            break;
          case 'drive':
            // TODO: Implement Google Drive write operations
            console.log('Drive drop not yet implemented');
            break;
          case 'github':
            // GitHub requires commit operations - read-only for now
            console.log('GitHub is read-only');
            break;
          case 'terminal':
            await handleTerminalDrop(item, pendingOperation!);
            break;
        }
      } catch (error) {
        console.error(`Failed to ${pendingOperation} ${item.id}:`, error);
      }
    }

    // Reset drag state
    useDragDropStore.getState().exitDragMode();
  };

  const handleStorageDrop = async (item: any, operation: 'copy' | 'move') => {
    // TODO: Implement actual file system copy/move
    // This requires access to the source file handle and target directory handle
    console.log(`Storage ${operation}:`, item);
  };

  const handleTerminalDrop = async (item: any, operation: 'copy' | 'move') => {
    // TODO: Implement WebContainer FS operations
    console.log(`Terminal ${operation}:`, item);
  };

  return null; // This is a logic-only component
}
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/prakash-app/src/components/DragDrop/useDragDrop.ts
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
import { useDrag, useDrop } from 'react-dnd';
import { useCallback, useRef, useState } from 'react';
import { useDragDropStore, useIsDragMode, useSelectedItems } from '@/stores/dragDropStore';
import { SelectedItem, SourceType } from '@/types/dragDrop';

interface UseDragDropOptions {
  item: any;
  id: string;
  sourceType: SourceType;
  panelId: string;
  onDrop?: (items: SelectedItem[], operation: 'copy' | 'move') => void;
}

export function useDragDrop({ item, id, sourceType, panelId, onDrop }: UseDragDropOptions) {
  const isDragMode = useIsDragMode();
  const selectedItems = useSelectedItems();
  const dragDropStore = useDragDropStore();
  
  const [isSelected, setIsSelected] = useState(false);
  const [isPressed, setIsPressed] = useState(false);
  const longPressTimer = useRef<NodeJS.Timeout | null>(null);
  const touchStartPos = useRef<{ x: number; y: number } | null>(null);

  // Check if this item is selected
  const isItemSelected = selectedItems.some(
    (si) => si.id === id && si.panelId === panelId
  );

  // Toggle selection
  const toggleSelection = useCallback(() => {
    const selectedItem: SelectedItem = {
      id,
      sourceType,
      item,
      panelId,
    };
    dragDropStore.toggleSelection(selectedItem);
  }, [id, sourceType, item, panelId, dragDropStore]);

  // Long press / touch handlers
  const handleTouchStart = useCallback((e: React.TouchEvent) => {
    const touch = e.touches[0];
    touchStartPos.current = { x: touch.clientX, y: touch.clientY };
    setIsPressed(true);
    
    // Start long press timer
    longPressTimer.current = setTimeout(() => {
      if (!isDragMode) {
        dragDropStore.enterDragMode(panelId);
        toggleSelection();
      }
    }, 500); // 500ms long press
  }, [isDragMode, panelId, dragDropStore, toggleSelection]);

  const handleTouchMove = useCallback((e: React.TouchEvent) => {
    if (!touchStartPos.current) return;
    
    const touch = e.touches[0];
    const deltaX = Math.abs(touch.clientX - touchStartPos.current.x);
    const deltaY = Math.abs(touch.clientY - touchStartPos.current.y);
    
    // Cancel long press if moved too much
    if (deltaX > 10 || deltaY > 10) {
      if (longPressTimer.current) {
        clearTimeout(longPressTimer.current);
        longPressTimer.current = null;
      }
      setIsPressed(false);
    }
    
    // Update drag position if in drag mode
    if (isDragMode && dragDropStore.isDragging) {
      dragDropStore.setDragImagePosition({ x: touch.clientX, y: touch.clientY });
    }
  }, [isDragMode, dragDropStore]);

  const handleTouchEnd = useCallback((e: React.TouchEvent) => {
    if (longPressTimer.current) {
      clearTimeout(longPressTimer.current);
      longPressTimer.current = null;
    }
    setIsPressed(false);
    touchStartPos.current = null;
    
    // If in drag mode and not dragging yet, start drag
    if (isDragMode && !dragDropStore.isDragging && isItemSelected) {
      const touch = e.changedTouches[0];
      dragDropStore.startDrag(panelId, { x: touch.clientX, y: touch.clientY });
    }
  }, [isDragMode, dragDropStore, isItemSelected, panelId]);

  // Mouse handlers for desktop
  const handleMouseDown = useCallback((e: React.MouseEvent) => {
    if (e.button !== 0) return; // Only left click
    
    if (isDragMode) {
      e.preventDefault();
      toggleSelection();
      
      if (!dragDropStore.isDragging && isItemSelected) {
        dragDropStore.startDrag(panelId, { x: e.clientX, y: e.clientY });
      }
    }
  }, [isDragMode, dragDropStore, isItemSelected, panelId, toggleSelection]);

  // React DnD setup
  const [{ isDragging }, drag] = useDrag(() => ({
    type: sourceType,
    item: { id, sourceType, item, panelId },
    collect: (monitor) => ({
      isDragging: !!monitor.isDragging(),
    }),
    canDrag: isDragMode && isItemSelected,
  }), [isDragMode, isItemSelected, id, sourceType, item, panelId]);

  const [{ isOver, canDrop }, drop] = useDrop(() => ({
    accept: ['storage', 'drive', 'github', 'terminal'],
    drop: (droppedItem: any, monitor) => {
      if (!monitor.didDrop()) {
        // Show confirm dialog
        dragDropStore.setTargetPanel(panelId);
        // The operation type will be set by the drag overlay buttons
      }
    },
    collect: (monitor) => ({
      isOver: !!monitor.isOver(),
      canDrop: !!monitor.canDrop(),
    }),
    canDrop: (droppedItem: any) => {
      // Don't drop on same panel
      return droppedItem.panelId !== panelId;
    },
  }), [panelId, dragDropStore]);

  // Combine refs
  const setRefs = useCallback((node: HTMLElement | null) => {
    drag(node);
    drop(node);
  }, [drag, drop]);

  return {
    setRef: setRefs,
    isSelected: isItemSelected,
    isDragging: isDragging || dragDropStore.isDragging,
    isOver,
    canDrop,
    isPressed,
    isDragMode,
    toggleSelection,
    handlers: {
      onTouchStart: handleTouchStart,
      onTouchMove: handleTouchMove,
      onTouchEnd: handleTouchEnd,
      onMouseDown: handleMouseDown,
    },
  };
}
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/prakash-app/src/components/DragDrop/DragDropProvider.tsx
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
"use client"
import React, { createContext, useContext, useState, useCallback } from 'react';

interface DragDropContextType {
  isDragging: boolean;
  dragData: any;
  startDrag: (data: any) => void;
  endDrag: () => void;
}

const DragDropContext = createContext<DragDropContextType | null>(null);

export function DragDropProvider({ children }: { children: React.ReactNode }) {
  const [isDragging, setIsDragging] = useState(false);
  const [dragData, setDragData] = useState<any>(null);

  const startDrag = useCallback((data: any) => {
    setDragData(data);
    setIsDragging(true);
  }, []);

  const endDrag = useCallback(() => {
    setIsDragging(false);
    setDragData(null);
  }, []);

  return (
    <DragDropContext.Provider value={{ isDragging, dragData, startDrag, endDrag }}>
      {children}
    </DragDropContext.Provider>
  );
}

export const useDragDrop = () => {
  const context = useContext(DragDropContext);
  if (!context) throw new Error('useDragDrop must be used within DragDropProvider');
  return context;
};

import { useState } from 'react';
import {
  Dialog,
  DialogContent,
  DialogDescription,
  DialogFooter,
  DialogHeader,
  DialogTitle,
} from "@/components/ui/dialog";
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { Input } from '@/components/ui/input';
import { usePanelStore } from '@/stores/panelStore';
import { fileSystemBackend } from '@/lib/fileSystemBackend';

interface CreateFolderDialogProps {
  open: boolean;
  onOpenChange: (open: boolean) => void;
  panelId: string;
}

export function CreateFolderDialog({ open, onOpenChange, panelId }: CreateFolderDialogProps) {
  const [folderName, setFolderName] = useState('');
  const [isCreating, setIsCreating] = useState(false);
  const panel = usePanelStore((s) => s.getPanel(panelId));

  const handleCreate = async () => {
    if (!folderName.trim() || !panel?.handle) return;
    
    setIsCreating(true);
    try {
      await fileSystemBackend.createDirectory(panel.handle, folderName.trim());
      // Refresh will happen via parent component
      onOpenChange(false);
      setFolderName('');
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('Failed to create folder:', err);
    } finally {
      setIsCreating(false);
    }
  };

  return (
    <Dialog open={open} onOpenChange={onOpenChange}>
      <DialogContent className="sm:max-w-md">
        <DialogHeader>
          <DialogTitle>Create New Folder</DialogTitle>
          <DialogDescription>
            Enter a name for the new folder.
          </DialogDescription>
        </DialogHeader>
        
        <div className="py-4">
          <Input
            placeholder="Folder name"
            value={folderName}
            onChange={(e) => setFolderName(e.target.value)}
            onKeyDown={(e) => {
              if (e.key === 'Enter') handleCreate();
            }}
            autoFocus
          />
        </div>

        <DialogFooter>
          <Button variant="outline" onClick={() => onOpenChange(false)}>
            Cancel
          </Button>
          <Button 
            onClick={handleCreate} 
            disabled={!folderName.trim() || isCreating}
          >
            {isCreating ? 'Creating...' : 'Create'}
          </Button>
        </DialogFooter>
      </DialogContent>
    </Dialog>
  );
}

import { FileSystemEntry, FileSystemDirectoryEntry } from '@/types/filesystem';
import { File, FolderOpen, Pencil } from 'lucide-react';
import { formatDistanceToNow } from 'date-fns';
import { DragDropItem } from '../DragDrop/DragDropItem';
import { InlineRenameInput } from '../Rename/InlineRenameInput';
import { useRenameStore } from '@/stores/renameStore';
import { useState } from 'react';

interface FileGridProps {
  entries: FileSystemEntry[];
  onNavigate: (entry: FileSystemDirectoryEntry) => void;
  panelId: string;
}

export function FileGrid({ entries, onNavigate, panelId }: FileGridProps) {

  const handleClick = (entry: FileSystemEntry) => {
    if (renamingId) return;

      onNavigate(entry as FileSystemDirectoryEntry);
    }

    setRenamingId(null);
  };

  return (
    <div className="grid grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-3 xl:grid-cols-4 gap-3 p-3">
      {entries.map((entry) => {
        const isRenaming = renamingId === entry.name;
        
        return (
          <DragDropItem
            key={entry.name}
            item={entry}
            id={entry.name}
            sourceType="storage"
            panelId={panelId}
            className="group flex flex-col items-center p-4 rounded-lg border border-border bg-card hover:bg-accent transition-all text-left relative"
          >
            {isRenaming ? (
              <div className="w-full">
                <InlineRenameInput
                  item={{
                    id: entry.name,
                    name: entry.name,
                    path: entry.handle?.name || entry.name,
                    sourceType: 'storage',
                    panelId,
                    handle: entry.handle,
                  }}
                  onComplete={handleRenameComplete}
                />
              </div>
            ) : (
              <>
                {/* Rename button */}
                <button
                  onClick={(e) => startRename(entry, e)}
                  className="absolute top-2 right-2 p-1 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 hover:bg-accent rounded transition-opacity"
                >
                  <Pencil className="w-3 h-3 text-muted-foreground" />
                </button>

                <div 
                  className="mb-2 text-primary group-hover:scale-110 transition-transform"
                  onClick={() => handleClick(entry)}
                >
                  {entry.kind === 'directory' ? (
                    <FolderOpen className="w-10 h-10" />
                  ) : (
                    <File className="w-10 h-10" />
                  )}
                </div>
                
                <p className="text-sm font-medium text-foreground truncate w-full text-center" title={entry.name}>
                  {entry.name}
                </p>
                <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-1">
                  {entry.kind === 'file' ? formatFileSize(entry.size) : 'Folder'}
                </p>
                <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">
                  {formatDistanceToNow(entry.lastModified, { addSuffix: true })}
                </p>
              </>
            )}
          </DragDropItem>
        );
      })}
    </div>
  );
}

function formatFileSize(bytes: number): string {
  if (bytes === 0) return '-';
  const units = ['B', 'KB', 'MB', 'GB', 'TB'];
  let size = bytes;
  let unitIndex = 0;
  while (size >= 1024 && unitIndex < units.length - 1) {
    size /= 1024;
    unitIndex++;
  }
  return `${size.toFixed(1)} ${units[unitIndex]}`;
}
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/prakash-app/src/components/FileManager/FileList.tsx
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
import { FileSystemEntry, FileSystemDirectoryEntry } from '@/types/filesystem';
import { Folder, File, ChevronRight, Pencil } from 'lucide-react';
import { formatDistanceToNow } from 'date-fns';
import { DragDropItem } from '../DragDrop/DragDropItem';
import { InlineRenameInput } from '../Rename/InlineRenameInput';
import { DFOLMenu } from '../DFOL/DFOLMenu';
import { TreeIconButton } from '../Tree/TreeIconButton';
import { useState } from 'react';

interface FileListProps {
  entries: FileSystemEntry[];
  onNavigate: (entry: FileSystemDirectoryEntry) => void;
  panelId: string;
}

export function FileList({ entries, onNavigate, panelId }: FileListProps) {
  const [renamingId, setRenamingId] = useState<string | null>(null);

  const handleClick = (entry: FileSystemEntry) => {
    if (renamingId) return;
    if (entry.kind === 'directory') {
      onNavigate(entry as FileSystemDirectoryEntry);
    }
  };

  const startRename = (entry: FileSystemEntry, e: React.MouseEvent) => {
    e.stopPropagation();
    setRenamingId(entry.name);
  };

  const handleRenameComplete = () => setRenamingId(null);

  return (
    <div className="divide-y divide-border">
      {entries.map((entry) => {
        const isRenaming = renamingId === entry.name;
        return (
          <DragDropItem
            key={entry.name}
            item={entry}
            id={entry.name}
            sourceType="storage"
            panelId={panelId}
            className="group flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-2 hover:bg-accent cursor-pointer transition-colors"
          >
            <div className="flex items-center gap-3 flex-1 min-w-0" onClick={() => handleClick(entry)}>
              {entry.kind === 'directory' ? (
                <Folder className="w-5 h-5 text-primary shrink-0" />
              ) : (
                <File className="w-5 h-5 text-muted-foreground shrink-0" />
              )}
              {isRenaming ? (
                <InlineRenameInput
                  item={{
                    id: entry.name,
                    name: entry.name,
                    path: entry.handle?.name || entry.name,
                    sourceType: 'storage',
                    panelId,
                    handle: entry.handle,
                  }}
                  onComplete={handleRenameComplete}
                />
              ) : (
                <span className="text-sm font-medium truncate">{entry.name}</span>
              )}
              {entry.kind === 'file' && !isRenaming && (
                <span className="text-xs text-muted-foreground shrink-0">{formatBytes(entry.size)}</span>
              )}
            </div>
            <div className="flex items-center gap-2 shrink-0">
              {!isRenaming && (
                <>
                  <button
                    onClick={(e) => startRename(entry, e)}
                    className="p-1 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 hover:bg-accent rounded transition-opacity"
                  >
                    <Pencil className="w-3 h-3 text-muted-foreground" />
                  </button>
                  <TreeIconButton item={entry} sourceType="storage" panelId={panelId} className="h-7 w-7 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100" />
                  <DFOLMenu item={entry} sourceType="storage" panelId={panelId} onRename={() => startRename(entry, {} as any)} onDelete={() => {}} onTreeView={() => {}} />
                  <ChevronRight className="w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100" />
                </>
              )}
            </div>
          </DragDropItem>
        );
      })}
    </div>
  );
}

function formatBytes(bytes: number): string {
  if (bytes === 0) return '-';
  const units = ['B', 'KB', 'MB', 'GB'];
  let size = bytes;
  let unitIndex = 0;
  while (size >= 1024 && unitIndex < units.length - 1) { size /= 1024; unitIndex++; }
  return `${size.toFixed(1)} ${units[unitIndex]}`;
}

} from "@/components/ui/dropdown-menu";
import { ViewMode, SortBy } from '@/types/filesystem';

interface ToolbarProps {
  viewMode: ViewMode;
  onViewModeChange: (mode: ViewMode) => void;
  sortBy: SortBy;
  onSortChange: (sort: SortBy) => void;
  onCreateFolder: () => void;
  onNavigateBack: () => void;
  onRefresh: () => void;
  canGoBack: boolean;
  isLoading: boolean;
  currentPath: string;
}

const sortLabels: Record<SortBy, string> = {
  'name-asc': 'Name (A-Z)',
  'name-desc': 'Name (Z-A)',
  'date': 'Date Modified',
  'size': 'Size',
};

export function Toolbar({ 
  viewMode, 
  onViewModeChange, 
  sortBy, 
  onSortChange,
  onCreateFolder,
  onNavigateBack,
  onRefresh,
  canGoBack,
  isLoading,
  currentPath
}: ToolbarProps) {
  return (
    <div className="flex items-center justify-between p-3 border-b border-border bg-card">
      {/* Left: Navigation */}
      <div className="flex items-center gap-2 min-w-0">

          variant="outline"
          size="icon"
          onClick={onNavigateBack}
          disabled={!canGoBack}
          className="h-8 w-8 shrink-0"
        >
          <ArrowLeft className="h-4 w-4" />
        </Button>
        
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2 ml-2 min-w-0">
          <span className="text-xs font-medium text-foreground truncate">
            {currentPath === '/' ? 'Root' : currentPath}
          </span>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Right: Actions */}
      <div className="flex items-center gap-1 shrink-0">
        <Button
          variant="ghost"
          size="icon"
          onClick={onRefresh}
          disabled={isLoading}
          className="h-8 w-8"
        >
          <RefreshCw className={`h-4 w-4 ${isLoading ? 'animate-spin' : ''}`} />
        </Button>

        <Button
          variant="ghost"
          size="icon"
          onClick={onCreateFolder}
          className="h-8 w-8"
        >
          <FolderPlus className="h-4 w-4" />
        </Button>

        <DropdownMenu>
          <DropdownMenuTrigger asChild>
            <Button variant="ghost" size="icon" className="h-8 w-8">
              <ArrowUpDown className="h-4 w-4" />
            </Button>
          </DropdownMenuTrigger>
          <DropdownMenuContent align="end">
            <DropdownMenuItem onClick={() => onSortChange('name-asc')}>
              Name (A-Z)
            </DropdownMenuItem>
            <DropdownMenuItem onClick={() => onSortChange('name-desc')}>

  );
}

import { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { Toolbar } from './Toolbar';
import { FileGrid } from './FileGrid';
import { FileList } from './FileList';
import { CreateFolderDialog } from './CreateFolderDialog';
import { MountPointsView } from './MountPointsView';
import { useFileSystemStore, useEntries, useViewMode, useSortBy, useCurrentHandle, useIsLoading, useCurrentPath, useHistory } from '@/stores/fileSystemStore';
import { ViewMode, SortBy } from '@/types/filesystem';

export function FileManager() {
  const [createDialogOpen, setCreateDialogOpen] = useState(false);
  
  const entries = useEntries();
  const viewMode = useViewMode();
  const sortBy = useSortBy();
  const currentHandle = useCurrentHandle();
  const isLoading = useIsLoading();
  const currentPath = useCurrentPath();
  const history = useHistory();
  
  const setViewMode = useFileSystemStore((s) => s.setViewMode);
  const setSortBy = useFileSystemStore((s) => s.setSortBy);
  const initMountPoints = useFileSystemStore((s) => s.initMountPoints);
  const navigateBack = useFileSystemStore((s) => s.navigateBack);
  const refreshCurrent = useFileSystemStore((s) => s.refreshCurrent);
  const createFolder = useFileSystemStore((s) => s.createFolder);
  const navigateTo = useFileSystemStore((s) => s.navigateTo);

  useEffect(() => {
    initMountPoints();
  }, [initMountPoints]);

  const handleCreateFolder = () => setCreateDialogOpen(true);
  const handleCreateConfirm = async (name: string) => {
    await createFolder(name);
    setCreateDialogOpen(false);
  };

  // If no directory is selected, show mount points
  if (!currentHandle) {
    return (
      <div className="h-full flex flex-col bg-background">
        <MountPointsView />
      </div>
    );
  }

  return (
    <div className="h-full flex flex-col bg-background">
      <Toolbar
        viewMode={viewMode}
        onViewModeChange={setViewMode}
        sortBy={sortBy}
        onSortChange={setSortBy}
        onCreateFolder={handleCreateFolder}
        onNavigateBack={navigateBack}
        onRefresh={refreshCurrent}
        canGoBack={history.length > 0}
        isLoading={isLoading}
        currentPath={currentPath}
      />
      
      <div className="flex-1 overflow-auto">
        {entries.length === 0 ? (
          <div className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center h-full text-muted-foreground">
            <p className="text-lg font-medium">Empty folder</p>
            <p className="text-sm">Create a new folder to get started</p>
          </div>
        ) : viewMode === 'grid' ? (
          <FileGrid entries={entries} onNavigate={navigateTo} panelId="storage-main" />
        ) : (
          <FileList entries={entries} onNavigate={navigateTo} panelId="storage-main" />
        )}
      </div>

      <CreateFolderDialog 
        open={createDialogOpen} 
        onOpenChange={setCreateDialogOpen} 
        panelId="storage-main"
      />
    </div>
  );
}

FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/prakash-app/src/components/GitHub/GitHubPanel.tsx

import { useEffect } from 'react';
import { AccountSelector } from './AccountSelector';
import { GitHubToolbar } from './GitHubToolbar';
import { RepoList } from './RepoList';
import { ContentList } from './ContentList';
import { FileViewer } from './FileViewer';
import { useGitHubStore, useGitHubRepositories, useGitHubContents, useGitHubViewMode, useGitHubSortBy, useGitHubActiveAccount, useGitHubCurrentRepo, useGitHubFileContent, useGitHubError } from '@/stores/githubStore';

function GitHubPanelContent() {
  const repos = useGitHubRepositories();
  const contents = useGitHubContents();
  const viewMode = useGitHubViewMode();
  const sortBy = useGitHubSortBy();
  const activeAccount = useGitHubActiveAccount();
  const currentRepo = useGitHubCurrentRepo();
  const fileContent = useGitHubFileContent();
  const error = useGitHubError();
  
  const {
    setViewMode,
    setSortBy,
    navigateBack,
    refreshCurrent,
    navigateToRoot,
    setActiveAccount,
    loadAccounts,
  } = useGitHubStore();

  // Load accounts on mount
  useEffect(() => {
    loadAccounts();
  }, [loadAccounts]);

  const handleBackToAccounts = () => {
    setActiveAccount(null);
  };

  // Show account selector if no active account
  if (!activeAccount) {
    return <AccountSelector />;
  }

  const currentView = currentRepo ? 'contents' : 'repos';

  return (
    <div className="h-full flex flex-col bg-background">
      <GitHubToolbar
        viewMode={viewMode}
        onViewModeChange={setViewMode}
        sortBy={sortBy}
        onSortChange={setSortBy}
        onNavigateBack={navigateBack}
        onRefresh={refreshCurrent}
        onLogout={handleBackToAccounts}
        currentView={currentView}
      />

      {error && (
        <div className="p-3 bg-destructive/10 text-destructive text-sm text-center">
          {error}
          <button 
            onClick={refreshCurrent}
            className="ml-2 underline hover:no-underline"
          >
            Retry
          </button>
        </div>
      )}

      <div className="flex-1 overflow-auto flex">
        <div className={`flex-1 ${fileContent ? 'hidden md:block md:w-1/2' : 'w-full'}`}>
          {currentView === 'repos' ? (
            repos.length === 0 ? (
              <div className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center h-full text-muted-foreground">
                <p className="text-sm">No repositories found</p>
              </div>
            ) : (
              <RepoList repos={repos} />
            )
          ) : (
            contents.length === 0 ? (
              <div className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center h-full text-muted-foreground">
                <p className="text-sm">Empty folder</p>
              </div>
            ) : (
              <ContentList contents={contents} />
            )
          )}
        </div>

        {/* File Viewer - shows when file is selected */}
        {fileContent && (
          <div className="w-full md:w-1/2 h-full">
            <FileViewer />
          </div>
        )}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

export function GitHubPanel() {
  return <GitHubPanelContent />;
}

FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/prakash-app/src/components/GitHub/AccountSelector.tsx
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
import { useState } from 'react';
import { Github, Plus, X } from 'lucide-react';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { Input } from '@/components/ui/input';
import { Label } from '@/components/ui/label';
import { useGitHubStore, useGitHubAccounts } from '@/stores/githubStore';

export function AccountSelector() {
  const accounts = useGitHubAccounts();
  const addAccount = useGitHubStore((s) => s.addAccount);
  const setActiveAccount = useGitHubStore((s) => s.setActiveAccount);
  const removeAccount = useGitHubStore((s) => s.removeAccount);
  const [showAddForm, setShowAddForm] = useState(false);
  const [username, setUsername] = useState('');
  const [token, setToken] = useState('');
  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(false);
  const [error, setError] = useState('');

  const handleAddAccount = async () => {
    if (!username.trim() || !token.trim()) {
      setError('Username and token are required');
      return;
    }
    setIsLoading(true);
    setError('');
    try {
      await addAccount(username.trim(), token.trim());
      setShowAddForm(false);
      setUsername('');
      setToken('');
    } catch (err) {
      setError((err as Error).message);
    } finally {
      setIsLoading(false);
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="h-full flex flex-col items-center justify-center p-6 bg-background">
      <div className="w-full max-w-md">
        <div className="text-center mb-6">
          <Github className="w-12 h-12 mx-auto text-primary mb-2" />
          <h2 className="text-xl font-semibold">GitHub Accounts</h2>
          <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">Connect your GitHub account to browse repositories</p>
        </div>

        {accounts.length > 0 && (
          <div className="space-y-2 mb-4">
            {accounts.map((account) => (
              <div
                key={account.id}
                className="flex items-center justify-between p-3 rounded-lg border border-border hover:bg-accent cursor-pointer"
                onClick={() => setActiveAccount(account.id)}
              >
                <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                  {account.avatarUrl ? (
                    <img src={account.avatarUrl} alt={account.id} className="w-8 h-8 rounded-full" />
                  ) : (
                    <div className="w-8 h-8 rounded-full bg-primary/10 flex items-center justify-center">
                      <Github className="w-4 h-4" />
                    </div>
                  )}
                  <div>
                    <p className="font-medium">{account.id}</p>
                    <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground capitalize">{account.permissions}</p>
                  </div>
                </div>
                <Button
                  variant="ghost"
                  size="icon"
                  className="h-7 w-7"
                  onClick={(e) => {
                    e.stopPropagation();
                    removeAccount(account.id);
                  }}
                >
                  <X className="w-3 h-3" />
                </Button>
              </div>
            ))}
          </div>
        )}

        {showAddForm ? (
          <div className="border border-border rounded-lg p-4 space-y-3">
            <div>
              <Label>GitHub Username</Label>
              <Input
                value={username}
                onChange={(e) => setUsername(e.target.value)}
                placeholder="username"
              />
            </div>
            <div>
              <Label>Personal Access Token</Label>
              <Input
                type="password"
                value={token}
                onChange={(e) => setToken(e.target.value)}
                placeholder="ghp_..."
              />
              <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-1">
                Needs <code className="text-xs">repo</code> and <code className="text-xs">read:user</code> scopes
              </p>
            </div>
            {error && <p className="text-sm text-destructive">{error}</p>}
            <div className="flex gap-2">
              <Button variant="outline" onClick={() => setShowAddForm(false)}>Cancel</Button>
              <Button onClick={handleAddAccount} disabled={isLoading}>
                {isLoading ? 'Connecting...' : 'Connect'}
              </Button>
            </div>
          </div>
        ) : (
          <Button variant="outline" className="w-full" onClick={() => setShowAddForm(true)}>
            <Plus className="w-4 h-4 mr-2" />
            Add GitHub Account
          </Button>
        )}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/prakash-app/src/components/GitHub/GitHubToolbar.tsx

import { Grid3X3, List, ArrowLeft, RefreshCw, ArrowUpDown, LogOut } from 'lucide-react';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { Toggle } from '@/components/ui/toggle';
import {
  DropdownMenu,
  DropdownMenuContent,
  DropdownMenuItem,
  DropdownMenuTrigger,
} from "@/components/ui/dropdown-menu";
import { GitHubViewMode, GitHubSortBy } from '@/types/github';

interface GitHubToolbarProps {
  viewMode: GitHubViewMode;
  onViewModeChange: (mode: GitHubViewMode) => void;
  sortBy: GitHubSortBy;
  onSortChange: (sort: GitHubSortBy) => void;
  onNavigateBack: () => void;
  onRefresh: () => void;
  onLogout: () => void;
  currentView: 'repos' | 'contents';
}

export function GitHubToolbar({
  viewMode,
  onViewModeChange,
  sortBy,
  onSortChange,
  onNavigateBack,
  onRefresh,
  onLogout,
  currentView,
}: GitHubToolbarProps) {
  return (
    <div className="flex items-center justify-between p-3 border-b border-border bg-card">
      <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
        {currentView === 'contents' && (
          <Button variant="outline" size="icon" onClick={onNavigateBack} className="h-8 w-8">
            <ArrowLeft className="h-4 w-4" />
          </Button>
        )}
        <Button variant="outline" size="icon" onClick={onRefresh} className="h-8 w-8">
          <RefreshCw className="h-4 w-4" />
        </Button>
      </div>

      <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
        <DropdownMenu>
          <DropdownMenuTrigger asChild>
            <Button variant="outline" size="icon" className="h-8 w-8">
              <ArrowUpDown className="h-4 w-4" />
            </Button>
          </DropdownMenuTrigger>
          <DropdownMenuContent align="end">
            <DropdownMenuItem onClick={() => onSortChange('name-asc')}>Name (A-Z)</DropdownMenuItem>
            <DropdownMenuItem onClick={() => onSortChange('name-desc')}>Name (Z-A)</DropdownMenuItem>
            {currentView === 'repos' && (
              <>
                <DropdownMenuItem onClick={() => onSortChange('updated')}>Recently Updated</DropdownMenuItem>
                <DropdownMenuItem onClick={() => onSortChange('stars')}>Stars</DropdownMenuItem>
              </>
            )}
            {currentView === 'contents' && (
              <DropdownMenuItem onClick={() => onSortChange('size')}>Size</DropdownMenuItem>
            )}
          </DropdownMenuContent>
        </DropdownMenu>

        <div className="flex items-center border rounded-md">
          <Toggle
            pressed={viewMode === 'grid'}
            onPressedChange={() => onViewModeChange('grid')}
            className="h-8 w-8 rounded-none rounded-l-md data-[state=on]:bg-primary data-[state=on]:text-primary-foreground"
          >
            <Grid3X3 className="h-4 w-4" />
          </Toggle>
          <Toggle
            pressed={viewMode === 'list'}
            onPressedChange={() => onViewModeChange('list')}
            className="h-8 w-8 rounded-none rounded-r-md data-[state=on]:bg-primary data-[state=on]:text-primary-foreground"
          >
            <List className="h-4 w-4" />
          </Toggle>
        </div>

        <Button variant="ghost" size="icon" onClick={onLogout} className="h-8 w-8" title="Switch Account">
          <LogOut className="h-4 w-4" />
        </Button>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

import { GitHubContent } from '@/types/github';
import { Folder, File, ChevronRight } from 'lucide-react';
import { formatDistanceToNow } from 'date-fns';
import { DFOLMenu } from '../DFOL/DFOLMenu';
import { TreeIconButton } from '../Tree/TreeIconButton';

interface ContentListProps {
  contents: GitHubContent[];
  onFileClick?: (file: GitHubContent) => void;
  onFolderClick?: (folder: GitHubContent) => void;
}

export function ContentList({ contents, onFileClick, onFolderClick }: ContentListProps) {
  const handleClick = (item: GitHubContent) => {
    if (item.type === 'dir') {
      onFolderClick?.(item);
    } else {
      onFileClick?.(item);
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="divide-y divide-border">
      {contents.map((item) => (
        <div
          key={item.path}
          className="flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-2 hover:bg-accent cursor-pointer group"
          onClick={() => handleClick(item)}
        >
          <div className="flex items-center gap-3 flex-1 min-w-0">
            {item.type === 'dir' ? (
              <Folder className="w-5 h-5 text-primary shrink-0" />
            ) : (
              <File className="w-5 h-5 text-muted-foreground shrink-0" />
            )}
            <span className="text-sm font-medium truncate">{item.name}</span>
            {item.type === 'file' && (
              <span className="text-xs text-muted-foreground shrink-0">
                {formatBytes(item.size)}
              </span>
            )}
          </div>
          <div className="flex items-center gap-2 shrink-0">
            <TreeIconButton
              item={item}
              sourceType="github"
              panelId="github-panel"
              className="h-7 w-7 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity"
            />
            <DFOLMenu
              item={item}
              sourceType="github"
              panelId="github-panel"
              onRename={() => {}}
              onDelete={() => {}}
              onTreeView={() => {}}
            />
            <ChevronRight className="w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" />
          </div>
        </div>
      ))}
    </div>
  );
}

function formatBytes(bytes: number): string {
  if (bytes === 0) return '-';
  const units = ['B', 'KB', 'MB', 'GB'];
  let size = bytes;
  let unitIndex = 0;
  while (size >= 1024 && unitIndex < units.length - 1) {
    size /= 1024;
    unitIndex++;
  }
  return `${size.toFixed(1)} ${units[unitIndex]}`;
}

import { useGitHubStore, useGitHubFileContent, useGitHubFileName } from '@/stores/githubStore';
import { X, FileText } from 'lucide-react';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { ScrollArea } from '@/components/ui/scroll-area';

export function FileViewer() {
  const fileContent = useGitHubFileContent();
  const fileName = useGitHubFileName();
  const closeFile = useGitHubStore((s) => s.closeFile);

  if (!fileContent || !fileName) return null;

  const isText = fileName.match(/\.(txt|js|ts|jsx|tsx|json|md|css|html|xml|sh|py|rb|go|java|c|cpp|h|hpp|yml|yaml)$/i);

  return (
    <div className="h-full flex flex-col border-l border-border bg-card">
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between p-3 border-b border-border">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
          <FileText className="w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground" />
          <span className="text-sm font-medium truncate">{fileName}</span>
        </div>
        <Button variant="ghost" size="icon" className="h-7 w-7" onClick={closeFile}>
          <X className="w-4 h-4" />
        </Button>
      </div>

      <ScrollArea className="flex-1 p-4">
        {isText ? (
          <pre className="text-sm font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words">
            {fileContent}
          </pre>
        ) : (
          <div className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center h-full text-muted-foreground">
            <FileText className="w-12 h-12 mb-2 opacity-50" />
            <p className="text-sm">Preview not available for binary files</p>
          </div>
        )}
      </ScrollArea>
    </div>
  );
}

export function AccountSelector() {
  const accounts = useDriveAccounts();
  const addAccount = useDriveStore((s) => s.addAccount);
  const setActiveAccount = useDriveStore((s) => s.setActiveAccount);
  const removeAccount = useDriveStore((s) => s.removeAccount);
  const { login, isLoading } = useGoogleDriveAuth();
  const [showAddForm, setShowAddForm] = useState(false);
  const [error, setError] = useState('');

  const handleAddAccount = async () => {
    setError('');
    try {
      await login();
      setShowAddForm(false);
    } catch (err) {
      setError((err as Error).message);
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="h-full flex flex-col items-center justify-center p-6 bg-background">
      <div className="w-full max-w-md">
        <div className="text-center mb-6">
          <FolderGit className="w-12 h-12 mx-auto text-primary mb-2" />
          <h2 className="text-xl font-semibold">Google Drive Accounts</h2>
          <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">Connect your Google Drive account</p>
        </div>

        {accounts.length > 0 && (
          <div className="space-y-2 mb-4">
            {accounts.map((account) => (
              <div
                key={account.id}
                onClick={() => setActiveAccount(account.id)}
                className="flex items-center justify-between p-3 rounded-lg border border-border hover:bg-accent cursor-pointer"
              >
                <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                  {account.picture ? (
                    <img src={account.picture} alt={account.name} className="w-8 h-8 rounded-full" />
                  ) : (
                    <div className="w-8 h-8 rounded-full bg-primary/10 flex items-center justify-center">
                      <FolderGit className="w-4 h-4" />
                    </div>
                  )}
                  <div>
                    <p className="font-medium">{account.name}</p>
                    <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">{account.id}</p>
                  </div>
                </div>
                <div className="flex items-center gap-1">
                  <TreeIconButton
                    item={{
                      id: account.id,
                      name: account.name,
                      path: '/',
                      type: 'root',
                      size: 0,
                      lastModified: new Date(),
                      properties: {
                        fileSystemType: 'Google Drive',
                        label: 'Cloud Storage',
                        owner: account.name,
                      }
                    }}
                    sourceType="drive"
                    panelId="drive-root"
                    className="h-7 w-7"
                  />
                  <Button
                    variant="ghost"
                    size="icon"
                    className="h-8 w-8 shrink-0"
                    onClick={(e) => {
                      e.stopPropagation();
                      removeAccount(account.id);
                    }}
                  >
                    <X className="h-4 w-4" />
                  </Button>
                </div>
              </div>
            ))}
          </div>
        )}

        {showAddForm ? (
          <div className="border border-border rounded-lg p-4 space-y-3">
            <div>
              <Label>Google Account</Label>
              <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground mb-2">
                Click the button below to sign in with Google.
              </p>
              {error && <p className="text-sm text-destructive">{error}</p>}
              <div className="flex gap-2 mt-3">
                <Button variant="outline" onClick={() => setShowAddForm(false)}>Cancel</Button>
                <Button onClick={handleAddAccount} disabled={isLoading}>
                  {isLoading ? 'Connecting...' : 'Sign in with Google'}
                </Button>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        ) : (
          <Button variant="outline" className="w-full" onClick={() => setShowAddForm(true)}>
            <Plus className="w-4 h-4 mr-2" />
            Add Google Drive Account
          </Button>
        )}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/prakash-app/src/components/GoogleDrive/DrivePanel.tsx
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
import { useEffect } from 'react';
import { AccountSelector } from './AccountSelector';
import { DriveToolbar } from './DriveToolbar';
import { DriveFileGrid } from './DriveFileGrid';
import { DriveFileList } from './DriveFileList';
import { useDriveStore, useDriveFiles, useDriveViewMode, useDriveSortBy, useDriveActiveAccount, useDriveError } from '@/stores/driveStore';
import { DriveFile } from '@/types/drive';
import { GoogleDriveProvider } from './GoogleDriveProvider';

function DrivePanelContent() {
  const files = useDriveFiles();
  const viewMode = useDriveViewMode();
  const sortBy = useDriveSortBy();
  const activeAccount = useDriveActiveAccount();
  const error = useDriveError();
  
  const {
    setViewMode,
    setSortBy,
    navigateToFolder,
    navigateBack,
    refreshCurrent,
    navigateToRoot,
    setActiveAccount,
  } = useDriveStore();

  const currentFolderName = useDriveStore((s) => s.getCurrentFolderName());

  // Refresh when account changes
  useEffect(() => {
    if (activeAccount) {
      navigateToRoot();
    }
  }, [activeAccount?.id]);

  const handleFolderClick = (file: DriveFile) => {
    navigateToFolder(file);
  };

  const handleFileClick = (file: DriveFile) => {
    if (file.webViewLink) {
      window.open(file.webViewLink, '_blank');
    }
  };

  const handleBackToAccounts = () => {
    setActiveAccount(null);
  };

  // Show account selector if no active account
  if (!activeAccount) {
    return <AccountSelector />;
  }

  return (
    <div className="h-full flex flex-col bg-background">
      <DriveToolbar
        viewMode={viewMode}
        onViewModeChange={setViewMode}
        sortBy={sortBy}
        onSortChange={setSortBy}
        onNavigateBack={navigateBack}
        onRefresh={refreshCurrent}
        onLogout={handleBackToAccounts}
        currentFolderName={currentFolderName}
      />

      {error && (
        <div className="p-3 bg-destructive/10 text-destructive text-sm text-center">
          {error}
          <button 
            onClick={refreshCurrent}
            className="ml-2 underline hover:no-underline"
          >
            Retry
          </button>
        </div>
      )}

      <div className="flex-1 overflow-auto">
        {files.length === 0 ? (
          <div className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center h-full text-muted-foreground">
            <p className="text-sm">Empty folder</p>
          </div>
        ) : viewMode === 'grid' ? (
          <DriveFileGrid 
            files={files} 
            onFolderClick={handleFolderClick}
            onFileClick={handleFileClick}
          />
        ) : (
          <DriveFileList 
            files={files} 
            onFolderClick={handleFolderClick}
            onFileClick={handleFileClick}
          />
        )}
      </div>

      {/* Add Account Button - Bottom Center */}
      <div className="p-3 border-t border-border flex justify-center">
        <button
          onClick={handleBackToAccounts}
          className="text-xs text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground transition-colors"
        >
          Switch Account
        </button>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

export function DrivePanel() {
  return (
    <GoogleDriveProvider>
      <DrivePanelContent />
    </GoogleDriveProvider>
  );
}

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
import { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import { GoogleOAuthProvider, useGoogleLogin } from '@react-oauth/google';
import { useDriveStore } from '@/stores/driveStore';
import { driveApi } from '@/lib/googleDriveApi';

const CLIENT_ID = import.meta.env.VITE_GOOGLE_CLIENT_ID || '';

interface GoogleDriveProviderProps {
  children: React.ReactNode;
}

export function GoogleDriveProvider({ children }: GoogleDriveProviderProps) {
  return (
    <GoogleOAuthProvider clientId={CLIENT_ID}>
      {children}
    </GoogleOAuthProvider>
  );
}

// Hook for Google Login
export function useGoogleDriveAuth() {
  const addAccount = useDriveStore((s) => s.addAccount);
  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(false);

  const login = useGoogleLogin({
    onSuccess: async (tokenResponse) => {
      setIsLoading(true);
      try {
        // Fetch user info
        const userInfoResponse = await fetch(
          'https://www.googleapis.com/oauth2/v3/userinfo',
          {
            headers: {
              Authorization: `Bearer ${tokenResponse.access_token}`,
            },
          }
        );
        
        if (!userInfoResponse.ok) {
          throw new Error('Failed to fetch user info');
        }

        const userInfo = await userInfoResponse.json();

        const account = {
          id: userInfo.email,
          name: userInfo.name,
          picture: userInfo.picture,
          accessToken: tokenResponse.access_token,
          expiresAt: Date.now() + (tokenResponse.expires_in || 3600) * 1000,
        };

        addAccount(account);
      } catch (err) {
        console.error('Login error:', err);
      } finally {
        setIsLoading(false);
      }
    },
    onError: (error) => {
      console.error('Login Failed:', error);
    },
    scope: 'https://www.googleapis.com/auth/drive.readonly https://www.googleapis.com/auth/drive.file',
  });

  return { login, isLoading };
}
