import { DriveFile } from '@/types/drive';
import { FolderOpen, File } from 'lucide-react';

interface DriveFileGridProps {
  files: DriveFile[];
  onFolderClick: (file: DriveFile) => void;
  onFileClick: (file: DriveFile) => void;
}

export function DriveFileGrid({ files, onFolderClick, onFileClick }: DriveFileGridProps) {
  const isFolder = (file: DriveFile) => file.mimeType === 'application/vnd.google-apps.folder';

  return (
    <div className="grid grid-cols-2 sm:grid-cols-3 md:grid-cols-4 lg:grid-cols-5 gap-4 p-4">
      {files.map((file) => (
        <div
          key={file.id}
          className="flex flex-col items-center p-4 rounded-lg border border-border bg-card hover:bg-accent cursor-pointer transition-colors"
          onClick={() => (isFolder(file) ? onFolderClick(file) : onFileClick(file))}
        >
          {isFolder(file) ? (
            <FolderOpen className="w-12 h-12 text-primary mb-2" />
          ) : (
            <File className="w-12 h-12 text-muted-foreground mb-2" />
          )}
          <span className="text-sm font-medium text-center truncate w-full" title={file.name}>
            {file.name}
          </span>
          <span className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-1">
            {isFolder(file) ? 'Folder' : formatBytes(parseInt(file.size || '0'))}
          </span>
        </div>
      ))}
    </div>
  );
}

function formatBytes(bytes: number): string {
  if (bytes === 0) return '-';
  const units = ['B', 'KB', 'MB', 'GB'];
  let size = bytes;
  let unitIndex = 0;
  while (size >= 1024 && unitIndex < units.length - 1) {
    size /= 1024;
    unitIndex++;
  }
  return `${size.toFixed(1)} ${units[unitIndex]}`;
}

import { DriveFile } from '@/types/drive';
import { Folder, File, ChevronRight } from 'lucide-react';
import { formatDistanceToNow } from 'date-fns';

interface DriveFileListProps {
  files: DriveFile[];
  onFolderClick: (file: DriveFile) => void;
  onFileClick: (file: DriveFile) => void;
}

export function DriveFileList({ files, onFolderClick, onFileClick }: DriveFileListProps) {
  const isFolder = (file: DriveFile) => file.mimeType === 'application/vnd.google-apps.folder';

  return (
    <div className="divide-y divide-border">
      {files.map((file) => (
        <div
          key={file.id}
          className="flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-2 hover:bg-accent cursor-pointer group"
          onClick={() => (isFolder(file) ? onFolderClick(file) : onFileClick(file))}
        >
          <div className="flex items-center gap-3 flex-1 min-w-0">
            {isFolder(file) ? (
              <Folder className="w-5 h-5 text-primary shrink-0" />
            ) : (
              <File className="w-5 h-5 text-muted-foreground shrink-0" />
            )}
            <span className="text-sm font-medium truncate">{file.name}</span>
            {!isFolder(file) && (
              <span className="text-xs text-muted-foreground shrink-0">
                {formatBytes(parseInt(file.size || '0'))}
              </span>
            )}
          </div>
          <div className="flex items-center gap-4 text-xs text-muted-foreground shrink-0">
            <span>{formatDistanceToNow(new Date(file.modifiedTime), { addSuffix: true })}</span>
            <ChevronRight className="w-4 h-4 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" />
          </div>
        </div>
      ))}
    </div>
  );
}

function formatBytes(bytes: number): string {
  if (bytes === 0) return '-';
  const units = ['B', 'KB', 'MB', 'GB'];
  let size = bytes;
  let unitIndex = 0;
  while (size >= 1024 && unitIndex < units.length - 1) {
    size /= 1024;
    unitIndex++;
  }
  return `${size.toFixed(1)} ${units[unitIndex]}`;
}

FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/prakash-app/src/components/Log/LogActionWrapper.tsx
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
import { useLogStore } from '@/stores/logStore';
import { useCallback } from 'react';

export function useLoggedAction() {
  const logAction = useLogStore((s) => s.logAction);

  const wrapAction = useCallback(<T extends (...args: any[]) => any>(
    actionName: string,
    fn: T,
    category?: Parameters<typeof logAction>[2]
  ): T => {
    return (async (...args: any[]) => {
      const startTime = performance.now();
      
      logAction(`${actionName}_start`, { args }, category);
      
      try {
        const result = await fn(...args);
        const duration = Math.round(performance.now() - startTime);
        
        logAction(`${actionName}_complete`, { 
          args, 
          result: typeof result === 'object' ? 'success' : result,
          duration 
        }, category);
        
        return result;
      } catch (error) {
        const duration = Math.round(performance.now() - startTime);
        
        logAction(`${actionName}_error`, { 
          args, 
          error: (error as Error).message,
          duration 
        }, category || 'system');
        
        throw error;
      }
    }) as T;
  }, [logAction]);

  return { wrapAction, logAction };
}

// Hook for component-level logging
export function useComponentLogger(componentName: string) {
  const logAction = useLogStore((s) => s.logAction);

  const logEvent = useCallback((event: string, details?: Record<string, any>) => {
    logAction(`${componentName}_${event}`, details || {}, 'ui');
  }, [logAction, componentName]);

  const logMount = useCallback(() => {
    logEvent('mount');
  }, [logEvent]);

  const logUnmount = useCallback(() => {
    logEvent('unmount');
  }, [logEvent]);

  const logClick = useCallback((element: string, details?: Record<string, any>) => {
    logEvent(`click_${element}`, details);
  }, [logEvent]);

  return { logEvent, logMount, logUnmount, logClick };
}

import { Bell, Check, AlertCircle, Info, X, Clock } from 'lucide-react';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { Badge } from '@/components/ui/badge';
import { ScrollArea } from '@/components/ui/scroll-area';
import { useLogStore, useLogNotifications, useLogUnreadCount } from '@/stores/logStore';
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';
import { useState, useEffect } from 'react';

export function NotificationBell() {
  const [isOpen, setIsOpen] = useState(false);
  const notifications = useLogNotifications();
  const unreadCount = useLogUnreadCount();
  const markNotificationRead = useLogStore((s) => s.markNotificationRead);
  const markAllRead = useLogStore((s) => s.markAllRead);
  const dismissNotification = useLogStore((s) => s.dismissNotification);

  // Auto-start background checks
  useEffect(() => {
    const { startBackgroundChecks } = useLogStore.getState();
    startBackgroundChecks();
    
    return () => {
      const { stopBackgroundChecks } = useLogStore.getState();
      stopBackgroundChecks();
    };
  }, []);

  const getIcon = (type: string) => {
    switch (type) {
      case 'success': return <Check className="w-4 h-4 text-green-500" />;
      case 'warning': return <AlertCircle className="w-4 h-4 text-yellow-500" />;
      case 'error': return <X className="w-4 h-4 text-destructive" />;
      default: return <Info className="w-4 h-4 text-blue-500" />;
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="relative">
      <Button
        variant="ghost"
        size="icon"
        className="relative"
        onClick={() => setIsOpen(!isOpen)}
      >
        <Bell className="w-5 h-5" />
        {unreadCount > 0 && (
          <Badge 
            variant="destructive" 
            className="absolute -top-1 -right-1 h-5 w-5 flex items-center justify-center p-0 text-xs"
          >
            {unreadCount > 9 ? '9+' : unreadCount}
          </Badge>
        )}
      </Button>

      {isOpen && (
        <>
          <div 
            className="fixed inset-0 z-40" 
            onClick={() => setIsOpen(false)}
          />
          <div className="absolute right-0 top-full mt-2 w-96 bg-card border border-border rounded-lg shadow-xl z-50">
            {/* Header */}
            <div className="flex items-center justify-between p-3 border-b border-border">
              <h3 className="font-semibold">Notifications</h3>
              {unreadCount > 0 && (
                <Button variant="ghost" size="sm" onClick={markAllRead}>
                  Mark all read
                </Button>
              )}
            </div>

            {/* Notifications */}
            <ScrollArea className="h-80">
              {notifications.length === 0 ? (
                <div className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center h-full text-muted-foreground">
                  <Bell className="w-8 h-8 mb-2 opacity-50" />
                  <p className="text-sm">No notifications</p>
                </div>
              ) : (
                <div className="divide-y divide-border">
                  {notifications.map((notif) => (
                    <div
                      key={notif.id}
                      className={cn(
                        "p-3 hover:bg-accent transition-colors",
                        !notif.read && "bg-primary/5"
                      )}
                      onClick={() => markNotificationRead(notif.id)}
                    >
                      <div className="flex items-start gap-3">
                        {getIcon(notif.type)}
                        <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
                          <p className="font-medium text-sm">{notif.title}</p>
                          <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-1">
                            {notif.message}
                          </p>
                          
                          <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mt-2">
                            <span className="text-xs text-muted-foreground flex items-center gap-1">
                              <Clock className="w-3 h-3" />
                              {new Date(notif.timestamp).toLocaleTimeString()}
                            </span>

                              <Button
                                variant="outline"
                                size="sm"
                                className="h-6 text-xs"
                                onClick={(e) => {
                                  e.stopPropagation();
                                  notif.action?.onClick();
                                }}
                              >
                                {notif.action.label}
                              </Button>
                            )}
                          </div>
                        </div>
                        
                        <Button
                          variant="ghost"
                          size="icon"
                          className="h-6 w-6 shrink-0"
                          onClick={(e) => {
                            e.stopPropagation();
                            dismissNotification(notif.id);
                          }}
                        >
                          <X className="w-3 h-3" />
                        </Button>
                      </div>
                    </div>
                  ))}
                </div>
              )}
            </ScrollArea>
          </div>
        </>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

import { usePanelStore } from '@/stores/panelStore';
import { FileGrid } from '../FileManager/FileGrid';
import { FileList } from '../FileManager/FileList';
import { Toolbar } from '../FileManager/Toolbar';
import { PanelState } from '@/types/panel';
import { FileSystemEntry, FileSystemDirectoryEntry } from '@/types/filesystem';

interface StoragePanelProps {
  panel: PanelState;
  entries: FileSystemEntry[];
  isLoading: boolean;
  onRefresh: () => void;
}

export function StoragePanel({ panel, entries, isLoading, onRefresh }: StoragePanelProps) {
  const navigatePanelForward = usePanelStore((s) => s.navigatePanelForward);
  const navigatePanelBack = usePanelStore((s) => s.navigatePanelBack);
  const setPanelViewMode = usePanelStore((s) => s.setPanelViewMode);
  const setPanelSortBy = usePanelStore((s) => s.setPanelSortBy);
  const getPanelEntries = usePanelStore((s) => s.getPanelEntries);
  const refreshPanelDirectory = usePanelStore((s) => s.refreshPanelDirectory);

  const handleNavigateTo = async (entry: FileSystemDirectoryEntry) => {
    if (entry.kind !== 'directory') return;
    navigatePanelForward(panel.id, entry.handle, entry.name);
    await refreshPanelDirectory(panel.id);
  };

  const handleCreateFolder = () => {
    // Implement folder creation dialog
    console.log('Create folder in panel', panel.id);
  };

  const handleNavigateBack = () => {
    navigatePanelBack(panel.id);
    refreshPanelDirectory(panel.id);
  };

  const getSortedEntries = () => {
    const sorted = [...entries];
    switch (panel.sortBy) {
      case 'name-asc':
        return sorted.sort((a, b) => a.name.localeCompare(b.name));
      case 'name-desc':
        return sorted.sort((a, b) => b.name.localeCompare(a.name));
      case 'date':
        return sorted.sort((a, b) => b.lastModified.getTime() - a.lastModified.getTime());
      case 'size':
        return sorted.sort((a, b) => b.size - a.size);
      default:
        return sorted;
    }
  };

  const canGoBack = panel.history.length > 0;

  return (
    <div className="h-full flex flex-col bg-background">
      <Toolbar
        viewMode={panel.viewMode}
        onViewModeChange={(mode) => setPanelViewMode(panel.id, mode)}
        sortBy={panel.sortBy}
        onSortChange={(sort) => setPanelSortBy(panel.id, sort)}
        onCreateFolder={handleCreateFolder}
        onNavigateBack={handleNavigateBack}
        onRefresh={onRefresh}
        canGoBack={canGoBack}
        isLoading={isLoading}
        currentPath={panel.path}
      />

      <div className="flex-1 overflow-auto">
        {entries.length === 0 ? (
          <div className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center h-full text-muted-foreground">
            <p className="text-lg font-medium">Empty folder</p>
            <p className="text-sm">Create a new folder to get started</p>
          </div>
        ) : panel.viewMode === 'grid' ? (
          <FileGrid
            entries={getSortedEntries()}
            onNavigate={handleNavigateTo}
            panelId={panel.id}
          />
        ) : (
          <FileList
            entries={getSortedEntries()}
            onNavigate={handleNavigateTo}
            panelId={panel.id}
          />
        )}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/prakash-app/src/components/Panel/PanelContent.tsx
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
import { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import { PanelState } from '@/types/panel';
import { FileSystemEntry } from '@/types/filesystem';
import { usePanelStore } from '@/stores/panelStore';
import { fileSystemBackend } from '@/lib/fileSystemBackend';
import { StoragePanel } from './StoragePanel';
import { PlaceholderPanel } from './PlaceholderPanel';
import { DrivePanel } from '../GoogleDrive/DrivePanel';
import { GitHubPanel } from '../GitHub/GitHubPanel';
import { TerminalPanel } from '../Terminal/TerminalPanel';

interface PanelContentProps {
  panel: PanelState;
}

export function PanelContent({ panel }: PanelContentProps) {
  const [entries, setEntries] = useState<FileSystemEntry[]>([]);
  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(false);

  // Load entries when handle changes (for storage)
  useEffect(() => {
    if (panel.source === 'storage' && panel.handle) {
      setIsLoading(true);
      fileSystemBackend.readDirectory(panel.handle)
        .then(setEntries)
        .finally(() => setIsLoading(false));
    }
  }, [panel.handle, panel.source, panel.id]);

  const handleRefresh = async () => {
    if (!panel.handle) return;
    setIsLoading(true);
    const newEntries = await fileSystemBackend.readDirectory(panel.handle);
    setEntries(newEntries);
    setIsLoading(false);
  };

  switch (panel.source) {
    case 'storage':
      return (
        <StoragePanel
          panel={panel}
          entries={entries}
          isLoading={isLoading}
          onRefresh={handleRefresh}
        />
      );
    case 'drive':
      return <DrivePanel />;
    case 'github':
      return <GitHubPanel />;
    case 'terminal':
      return <TerminalPanel />;
    default:
      return null;
  }
}

};

import { PanelState } from '@/types/panel';
import { SourceType } from '@/stores/appStore';
import { 
  HardDrive, 
  FolderGit, 
  Github, 
  Terminal,
  CheckCircle
} from 'lucide-react';

const sourceIcons: Record<SourceType, React.ElementType> = {
  storage: HardDrive,
  drive: FolderGit,
  github: Github,
  terminal: Terminal,
};

const sourceLabels: Record<SourceType, string> = {
  storage: 'Storage',
  drive: 'Google Drive',
  github: 'GitHub',
  terminal: 'Terminal',
};

interface PlaceholderPanelProps {
  panel: PanelState;
  source: SourceType;
}

export function PlaceholderPanel({ panel, source }: PlaceholderPanelProps) {
  const Icon = sourceIcons[source];
  const label = sourceLabels[source];

  // Terminal is now fully implemented, shouldn't show placeholder
  if (source === 'terminal') {
    return (
      <div className="h-full flex flex-col items-center justify-center p-6 text-center">
        <CheckCircle className="w-12 h-12 text-green-500 mb-4" />
        <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold text-foreground">Terminal Ready</h3>
        <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">
          Click the Terminal button in the panel header to initialize WebContainer.
        </p>
      </div>
    );
  }

  return (
    <div className="h-full flex flex-col items-center justify-center p-6 text-center">
      <div className="p-4 rounded-xl bg-primary/10 text-primary mb-4">
        <Icon className="w-12 h-12" />
      </div>
      <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold text-foreground mb-2">{label}</h3>
      <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground max-w-xs">
        This {label} panel is independent from other panels.
        <br />
        Source: <span className="font-medium capitalize">{panel.source}</span>
      </p>
      <div className="mt-4 p-3 rounded-lg bg-muted text-xs text-muted-foreground">
        Panel ID: {panel.id}
        <br />
        Path: {panel.path}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

import { useRef, useCallback } from 'react';
import { useDrop } from 'react-dnd';
import { PanelState } from '@/types/panel';
import { usePanelStore } from '@/stores/panelStore';
import { useResizable } from '@/hooks/useResizable';
import { PanelHeader } from './PanelHeader';
import { PanelContent } from './PanelContent';
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';
import { MIN_PANEL_WIDTH } from '@/types/panel';
import { useDragDropStore, useIsDragging, usePendingOperation, useTargetPanel } from '@/stores/dragDropStore';

interface ResizablePanelProps {
  panel: PanelState;
  isActive: boolean;
  isLast: boolean;
  onActivate: () => void;
  onClose: () => void;
}

export function ResizablePanel({ 
  panel, 
  isActive, 
  isLast,
  onActivate, 
  onClose 
}: ResizablePanelProps) {
  const setPanelWidth = usePanelStore((s) => s.setPanelWidth);
  const isDraggingGlobal = useIsDragging();
  const pendingOperation = usePendingOperation();
  const targetPanel = useTargetPanel();
  const dragDropStore = useDragDropStore();
  
  const { width, isResizing, startResize } = useResizable({
    initialWidth: panel.width,
    minWidth: MIN_PANEL_WIDTH,
    onResize: (newWidth) => setPanelWidth(panel.id, newWidth),
  });

  // Drop target for drag and drop
  const [{ isOver, canDrop }, drop] = useDrop(() => ({
    accept: ['storage', 'drive', 'github', 'terminal'],
    drop: (item: any, monitor) => {
      if (!monitor.didDrop()) {
        dragDropStore.setTargetPanel(panel.id);
        // Don't complete here - wait for user to select copy/move from floating handle
      }
    },
    collect: (monitor) => ({
      isOver: !!monitor.isOver(),
      canDrop: !!monitor.canDrop(),
    }),
    canDrop: (item: any) => {
      return item.panelId !== panel.id;
    },
  }), [panel.id, dragDropStore]);

  // Handle drop completion when operation is confirmed
  const handleDropComplete = useCallback(() => {
    if (targetPanel === panel.id && pendingOperation) {
      // Execute the copy/move operation
      const selectedItems = dragDropStore.selectedItems;
      
      // TODO: Implement actual copy/move logic based on source and target types
      console.log(`${pendingOperation} ${selectedItems.length} items to panel ${panel.id}`);
      
      // Reset drag state
      dragDropStore.exitDragMode();
    }
  }, [targetPanel, pendingOperation, panel.id, dragDropStore]);

  // Watch for operation confirmation
  useRef(() => {
    if (!dragDropStore.showConfirmDialog && pendingOperation && targetPanel === panel.id) {
      handleDropComplete();
    }
  });

  return (
    <div
      ref={drop}
      className={cn(
        'flex flex-col h-full relative border-r border-border last:border-r-0',
        isActive && 'ring-1 ring-primary/20',
        isResizing && 'select-none',
        isOver && canDrop && 'bg-accent/20 ring-2 ring-accent ring-inset',
        isOver && !canDrop && 'bg-destructive/10'
      )}
      style={{ 
        width: panel.isMinimized ? 60 : width,
        minWidth: panel.isMinimized ? 60 : MIN_PANEL_WIDTH,
        flexShrink: 0,
      }}
    >
      <PanelHeader
        panel={panel}
        isActive={isActive}
        onActivate={onActivate}
        onClose={onClose}
      />
      
      {!panel.isMinimized && (
        <div className="flex-1 overflow-hidden">
          <PanelContent panel={panel} />
        </div>
      )}

      {/* Drop indicator */}
      {isOver && canDrop && (
        <div className="absolute inset-0 flex items-center justify-center pointer-events-none bg-accent/10 z-50">
          <div className="bg-card border border-border shadow-lg rounded-lg px-4 py-2">
            <p className="text-sm font-medium">Drop here</p>
            <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">Select copy or move from handle</p>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* Resize handle */}
      {!isLast && !panel.isMinimized && !isDraggingGlobal && (
        <div
          className={cn(
            'absolute right-0 top-0 bottom-0 w-1 cursor-col-resize z-10',
            'hover:bg-primary/50 transition-colors',
            isResizing && 'bg-primary'
          )}
          onMouseDown={startResize}
        />
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

import { Folder, File } from 'lucide-react';
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';

interface FileGridProps {
  files?: Array<{ id: string; name: string; type: 'file' | 'folder'; size?: number }>;
  onFileClick?: (file: any) => void;
}

export function FileGrid({ files = [], onFileClick }: FileGridProps) {
  if (files.length === 0) {
    return <div className="flex items-center justify-center h-64 text-muted-foreground">No files found</div>;
  }
  return (
    <div className="grid grid-cols-2 sm:grid-cols-3 md:grid-cols-4 gap-4 p-4">
      {files.map((file) => (
        <button key={file.id} onClick={() => onFileClick?.(file)} className={cn("flex flex-col items-center p-4 rounded-lg hover:bg-accent transition-colors")}>
          {file.type === 'folder' ? <Folder className="w-12 h-12 text-blue-500 mb-2" /> : <File className="w-12 h-12 text-gray-500 mb-2" />}
          <span className="text-sm text-center truncate w-full">{file.name}</span>
        </button>
      ))}
    </div>
  );
}

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/prakash-app/src/components/PromptManager/PromptFileManager.tsx
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
import { useState } from 'react';
import { usePromptStore, usePromptFolderStructure, usePromptSessionFiles } from '@/stores/promptStore';
import { Folder, File, Plus, Trash2, Edit2, Archive, ChevronRight, ChevronDown } from 'lucide-react';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';
import { PromptFile, PromptFolder } from '@/types/prompt';

export function PromptFileManager() {
  const folderStructure = usePromptFolderStructure();
  const files = usePromptSessionFiles();
  const createFolder = usePromptStore((s) => s.createFolder);
  const renameFolder = usePromptStore((s) => s.renameFolder);
  const deleteFolder = usePromptStore((s) => s.deleteFolder);
  const addFile = usePromptStore((s) => s.addFile);
  const renameFile = usePromptStore((s) => s.renameFile);
  const deleteFile = usePromptStore((s) => s.deleteFile);
  const compressFile = usePromptStore((s) => s.compressFile);

  const [expandedFolders, setExpandedFolders] = useState<Set<string>>(new Set(['root']));
  const [selectedItem, setSelectedItem] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [renamingId, setRenamingId] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [newName, setNewName] = useState('');

  const toggleFolder = (folderId: string) => {
    const newExpanded = new Set(expandedFolders);
    if (newExpanded.has(folderId)) newExpanded.delete(folderId);
    else newExpanded.add(folderId);
    setExpandedFolders(newExpanded);
  };

  const handleCreateFolder = () => {
    const name = prompt('Folder name:');
    if (name) createFolder(name, '/');
  };

  const handleUpload = () => {
    const input = document.createElement('input');
    input.type = 'file';
    input.multiple = true;
    input.onchange = (e) => {
      const files = (e.target as HTMLInputElement).files;
      if (files) {
        Array.from(files).forEach(file => {
          addFile({
            name: file.name,
            size: file.size,
            type: file.type,
            source: 'upload',
            folderPath: '/',
            isCompressed: false,
            content: file,
          });
        });
      }
    };
    input.click();
  };

  const startRename = (item: PromptFile | PromptFolder) => {
    setRenamingId(item.id);
    setNewName(item.name);
  };

  const confirmRename = () => {
    if (renamingId && newName) {
      const isFolder = 'children' in (files.find(f => f.id === renamingId) || {});
      if (isFolder) renameFolder(renamingId, newName);
      else renameFile(renamingId, newName);
    }
    setRenamingId(null);
    setNewName('');
  };

  const renderItem = (item: PromptFile | PromptFolder, depth = 0) => {
    const isFolder = 'children' in item;
    const isExpanded = expandedFolders.has(item.id);
    const isSelected = selectedItem === item.id;
    const isRenaming = renamingId === item.id;

    return (
      <div key={item.id}>
        <div
          className={cn(
            "flex items-center gap-2 px-3 py-2 hover:bg-accent cursor-pointer group",
            isSelected && "bg-accent",
            depth > 0 && "border-l border-border ml-3"
          )}
          style={{ paddingLeft: `${12 + depth * 16}px` }}
          onClick={() => setSelectedItem(item.id)}
        >
          {isFolder && (
            <button onClick={(e) => { e.stopPropagation(); toggleFolder(item.id); }} className="p-0.5 hover:bg-accent rounded">
              {isExpanded ? <ChevronDown className="w-4 h-4" /> : <ChevronRight className="w-4 h-4" />}
            </button>
          )}
          {!isFolder && <span className="w-5" />}
          {isFolder ? <Folder className="w-4 h-4 text-primary shrink-0" /> : <File className="w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground shrink-0" />}
          {isRenaming ? (
            <input type="text" value={newName} onChange={e => setNewName(e.target.value)} onBlur={confirmRename} onKeyDown={e => e.key === 'Enter' && confirmRename()} className="flex-1 px-2 py-0.5 text-sm border rounded bg-background" autoFocus />
          ) : (
            <span className="flex-1 text-sm truncate">{item.name}</span>
          )}
          {!isFolder && (item as PromptFile).isCompressed && <Archive className="w-3 h-3 text-muted-foreground" />}
          <div className="flex items-center gap-1 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100">
            <Button variant="ghost" size="icon" className="h-6 w-6" onClick={(e) => { e.stopPropagation(); startRename(item); }}><Edit2 className="w-3 h-3" /></Button>
            <Button variant="ghost" size="icon" className="h-6 w-6" onClick={(e) => { e.stopPropagation(); if (isFolder) deleteFolder(item.id); else deleteFile(item.id); }}><Trash2 className="w-3 h-3 text-destructive" /></Button>
          </div>
        </div>
        {isFolder && isExpanded && (item as PromptFolder).children.map(child => renderItem(child, depth + 1))}
      </div>
    );
  };

  return (
    <div className="h-full flex flex-col">
      <div className="p-2 border-b border-border flex gap-2">
        <Button variant="outline" size="sm" onClick={handleCreateFolder}><Plus className="w-3 h-3 mr-1" />Folder</Button>
        <Button variant="outline" size="sm" onClick={handleUpload}><Plus className="w-3 h-3 mr-1" />Upload</Button>
      </div>
      <div className="flex-1 overflow-auto">{renderItem(folderStructure)}</div>
      <div className="p-2 border-t border-border text-xs text-muted-foreground">{files.length} files • {formatBytes(files.reduce((sum, f) => sum + f.size, 0))}</div>
    </div>
  );
}

function formatBytes(bytes: number): string {
  if (bytes === 0) return '0 B';
  const units = ['B', 'KB', 'MB', 'GB'];
  let size = bytes;
  let unitIndex = 0;
  while (size >= 1024 && unitIndex < units.length - 1) { size /= 1024; unitIndex++; }
  return `${size.toFixed(1)} ${units[unitIndex]}`;
}

export function PromptManagerPage() {

// src/components/PromptManager/PromptSessionList.tsx
import { usePromptStore, usePromptSessions, usePromptCurrentSession } from '@/stores/promptStore';
import { Clock, Copy, Trash2, Edit2, ExternalLink, FolderOpen } from 'lucide-react';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';
import { formatDistanceToNow } from 'date-fns';

export function PromptSessionList() {
  const sessions = usePromptSessions();
  const currentSession = usePromptCurrentSession();
  const loadSession = usePromptStore((s) => s.loadSession);
  const deleteSession = usePromptStore((s) => s.deleteSession);
  const duplicateSession = usePromptStore((s) => s.duplicateSession);
  const renameSession = usePromptStore((s) => s.renameSession);

  const handleRename = (id: string, currentName: string) => {
    const newName = prompt('New session name:', currentName);
    if (newName && newName.trim()) {
      renameSession(id, newName.trim());
    }
  };

  const handleOpenInDrive = (session: any) => {
    if (session.uploadResult?.shareLink) {
      window.open(session.uploadResult.shareLink, '_blank');
    } else {
      alert('Session not uploaded yet');
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="h-full flex flex-col">
      <div className="p-3 border-b border-border">
        <h3 className="font-medium text-sm">All Sessions</h3>
        <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">
          {sessions.length} session{sessions.length !== 1 ? 's' : ''} saved
        </p>
      </div>

      <div className="flex-1 overflow-auto p-2 space-y-1">
        {sessions.length === 0 ? (
          <p className="text-center text-muted-foreground text-sm py-8">
            No sessions yet. Create one from the File Manager tab.
          </p>
        ) : (
          sessions.map((session) => {
            const isActive = currentSession?.id === session.id;
            return (
              <div
                key={session.id}
                className={cn(
                  "group flex items-center justify-between p-2 rounded-lg cursor-pointer transition-colors",
                  isActive ? "bg-primary/10 border border-primary/20" : "hover:bg-accent"
                )}
                onClick={() => loadSession(session.id)}
              >
                <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
                  <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                    <FolderOpen className="w-4 h-4 text-primary shrink-0" />
                    <span className="font-medium text-sm truncate">{session.name}</span>
                    {session.isCompleted && (
                      <span className="text-[10px] bg-green-100 text-green-700 px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded-full">
                        Done
                      </span>
                    )}
                  </div>
                  <div className="flex items-center gap-3 mt-0.5 text-xs text-muted-foreground">
                    <span className="flex items-center gap-1">
                      <Clock className="w-3 h-3" />
                      {formatDistanceToNow(session.updatedAt, { addSuffix: true })}
                    </span>
                    <span>{session.files.length} files</span>
                    <span>{session.notes.length} notes</span>
                  </div>
                </div>

                {/* Actions */}
                <div className="flex items-center gap-1 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity">
                  <Button
                    variant="ghost"
                    size="icon"
                    className="h-7 w-7"
                    onClick={(e) => {
                      e.stopPropagation();
                      const newSession = duplicateSession(session.id);
                      loadSession(newSession.id);
                    }}
                    title="Duplicate"
                  >
                    <Copy className="w-3.5 h-3.5" />
                  </Button>
                  
                  <Button
                    variant="ghost"
                    size="icon"
                    className="h-7 w-7"
                    onClick={(e) => {
                      e.stopPropagation();
                      handleRename(session.id, session.name);
                    }}
                    title="Rename"
                  >
                    <Edit2 className="w-3.5 h-3.5" />
                  </Button>
                  
                  {session.uploadResult && (
                    <Button
                      variant="ghost"
                      size="icon"
                      className="h-7 w-7"
                      onClick={(e) => {
                        e.stopPropagation();
                        handleOpenInDrive(session);
                      }}
                      title="Open in Drive/GitHub"
                    >
                      <ExternalLink className="w-3.5 h-3.5" />
                    </Button>
                  )}
                  
                  <Button
                    variant="ghost"
                    size="icon"
                    className="h-7 w-7 text-destructive hover:text-destructive"
                    onClick={(e) => {
                      e.stopPropagation();
                      if (confirm(`Delete session "${session.name}"?`)) {
                        deleteSession(session.id);
                      }
                    }}
                    title="Delete"
                  >
                    <Trash2 className="w-3.5 h-3.5" />
                  </Button>
                </div>
              </div>
            );
          })
        )}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

export function PromptWritingArea() {

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/prakash-app/src/components/Rename/WebWorkerConverter.ts
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
// Web Worker for running conversions off main thread

const workerCode = `
self.onmessage = async (e) => {
  const { type, fileData, fromExt, toExt } = e.data;
  
  try {
    switch (type) {
      case 'ffmpeg':
        // FFmpeg operations would go here
        // Note: FFmpeg WASM can't easily run in worker due to SharedArrayBuffer
        self.postMessage({ type: 'progress', progress: 50 });
        break;
        
      case 'image':
        // Canvas-based image conversion
        const result = await convertImage(fileData, fromExt, toExt);
        self.postMessage({ type: 'complete', result });
        break;
        
      default:
        throw new Error('Unknown conversion type');
    }
  } catch (error) {
    self.postMessage({ type: 'error', error: error.message });
  }
};

async function convertImage(fileData: ArrayBuffer, fromExt: string, toExt: string): Promise<ArrayBuffer> {
  // Create blob from array buffer
  const blob = new Blob([fileData]);
  const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
  
  try {
    const img = await loadImage(url);
    const canvas = new OffscreenCanvas(img.width, img.height);
    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
    
    if (!ctx) throw new Error('Canvas context not available');
    
    ctx.drawImage(img, 0, 0);
    URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
    
    const mimeType = toExt === '.jpg' || toExt === '.jpeg' 
      ? 'image/jpeg' 
      : toExt === '.webp' 
        ? 'image/webp' 
        : 'image/png';
    
    const outputBlob = await canvas.convertToBlob({ type: mimeType, quality: 0.9 });
    return await outputBlob.arrayBuffer();
  } catch (error) {
    URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
    throw error;
  }
}

function loadImage(url: string): Promise<ImageBitmap> {
  return fetch(url)
    .then(r => r.blob())
    .then(b => createImageBitmap(b));
}
`;

// Create worker from code string
export function createConverterWorker(): Worker {
  const blob = new Blob([workerCode], { type: 'application/javascript' });
  const workerUrl = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
  return new Worker(workerUrl);
}

FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/prakash-app/src/components/Rename/InlineRenameInput.tsx
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
import { useState, useEffect, useRef } from 'react';
import { Input } from '@/components/ui/input';
import { useRenameStore } from '@/stores/renameStore';

interface InlineRenameInputProps {
  item: {
    id: string;
    name: string;
    path: string;
    sourceType: 'storage' | 'drive' | 'github' | 'terminal';
    panelId: string;
    handle?: any;
  };
  onComplete?: () => void;
}

export function InlineRenameInput({ item, onComplete }: InlineRenameInputProps) {
  const [value, setValue] = useState(item.name);
  const inputRef = useRef<HTMLInputElement>(null);
  const startRename = useRenameStore((s) => s.startRename);
  const updateNewName = useRenameStore((s) => s.updateNewName);
  const confirmRename = useRenameStore((s) => s.confirmRename);
  const cancelRename = useRenameStore((s) => s.cancelRename);

  useEffect(() => {
    startRename(item);
    inputRef.current?.focus();
    inputRef.current?.select();
  }, [item, startRename]);

  const handleKeyDown = (e: React.KeyboardEvent) => {
    if (e.key === 'Enter') {
      updateNewName(value);
      confirmRename();
      onComplete?.();
    } else if (e.key === 'Escape') {
      cancelRename();
      onComplete?.();
    }
  };

  const handleBlur = () => {
    if (value !== item.name) {
      updateNewName(value);
      confirmRename();
    } else {
      cancelRename();
    }
    onComplete?.();
  };

  return (
    <Input
      ref={inputRef}
      value={value}
      onChange={(e) => setValue(e.target.value)}
      onKeyDown={handleKeyDown}
      onBlur={handleBlur}
      className="h-8 text-sm"
    />
  );
}

import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';

import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';
import { useState, useMemo } from 'react';

const sourceIcons = {
  storage: HardDrive,
  drive: FolderGit,
  github: Github,
  terminal: Terminal,
};

export function FilterPanel() {
  const isOpen = useIsFilterPanelOpen();
  const filters = useSearchFilters();
  const extensions = useAvailableExtensions();
  const accounts = useAvailableAccounts();
  const setFilters = useSearchStore((s) => s.setFilters);
  const resetFilters = useSearchStore((s) => s.resetFilters);
  const toggleFilterPanel = useSearchStore((s) => s.toggleFilterPanel);

  const [extensionSearch, setExtensionSearch] = useState('');

  const filteredExtensions = useMemo(() => {
    if (!extensionSearch) return extensions.slice(0, 50);
    return extensions
      .filter(e => e.extension.toLowerCase().includes(extensionSearch.toLowerCase()))
      .sort((a, b) => b.count - a.count);
  }, [extensions, extensionSearch]);

  if (!isOpen) return null;

  const toggleSource = (source: string) => {
    const newSources = filters.sources.includes(source as any)
      ? filters.sources.filter(s => s !== source)
      : [...filters.sources, source as any];
    setFilters({ sources: newSources });
  };

  const toggleAccount = (accountId: string) => {
    const newAccounts = filters.accounts.includes(accountId)
      ? filters.accounts.filter(a => a !== accountId)
      : [...filters.accounts, accountId];
    setFilters({ accounts: newAccounts });
  };

  const toggleExtension = (ext: string) => {
    const newExtensions = filters.extensions.includes(ext)
      ? filters.extensions.filter(e => e !== ext)
      : [...filters.extensions, ext];
    setFilters({ extensions: newExtensions });
  };

  const activeFilterCount = 
    (filters.sources.length < 4 ? 1 : 0) +
    (filters.accounts.length > 0 ? 1 : 0) +
    (filters.extensions.length > 0 ? 1 : 0) +
    (filters.type !== 'all' ? 1 : 0) +
    (filters.includeHidden ? 1 : 0);

  return (
    <div className="fixed inset-0 z-50 flex items-start justify-center pt-20 bg-black/30 p-4">
      <div className="w-full max-w-4xl max-h-[80vh] bg-background rounded-lg shadow-2xl flex flex-col overflow-hidden">
        {/* Header */}
        <div className="flex items-center justify-between p-4 border-b border-border">
          <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
            <h2 className="text-lg font-semibold">Search Filters</h2>
            {activeFilterCount > 0 && (
              <Badge variant="secondary">{activeFilterCount} active</Badge>
            )}
          </div>
          <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
            <Button variant="ghost" size="sm" onClick={resetFilters}>
              Reset All
            </Button>
            <Button variant="ghost" size="icon" onClick={toggleFilterPanel}>
              <X className="w-4 h-4" />
            </Button>
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* Content */}
        <div className="flex-1 overflow-hidden flex">
          {/* Left: Sources & Accounts */}
          <div className="w-1/3 border-r border-border p-4 space-y-6">
            {/* Sources */}
            <div>
              <h3 className="text-sm font-medium mb-3 flex items-center gap-2">
                <HardDriveIcon className="w-4 h-4" />
                Sources
              </h3>
              <div className="space-y-2">
                {(Object.keys(sourceIcons) as Array<keyof typeof sourceIcons>).map(source => {
                  const Icon = sourceIcons[source];
                  const isActive = filters.sources.includes(source);
                  
                  return (
                    <button
                      key={source}
                      onClick={() => toggleSource(source)}
                      className={cn(
                        "w-full flex items-center gap-2 px-3 py-2 rounded-lg text-sm transition-colors",
                        isActive ? "bg-primary/10 text-primary" : "hover:bg-accent text-muted-foreground"
                      )}
                    >
                      <Icon className="w-4 h-4" />
                      <span className="capitalize">{source}</span>
                      {isActive && <Badge variant="outline" className="ml-auto text-xs">On</Badge>}
                    </button>
                  );
                })}
              </div>
            </div>

            <Separator />

            {/* Accounts */}
            <div>
              <h3 className="text-sm font-medium mb-3">Accounts</h3>
              <ScrollArea className="h-48">

                  {accounts.map(account => {

                        className={cn(
                          "w-full flex items-center gap-2 px-3 py-2 rounded-lg text-sm transition-colors",

                      >
                        <div className="w-6 h-6 rounded-full bg-primary/10 flex items-center justify-center text-xs">
                          {account.name.charAt(0).toUpperCase()}
                        </div>
                        <span className="truncate">{account.name}</span>
                        {isActive && <Check className="w-3 h-3 ml-auto" />}
                      </button>
                    );
                  })}
                  
                  {accounts.length === 0 && (
                    <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground text-center py-4">

                    </p>
                  )}
                </div>
              </ScrollArea>
            </div>

                ))}

                    onCheckedChange={(checked) => 
                      setFilters({ includeHidden: checked as boolean })
                    }

  );

import { Search, Filter, Globe, X, Clock, Loader2 } from 'lucide-react';
import { Input } from '@/components/ui/input';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { Badge } from '@/components/ui/badge';
import { useSearchStore, useSearchQuery, useIsSearching, useIsGlobalMode, useRecentSearches, useIndexedCount } from '@/stores/searchStore';
import { useEffect, useRef, useState } from 'react';
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';

export function GlobalSearchBar() {
  const query = useSearchQuery();
  const isSearching = useIsSearching();
  const isGlobalMode = useIsGlobalMode();
  const recentSearches = useRecentSearches();
  const indexedCount = useIndexedCount();
  const setQuery = useSearchStore((s) => s.setQuery);
  const toggleFilterPanel = useSearchStore((s) => s.toggleFilterPanel);
  const toggleGlobalMode = useSearchStore((s) => s.toggleGlobalMode);
  const addRecentSearch = useSearchStore((s) => s.addRecentSearch);
  const initializeSearch = useSearchStore((s) => s.initializeSearch);
  
  const [showRecent, setShowRecent] = useState(false);
  const inputRef = useRef<HTMLInputElement>(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    initializeSearch();
  }, [initializeSearch]);

  const handleSubmit = (e: React.FormEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    addRecentSearch(query);
    setShowRecent(false);
  };

  const handleRecentClick = (search: string) => {
    setQuery(search);
    setShowRecent(false);
    inputRef.current?.focus();
  };

  return (
    <div className="relative flex-1 max-w-2xl">
      <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} className="relative flex items-center gap-2">
        <div className="relative flex-1">
          <Search className="absolute left-3 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground" />
          
          <Input
            ref={inputRef}
            type="text"
            placeholder={`Search ${indexedCount.toLocaleString()} indexed files...`}
            value={query}
            onChange={(e) => setQuery(e.target.value)}
            onFocus={() => setShowRecent(true)}
            onBlur={() => setTimeout(() => setShowRecent(false), 200)}
            className="pl-10 pr-20 h-10"
          />
          
          {/* Clear button */}
          {query && (
            <button
              type="button"
              onClick={() => setQuery('')}
              className="absolute right-24 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 p-1 hover:bg-accent rounded"
            >
              <X className="w-3 h-3" />
            </button>
          )}

          {/* Global mode toggle */}
          <Button
            type="button"
            variant="ghost"
            size="sm"
            onClick={toggleGlobalMode}
            className={cn(
              "absolute right-12 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 h-6 px-2",
              isGlobalMode && "text-primary bg-primary/10"
            )}
          >
            <Globe className="w-4 h-4" />
          </Button>

          {/* Filter button */}
          <Button
            type="button"
            variant="ghost"
            size="sm"
            onClick={toggleFilterPanel}
            className="absolute right-2 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 h-6 px-2"
          >
            <Filter className="w-4 h-4" />
          </Button>

          {/* Searching indicator */}
          {isSearching && (
            <Loader2 className="absolute right-32 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 w-4 h-4 animate-spin text-primary" />
          )}
        </div>
      </form>

      {/* Recent searches dropdown */}
      {showRecent && recentSearches.length > 0 && !query && (
        <div className="absolute top-full left-0 right-0 mt-1 bg-card border border-border rounded-lg shadow-lg z-50 py-2">
          <p className="px-3 py-1 text-xs font-medium text-muted-foreground flex items-center gap-2">
            <Clock className="w-3 h-3" />
            Recent Searches

            <button

            >
              <Search className="w-3 h-3 text-muted-foreground" />
              {search}
            </button>
          ))}
        </div>

      {/* Global mode badge */}
      {isGlobalMode && (
        <Badge variant="secondary" className="absolute -bottom-6 left-0 text-xs">
          <Globe className="w-3 h-3 mr-1" />
          Global Search Active
        </Badge>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

import { useSearchStore, useSearchResults, useSearchQuery } from '@/stores/searchStore';
import { HardDrive, Github, FolderGit, Terminal, File, Folder, X, ExternalLink, Pencil, Move, MoreVertical } from 'lucide-react';
import { ScrollArea } from '@/components/ui/scroll-area';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { Badge } from '@/components/ui/badge';
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';
import { useState } from 'react';
import { DFOLMenu } from '../DFOL/DFOLMenu';
import { TreeIconButton } from '../Tree/TreeIconButton';

const sourceIcons = {
  storage: HardDrive,
  drive: FolderGit,
  github: Github,
  terminal: Terminal,
};

export function SearchResultsOverlay() {
  const results = useSearchResults();
  const query = useSearchQuery();
  const setQuery = useSearchStore((s) => s.setQuery);
  
  const [selectedResult, setSelectedResult] = useState<string | null>(null);

  if (!query.trim() || results.length === 0) return null;

  const handleOpen = (result: any) => {
    // Open in appropriate panel
    console.log('Opening:', result.item.path);
  };

  const handleRename = (result: any) => {
    // Trigger rename
    console.log('Renaming:', result.item.name);
  };

  return (
    <div className="fixed top-16 left-1/2 -translate-x-1/2 w-full max-w-3xl max-h-[70vh] bg-card border border-border rounded-lg shadow-2xl z-40 flex flex-col">
      {/* Header */}
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between p-3 border-b border-border">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
          <Badge variant="secondary">{results.length} results</Badge>
          <span className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">
            for "{query}"
          </span>
        </div>
        <Button variant="ghost" size="icon" onClick={() => setQuery('')}>
          <X className="w-4 h-4" />
        </Button>
      </div>

      {/* Results */}
      <ScrollArea className="flex-1">
        <div className="divide-y divide-border">
          {results.map((result, index) => {
            const Icon = sourceIcons[result.item.sourceType];
            const isSelected = selectedResult === result.item.id;
            
            return (
              <div
                key={result.item.id}
                className={cn(
                  "group p-3 hover:bg-accent transition-colors cursor-pointer",
                  isSelected && "bg-accent"
                )}
                onClick={() => setSelectedResult(result.item.id)}
                onDoubleClick={() => handleOpen(result)}
              >
                <div className="flex items-start gap-3">
                  {/* Icon */}
                  <div className={cn(
                    "w-10 h-10 rounded-lg flex items-center justify-center shrink-0",
                    result.item.type === 'directory' ? "bg-primary/10" : "bg-muted"
                  )}>
                    {result.item.type === 'directory' ? (
                      <Folder className="w-5 h-5 text-primary" />
                    ) : (
                      <File className="w-5 h-5 text-muted-foreground" />
                    )}
                  </div>

                  {/* Content */}
                  <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
                    <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                      <Icon className="w-3 h-3 text-muted-foreground" />
                      <span className="text-xs text-muted-foreground uppercase">
                        {result.item.sourceType}
                      </span>
                      <span className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">•</span>
                      <span className="text-xs text-muted-foreground truncate">
                        {result.item.accountId}
                      </span>
                    </div>
                    
                    <p className="font-medium truncate" title={result.item.path}>
                      <HighlightMatches text={result.item.name} matches={result.matches} />
                    </p>
                    
                    <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground truncate">
                      {result.item.path}
                    </p>

                    <div className="flex items-center gap-3 mt-1 text-xs text-muted-foreground">
                      <span>{formatBytes(result.item.size)}</span>
                      <span>•</span>
                      <span>{new Date(result.item.lastModified).toLocaleDateString()}</span>
                      {result.item.extension && (
                        <>
                          <span>•</span>
                          <Badge variant="outline" className="text-[10px] px-1">
                            {result.item.extension}
                          </Badge>
                        </>
                      )}
                    </div>
                  </div>

                  {/* Actions */}
                  <div className="flex items-center gap-1 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity">
                    <Button
                      variant="ghost"
                      size="icon"
                      className="h-7 w-7"
                      onClick={(e) => {
                        e.stopPropagation();
                        handleOpen(result);
                      }}
                    >
                      <ExternalLink className="w-4 h-4" />
                    </Button>
                    
                    <TreeIconButton
                      item={result.item}
                      sourceType={result.item.sourceType}
                      panelId="search"
                      className="h-7 w-7"
                    />
                    
                    <DFOLMenu
                      item={result.item}
                      sourceType={result.item.sourceType}
                      panelId="search"
                      onRename={() => handleRename(result)}
                      onDelete={() => {}}
                      onTreeView={() => {}}
                    />
                  </div>
                </div>

                {/* Match highlights */}
                {result.matches.length > 0 && result.matches[0].key !== 'name' && (
                  <div className="mt-2 pl-13 text-xs text-muted-foreground">
                    <HighlightMatches 
                      text={result.matches[0].value} 
                      matches={[result.matches[0]]}
                      maxLength={100}
                    />
                  </div>
                )}
              </div>
            );
          })}
        </div>
      </ScrollArea>

      {/* Footer */}
      <div className="p-2 border-t border-border bg-muted/50 text-xs text-muted-foreground text-center">
        Double-click to open • Use DFOL menu for batch operations
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

function HighlightMatches({ 
  text, 
  matches, 
  maxLength = 50 
}: { 
  text: string; 
  matches: Array<{ key: string; value: string; indices: number[][] }>;
  maxLength?: number;
}) {
  if (!matches || matches.length === 0) {
    return <span>{text.length > maxLength ? text.slice(0, maxLength) + '...' : text}</span>;
  }

  // Get all indices from all matches
  const allIndices = matches.flatMap(m => m.indices);
  allIndices.sort((a, b) => a[0] - b[0]);

  // Merge overlapping indices
  const mergedIndices: number[][] = [];
  let current: number[] | null = null;
  
  for (const [start, end] of allIndices) {
    if (!current || start > current[1] + 1) {
      if (current) mergedIndices.push(current);
      current = [start, end];
    } else {
      current[1] = Math.max(current[1], end);
    }
  }
  if (current) mergedIndices.push(current);

  // Build highlighted text
  const parts: React.ReactNode[] = [];
  let lastEnd = 0;
  
  for (const [start, end] of mergedIndices) {
    if (start > lastEnd) {
      parts.push(
        <span key={`text-${lastEnd}`}>
          {text.slice(lastEnd, start)}
        </span>
      );
    }
    parts.push(
      <mark key={`mark-${start}`} className="bg-yellow-200 dark:bg-yellow-900 px-0.5 rounded">
        {text.slice(start, end + 1)}
      </mark>
    );
    lastEnd = end + 1;
  }
  
  if (lastEnd < text.length) {
    parts.push(
      <span key={`text-${lastEnd}`}>
        {text.slice(lastEnd, maxLength)}
      </span>
    );
  }

  return <>{parts}{text.length > maxLength && '...'}</>;
}

function formatBytes(bytes: number): string {
  if (bytes === 0) return '-';
  const units = ['B', 'KB', 'MB', 'GB'];
  let size = bytes;
  let unitIndex = 0;
  while (size >= 1024 && unitIndex < units.length - 1) {
    size /= 1024;
    unitIndex++;
  }
  return `${size.toFixed(1)} ${units[unitIndex]}`;
}

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
import { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import { Terminal } from 'lucide-react';

export function BootScreen({ onBootComplete }: { onBootComplete?: () => void }) {
  const [bootText, setBootText] = useState<string[]>([]);
  const bootLines = ['Initializing kernel...', 'Loading drivers...', 'Mounting file systems...', 'Starting system services...', 'Ready.'];

  useEffect(() => {
    let lineIndex = 0;
    const interval = setInterval(() => {
      if (lineIndex < bootLines.length) {
        setBootText(prev => [...prev, bootLines[lineIndex]]);
        lineIndex++;
      } else {
        clearInterval(interval);
        setTimeout(onBootComplete, 500);
      }
    }, 400);
    return () => clearInterval(interval);
  }, [onBootComplete]);

  return (
    <div className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center h-full bg-black text-green-400 font-mono p-8">
      <Terminal className="w-16 h-16 mb-4 animate-pulse" />
      <div className="w-full max-w-md space-y-1">
        {bootText.map((line, i) => <div key={i} className="text-sm">{`> ${line}`}</div>)}
        <div className="animate-pulse">_</div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

          </Toggle>
          <Toggle
            pressed={viewMode === 'list'}
            onPressedChange={() => onViewModeChange('list')}
            className="h-8 w-8 rounded-none rounded-r-md data-[state=on]:bg-primary data-[state=on]:text-primary-foreground"
          >
            <List className="h-4 w-4" />
          </Toggle>

import { useTerminalStore, useTerminalSelectedFile } from '@/stores/terminalStore';
import { X, FileText } from 'lucide-react';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { ScrollArea } from '@/components/ui/scroll-area';

export function FileViewer() {
  const selectedFile = useTerminalSelectedFile();
  const selectFile = useTerminalStore((s) => s.selectFile);

  if (!selectedFile) return null;

  const isText = selectedFile.name.match(/\.(txt|js|ts|jsx|tsx|json|md|css|html|xml|sh|py|rb|go|java|c|cpp|h|hpp)$/i);

  return (
    <div className="h-full flex flex-col border-l border-border bg-card">
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between p-3 border-b border-border">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
          <FileText className="w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground" />
          <span className="text-sm font-medium truncate">{selectedFile.name}</span>
        </div>
        <Button variant="ghost" size="icon" className="h-7 w-7" onClick={() => selectFile(null)}>
          <X className="w-4 h-4" />
        </Button>
      </div>

      <ScrollArea className="flex-1 p-4">
        {isText ? (
          <pre className="text-sm font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words">
            {selectedFile.content || 'No content preview available'}
          </pre>
        ) : (
          <div className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center h-full text-muted-foreground">
            <FileText className="w-12 h-12 mb-2 opacity-50" />
            <p className="text-sm">Preview not available for binary files</p>
            <p className="text-xs">Size: {formatBytes(selectedFile.size)}</p>
          </div>
        )}
      </ScrollArea>
    </div>
  );
}

function formatBytes(bytes: number): string {
  if (bytes === 0) return '-';
  const units = ['B', 'KB', 'MB', 'GB'];
  let size = bytes;
  let unitIndex = 0;
  while (size >= 1024 && unitIndex < units.length - 1) {
    size /= 1024;
    unitIndex++;
  }
  return `${size.toFixed(1)} ${units[unitIndex]}`;
}

FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/prakash-app/src/components/Tree/TreeIconButton.tsx
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
import { TreePine } from 'lucide-react';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { useTreeStore } from '@/stores/treeStore';
import { TreeNode, NodeProperties } from '@/types/tree';

interface TreeIconButtonProps {
  item: any;
  sourceType: 'storage' | 'drive' | 'github' | 'terminal';
  panelId: string;
  className?: string;
}

export function TreeIconButton({ item, sourceType, panelId, className }: TreeIconButtonProps) {
  const openTree = useTreeStore((s) => s.openTree);

  const handleClick = async () => {
    // Build tree node from item
    const treeNode = await buildTreeNode(item, sourceType, panelId);
    openTree(treeNode);
  };

  return (
    <Button
      variant="ghost"
      size="icon"
      className={className}
      onClick={handleClick}
      title="View Tree Structure"
    >
      <TreePine className="w-4 h-4 text-primary" />
    </Button>
  );
}

async function buildTreeNode(
  item: any, 
  sourceType: string, 
  panelId: string
): Promise<TreeNode> {
  const baseNode: TreeNode = {
    id: item.id || item.name || String(Date.now()),
    name: item.name || 'Unknown',
    type: getNodeType(item, sourceType),
    path: item.path || item.name || '/',
    size: item.size || 0,
    lastModified: item.lastModified ? new Date(item.lastModified) : new Date(),
    depth: 0,
    properties: await buildProperties(item, sourceType),
  };

  // Build children if it's a directory
  if (baseNode.type === 'directory' && item.children) {
    baseNode.children = item.children.map((child: any, index: number) => ({
      ...buildTreeNode(child, sourceType, panelId),
      parent: baseNode,
      depth: 1,
    }));
  }

  return baseNode;
}

function getNodeType(item: any, sourceType: string): 'file' | 'directory' | 'symlink' | 'root' {
  if (sourceType === 'storage' || sourceType === 'terminal') {
    return item.kind === 'directory' ? 'directory' : 
           item.type === 'symlink' ? 'symlink' : 'file';
  }
  if (sourceType === 'drive') {
    return item.mimeType === 'application/vnd.google-apps.folder' ? 'directory' : 'file';
  }
  if (sourceType === 'github') {
    return item.type === 'dir' ? 'directory' : 
           item.type === 'symlink' ? 'symlink' : 'file';
  }
  return 'file';
}

async function buildProperties(item: any, sourceType: string): Promise<NodeProperties> {
  const props: NodeProperties = {
    createdAt: item.createdAt ? new Date(item.createdAt) : undefined,
    modifiedAt: item.lastModified ? new Date(item.lastModified) : undefined,
    mimeType: item.mimeType,
    isHidden: item.name?.startsWith('.'),
    isReadOnly: item.permissions && !item.permissions.includes('w'),
  };

  // Add source-specific properties
  switch (sourceType) {
    case 'storage':
      props.permissions = item.permissions;
      props.mountPath = item.path;
      break;
    case 'drive':
      props.fileSystemType = 'Google Drive';
      props.label = 'Cloud Storage';
      break;
    case 'github':
      props.fileSystemType = 'Git Repository';
      props.owner = item.owner;
      props.version = item.sha;
      break;
    case 'terminal':
      props.fileSystemType = 'WebContainer FS';
      props.permissions = item.permissions;
      props.owner = 'root';
      props.group = 'root';
      break;
  }

  return props;
}
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/prakash-app/src/components/Tree/TreeViewModal.tsx
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
import { Dialog, DialogContent, DialogHeader, DialogTitle } from '@/components/ui/dialog';
import { Folder, File } from 'lucide-react';

export function TreeViewModal({ isOpen = false, onClose, items = [], title = 'File Tree' }: any) {
  const renderTree = (items: any[], depth = 0) => items.map((item) => (
    <div key={item.id} style={{ paddingLeft: `${depth * 16}px` }} className="py-1">
      <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
        {item.type === 'folder' ? <Folder className="w-4 h-4 text-blue-500" /> : <File className="w-4 h-4 text-gray-500" />}
        <span className="text-sm">{item.name}</span>
      </div>
      {item.children && renderTree(item.children, depth + 1)}
    </div>
  ));
  return (
    <Dialog open={isOpen} onOpenChange={onClose}>
      <DialogContent>
        <DialogHeader><DialogTitle>{title}</DialogTitle></DialogHeader>
        <div className="max-h-[400px] overflow-auto">{items.length === 0 ? <div>No items</div> : renderTree(items)}</div>
      </DialogContent>
    </Dialog>
  );
}

import * as React from "react"
import { Slot } from "@radix-ui/react-slot"
import { cva, type VariantProps } from "class-variance-authority"

import { cn } from "@/lib/utils"

const buttonVariants = cva(
  "inline-flex items-center justify-center gap-2 whitespace-nowrap rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-all disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 [&_svg]:pointer-events-none [&_svg:not([class*='size-'])]:size-4 shrink-0 [&_svg]:shrink-0 outline-none focus-visible:border-ring focus-visible:ring-ring/50 focus-visible:ring-[3px] aria-invalid:ring-destructive/20 dark:aria-invalid:ring-destructive/40 aria-invalid:border-destructive",
  {
    variants: {
      variant: {
        default: "bg-primary text-primary-foreground hover:bg-primary/90",
        destructive:
          "bg-destructive text-white hover:bg-destructive/90 focus-visible:ring-destructive/20 dark:focus-visible:ring-destructive/40 dark:bg-destructive/60",
        outline:
          "border bg-background shadow-xs hover:bg-accent hover:text-accent-foreground dark:bg-input/30 dark:border-input dark:hover:bg-input/50",
        secondary:
          "bg-secondary text-secondary-foreground hover:bg-secondary/80",
        ghost:
          "hover:bg-accent hover:text-accent-foreground dark:hover:bg-accent/50",
        link: "text-primary underline-offset-4 hover:underline",
      },
      size: {
        default: "h-9 px-4 py-2 has-[>svg]:px-3",
        sm: "h-8 rounded-md gap-1.5 px-3 has-[>svg]:px-2.5",
        lg: "h-10 rounded-md px-6 has-[>svg]:px-4",
        icon: "size-9",
      },
    },
    defaultVariants: {
      variant: "default",
      size: "default",
    },
  }
)

function Button({
  className,
  variant,
  size,
  asChild = false,
  ...props
}: React.ComponentProps<"button"> &
  VariantProps<typeof buttonVariants> & {
    asChild?: boolean
  }) {
  const Comp = asChild ? Slot : "button"

  return (
    <Comp
      data-slot="button"
      className={cn(buttonVariants({ variant, size, className }))}
      {...props}
    />
  )
}

export { Button, buttonVariants }

import * as React from "react";

export function Badge({
  children,
  className = "",
  variant = "default",
}: {
  children: React.ReactNode;
  className?: string;
  variant?: "default" | "secondary" | "outline" | "destructive";
}) {
  const base =
    "inline-flex items-center rounded-md px-2 py-0.5 text-xs font-medium";

  const variants: Record<string, string> = {
    default: "bg-primary text-white",
    secondary: "bg-gray-200 text-gray-800",
    outline: "border border-gray-300 text-gray-800",
    destructive: "bg-red-500 text-white",
  };

  return (
    <span className={`${base} ${variants[variant]} ${className}`}>
      {children}
    </span>
  );
}

import * as React from "react";

export function Switch({
  checked,
  onCheckedChange,
}: {
  checked?: boolean;
  onCheckedChange?: (checked: boolean) => void;
}) {
  return (
    <button
      onClick={() => onCheckedChange?.(!checked)}
      className={`w-10 h-5 flex items-center rounded-full transition ${
        checked ? "bg-primary" : "bg-gray-300"
      }`}
    >
      <div
        className={`w-4 h-4 bg-white rounded-full shadow transform transition ${
          checked ? "translate-x-5" : "translate-x-1"
        }`}
      />
    </button>
  );
}

import { usePanelStore, usePanels, useActivePanelId } from '@/stores/panelStore';
import { ResizablePanel } from './Panel/ResizablePanel';
import { GlobalSearchBar } from './Search/GlobalSearchBar';
import { FilterPanel } from './Search/FilterPanel';
import { SearchResultsOverlay } from './Search/SearchResultsOverlay';
import { Plus } from 'lucide-react';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { MAX_PANELS } from '@/types/panel';

export function PanelContainer() {
  const panels = usePanels();
  const activePanelId = useActivePanelId();
  const { addPanel, removePanel, setActivePanel } = usePanelStore();

  const canAddPanel = panels.length < MAX_PANELS;

  return (
    <div className="flex-1 flex flex-col h-full overflow-hidden bg-background">
      {/* Top bar with search */}
      <div className="flex items-center gap-4 px-4 py-2 border-b border-border bg-card">
        <GlobalSearchBar />
        
        <Button
          variant="outline"
          size="sm"
          onClick={addPanel}
          disabled={!canAddPanel}
          className="shrink-0 gap-2"
        >
          <Plus className="h-4 w-4" />
          Add Panel
        </Button>
      </div>

      {/* Filter Panel */}
      <FilterPanel />

      {/* Search Results */}
      <SearchResultsOverlay />

      {/* Panels */}
      <div className="flex-1 flex overflow-x-auto overflow-y-hidden">
        {panels.map((panel, index) => (
          <ResizablePanel
            key={panel.id}
            panel={panel}
            isActive={panel.id === activePanelId}
            isLast={index === panels.length - 1}
            onActivate={() => setActivePanel(panel.id)}
            onClose={() => removePanel(panel.id)}
          />
        ))}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

import { useAppStore } from '@/stores/appStore';
import { FileManager } from './FileManager';
import { 
  HardDrive, 
  FolderGit, 
  Github, 
  Terminal,
  FileText,
  Database
} from 'lucide-react';

const placeholderContent: Record<string, { title: string; icon: React.ElementType; component?: React.ReactNode }> = {
  storage: {
    title: 'File Manager',
    icon: Database,
    component: <FileManager />,
  },
  drive: {
    title: 'Drive Files',
    icon: FolderGit,
  },
  github: {
    title: 'GitHub Repositories',
    icon: Github,
  },
  terminal: {
    title: 'Terminal Sessions',
    icon: Terminal,
  },
};

function PlaceholderContent({ source }: { source: string }) {
  const content = placeholderContent[source];
  const Icon = content.icon;

  return (
    <div className="flex-1 bg-background p-6 overflow-auto">
      <div className="max-w-4xl mx-auto">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-3 mb-6">
          <div className="p-3 rounded-xl bg-primary/10 text-primary">
            <Icon className="w-8 h-8" />
          </div>
          <div>
            <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold text-foreground">{content.title}</h2>
            <p className="text-muted-foreground">Placeholder for {source} content</p>
          </div>
        </div>

        <div className="p-8 rounded-lg border border-border bg-card">
          <p className="text-muted-foreground text-center">
            This feature is not yet implemented.
          </p>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

export function RightPanel() {
  const activeSource = useAppStore((state) => state.activeSource);
  const content = placeholderContent[activeSource];

  // If storage is selected, show FileManager
  if (activeSource === 'storage' && content.component) {
    return (
      <div className="flex-1 h-screen overflow-hidden">
        {content.component}
      </div>
    );
  }

  return <PlaceholderContent source={activeSource} />;
}
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/prakash-app/src/hooks/useResizable.ts
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
import { useState, useCallback, useRef, useEffect } from 'react';

interface UseResizableOptions {
  initialWidth: number;
  minWidth: number;
  onResize: (width: number) => void;
}

export function useResizable({ initialWidth, minWidth, onResize }: UseResizableOptions) {
  const [isResizing, setIsResizing] = useState(false);
  const [currentWidth, setCurrentWidth] = useState(initialWidth);
  const startXRef = useRef(0);
  const startWidthRef = useRef(initialWidth);

  const startResize = useCallback((e: React.MouseEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    setIsResizing(true);
    startXRef.current = e.clientX;
    startWidthRef.current = currentWidth;
  }, [currentWidth]);

  useEffect(() => {
    const handleMouseMove = (e: MouseEvent) => {
      if (!isResizing) return;
      
      const delta = e.clientX - startXRef.current;
      const newWidth = Math.max(minWidth, startWidthRef.current + delta);
      setCurrentWidth(newWidth);
      onResize(newWidth);
    };

    const handleMouseUp = () => {
      setIsResizing(false);
    };

    if (isResizing) {
      document.addEventListener('mousemove', handleMouseMove);
      document.addEventListener('mouseup', handleMouseUp);
      document.body.style.cursor = 'col-resize';
      document.body.style.userSelect = 'none';
    }

    return () => {
      document.removeEventListener('mousemove', handleMouseMove);
      document.removeEventListener('mouseup', handleMouseUp);
      document.body.style.cursor = '';
      document.body.style.userSelect = '';
    };
  }, [isResizing, minWidth, onResize]);

  return {
    width: currentWidth,
    isResizing,
    startResize,
  };
}
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/prakash-app/src/lib/utils.ts
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
import { type ClassValue, clsx } from "clsx"
import { twMerge } from "tailwind-merge"

export function cn(...inputs: ClassValue[]) {
  return twMerge(clsx(inputs))
}
