FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/prakash-app/src/lib/conversionEngines.ts
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
import { ConversionEngine, CONVERSION_RULES } from '@/types/rename';
import { FFmpeg } from '@ffmpeg/ffmpeg';
import { fetchFile, toBlobURL } from '@ffmpeg/util';
import JSZip from 'jszip';
import mammoth from 'mammoth';
import { saveAs } from 'file-saver';

// FFmpeg WASM Engine
class FFmpegEngine implements ConversionEngine {
  name = 'ffmpeg';
  isReady = false;
  private ffmpeg: FFmpeg | null = null;

  async init(): Promise<void> {
    if (this.isReady) return;
    
    this.ffmpeg = new FFmpeg();
    const baseURL = 'https://unpkg.com/@ffmpeg/core@0.12.6/dist/umd';
    
    await this.ffmpeg.load({
      coreURL: await toBlobURL(`${baseURL}/ffmpeg-core.js`, 'text/javascript'),
      wasmURL: await toBlobURL(`${baseURL}/ffmpeg-core.wasm`, 'application/wasm'),
    });
    
    this.isReady = true;
  }

  async convert(
    file: Blob, 
    fromExt: string, 
    toExt: string, 
    onProgress?: (p: number) => void
  ): Promise<Blob> {
    if (!this.ffmpeg) throw new Error('FFmpeg not initialized');
    
    const inputName = `input${fromExt}`;
    const outputName = `output${toExt}`;
    
    // Write file to FFmpeg FS
    const fileData = await fetchFile(file);
    await this.ffmpeg.writeFile(inputName, fileData);
    
    // Run conversion
    const args = this.getConversionArgs(fromExt, toExt, inputName, outputName);
    
    this.ffmpeg.on('progress', ({ progress }) => {
      onProgress?.(Math.round(progress * 100));
    });
    
    await this.ffmpeg.exec(args);
    
    // Read output
    const data = await this.ffmpeg.readFile(outputName);
    const outputBlob = new Blob([data], { type: this.getMimeType(toExt) });
    
    // Cleanup
    await this.ffmpeg.deleteFile(inputName);
    await this.ffmpeg.deleteFile(outputName);
    
    return outputBlob;
  }

  private getConversionArgs(fromExt: string, toExt: string, input: string, output: string): string[] {
    // Video to video
    if (['.mp4', '.avi', '.mov', '.mkv', '.webm'].includes(fromExt)) {
      if (toExt === '.webm') return ['-i', input, '-c:v', 'libvpx-vp9', '-c:a', 'libopus', output];
      return ['-i', input, '-c:v', 'libx264', '-c:a', 'aac', output];
    }
    
    // Audio to audio
    if (['.mp3', '.wav', '.aac', '.ogg', '.flac'].includes(fromExt)) {
      if (toExt === '.mp3') return ['-i', input, '-c:a', 'libmp3lame', '-q:a', '2', output];
      return ['-i', input, output];
    }
    
    return ['-i', input, output];
  }

  private getMimeType(ext: string): string {
    const mimeTypes: Record<string, string> = {
      '.mp4': 'video/mp4',
      '.webm': 'video/webm',
      '.mp3': 'audio/mpeg',
      '.wav': 'audio/wav',
    };
    return mimeTypes[ext] || 'application/octet-stream';
  }
}

// Sharp-like Image Engine (using Canvas API for browser)
class CanvasImageEngine implements ConversionEngine {
  name = 'sharp';
  isReady = true;

  async init(): Promise<void> {
    this.isReady = true;
  }

  async convert(
    file: Blob, 
    fromExt: string, 
    toExt: string, 
    onProgress?: (p: number) => void
  ): Promise<Blob> {
    return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
      const img = new Image();
      const url = URL.createObjectURL(file);
      
      img.onload = () => {
        const canvas = document.createElement('canvas');
        canvas.width = img.width;
        canvas.height = img.height;
        
        const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
        if (!ctx) {
          reject(new Error('Canvas not supported'));
          return;
        }
        
        // Handle transparency for PNG/WebP
        if (toExt === '.png' || toExt === '.webp') {
          ctx.clearRect(0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);
        }
        
        ctx.drawImage(img, 0, 0);
        URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
        
        const mimeType = toExt === '.jpg' || toExt === '.jpeg' 
          ? 'image/jpeg' 
          : toExt === '.webp' 
            ? 'image/webp' 
            : 'image/png';
        
        canvas.toBlob((blob) => {
          if (blob) {
            resolve(blob);
          } else {
            reject(new Error('Canvas to Blob failed'));
          }
        }, mimeType, 0.9);
      };
      
      img.onerror = () => {
        URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
        reject(new Error('Image load failed'));
      };
      
      img.src = url;
    });
  }
}

// Mammoth Document Engine
class MammothEngine implements ConversionEngine {
  name = 'mammoth';
  isReady = true;

  async init(): Promise<void> {
    this.isReady = true;
  }

  async convert(
    file: Blob, 
    fromExt: string, 
    toExt: string, 
    onProgress?: (p: number) => void
  ): Promise<Blob> {
    const arrayBuffer = await file.arrayBuffer();
    
    let result: { value: string };
    
    if (toExt === '.html') {
      result = await mammoth.convertToHtml({ arrayBuffer });
    } else {
      result = await mammoth.extractRawText({ arrayBuffer });
    }
    
    const mimeType = toExt === '.html' ? 'text/html' : 'text/plain';
    return new Blob([result.value], { type: mimeType });
  }
}

// JSZip Archive Engine
class JSZipEngine implements ConversionEngine {
  name = 'jszip';
  isReady = true;

  async init(): Promise<void> {
    this.isReady = true;
  }

  async convert(
    file: Blob, 
    fromExt: string, 
    toExt: string, 
    onProgress?: (p: number) => void
  ): Promise<Blob> {
    // For folder to zip conversion
    // This requires the folder contents to be passed separately
    // For now, return empty zip as placeholder
    const zip = new JSZip();
    const content = await zip.generateAsync({ type: 'blob' });
    return content;
  }

  async compressFolder(
    files: { name: string; content: Blob | string }[],
    onProgress?: (p: number) => void
  ): Promise<Blob> {
    const zip = new JSZip();
    
    files.forEach((file, index) => {
      zip.file(file.name, file.content);
      onProgress?.(Math.round((index / files.length) * 50));
    });
    
    const content = await zip.generateAsync(
      { type: 'blob' },
      (metadata) => {
        onProgress?.(50 + Math.round(metadata.percent / 2));
      }
    );
    
    return content;
  }
}

// Export engines
export const ffmpegEngine = new FFmpegEngine();
export const imageEngine = new CanvasImageEngine();
export const mammothEngine = new MammothEngine();
export const zipEngine = new JSZipEngine();

export function getEngineForConversion(fromExt: string, toExt: string): ConversionEngine | null {
  const rule = CONVERSION_RULES.find(r => 
    r.from.includes(fromExt.toLowerCase()) && r.to === toExt.toLowerCase()
  );
  
  if (!rule) return null;
  
  switch (rule.engine) {
    case 'ffmpeg': return ffmpegEngine;
    case 'sharp': return imageEngine;
    case 'mammoth': return mammothEngine;
    case 'jszip': return zipEngine;
    default: return null;
  }
}

export function needsConversion(oldName: string, newName: string): boolean {
  const oldExt = getExtension(oldName);
  const newExt = getExtension(newName);
  return oldExt !== newExt && getEngineForConversion(oldExt, newExt) !== null;
}

export function getExtension(filename: string): string {
  const ext = filename.slice(filename.lastIndexOf('.')).toLowerCase();
  return ext.includes('.') ? ext : '';
}

FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/prakash-app/src/lib/fileSystemBackend.ts
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
export const fileSystemBackend = {
  async pickDirectory(): Promise<FileSystemDirectoryHandle | null> {
    try {
      const handle = await window.showDirectoryPicker();
      return handle;
    } catch (err) {
      console.warn('Directory picker cancelled or failed', err);
      return null;
    }
  },

  async readDirectory(handle: FileSystemDirectoryHandle) {
    const entries: any[] = [];
    for await (const entry of handle.values()) {
      let size = 0;
      let lastModified = new Date();
      if (entry.kind === 'file') {
        const file = await entry.getFile();
        size = file.size;
        lastModified = new Date(file.lastModified);
      } else if (entry.kind === 'directory') {
        // For directories we don't pre-calculate size
        size = 0;
      }
      entries.push({
        name: entry.name,
        kind: entry.kind,
        size,
        lastModified,
        handle: entry,
      });
    }
    // Sort: directories first, then files
    entries.sort((a, b) => {
      if (a.kind === 'directory' && b.kind !== 'directory') return -1;
      if (a.kind !== 'directory' && b.kind === 'directory') return 1;
      return a.name.localeCompare(b.name);
    });
    return entries;
  },

  async createDirectory(parentHandle: FileSystemDirectoryHandle, name: string) {
    return parentHandle.getDirectoryHandle(name, { create: true });
  },

  async deleteEntry(parentHandle: FileSystemDirectoryHandle, name: string) {
    return parentHandle.removeEntry(name, { recursive: true });
  },

  async renameEntry(parentHandle: FileSystemDirectoryHandle, oldName: string, newName: string) {
    const oldEntry = await parentHandle.getFileHandle(oldName).catch(() =>
      parentHandle.getDirectoryHandle(oldName)
    );
    const file = await oldEntry.getFile();
    const newHandle = await parentHandle.getFileHandle(newName, { create: true });
    const writable = await newHandle.createWritable();
    await writable.write(file);
    await writable.close();
    await parentHandle.removeEntry(oldName, { recursive: true });
  },

  async getFileSize(handle: FileSystemFileHandle) {
    const file = await handle.getFile();
    return file.size;
  },

  async getFileDate(handle: FileSystemFileHandle) {
    const file = await handle.getFile();
    return new Date(file.lastModified);
  },
};

FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/prakash-app/src/lib/githubApi.ts
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
import { Octokit } from '@octokit/rest';
import { 
  GitHubAccount, 
  GitHubRepository, 
  GitHubContent,
  GitHubPermission 
} from '@/types/github';

class GitHubApi {
  private octokit: Octokit | null = null;
  private currentToken: string | null = null;

  async authenticate(token: string): Promise<{ username: string; avatarUrl?: string }> {
    this.octokit = new Octokit({ auth: token });
    this.currentToken = token;

    try {
      const { data } = await this.octokit.users.getAuthenticated();
      return {
        username: data.login,
        avatarUrl: data.avatar_url,
      };
    } catch (error) {
      throw new Error('Invalid token or authentication failed');
    }
  }

  setToken(token: string): void {
    this.octokit = new Octokit({ auth: token });
    this.currentToken = token;
  }

  async listRepositories(username: string): Promise<GitHubRepository[]> {
    if (!this.octokit) throw new Error('Not authenticated');

    try {
      const { data } = await this.octokit.repos.listForUser({
        username,
        sort: 'updated',
        per_page: 100,
      });
      return data as GitHubRepository[];
    } catch (error) {
      throw new Error('Failed to fetch repositories');
    }
  }

  async getRepositoryContents(
    owner: string,
    repo: string,
    path: string = ''
  ): Promise<GitHubContent[]> {
    if (!this.octokit) throw new Error('Not authenticated');

    try {
      const { data } = await this.octokit.repos.getContent({
        owner,
        repo,
        path,
      });

      // Handle single file vs directory
      if (!Array.isArray(data)) {
        return [data as GitHubContent];
      }

      return data as GitHubContent[];
    } catch (error) {
      throw new Error('Failed to fetch repository contents');
    }
  }

  async getFileContent(
    owner: string,
    repo: string,
    path: string
  ): Promise<{ content: string; name: string; downloadUrl: string | null }> {
    if (!this.octokit) throw new Error('Not authenticated');

    try {
      const { data } = await this.octokit.repos.getContent({
        owner,
        repo,
        path,
      });

      if (Array.isArray(data)) {
        throw new Error('Path is a directory, not a file');
      }

      const fileData = data as GitHubContent;
      
      // Decode base64 content
      let decodedContent = '';
      if (fileData.content && fileData.encoding === 'base64') {
        decodedContent = atob(fileData.content.replace(/\n/g, ''));
      }

      return {
        content: decodedContent,
        name: fileData.name,
        downloadUrl: fileData.download_url,
      };
    } catch (error) {
      throw new Error('Failed to fetch file content');
    }
  }

  async validateToken(token: string): Promise<boolean> {
    try {
      const tempOctokit = new Octokit({ auth: token });
      await tempOctokit.users.getAuthenticated();
      return true;
    } catch {
      return false;
    }
  }

  getPermissionLevel(scopes: string[]): GitHubPermission {
    // Determine permission based on token scopes
    if (scopes.includes('delete_repo') || scopes.includes('admin:org')) {
      return 'admin';
    }
    if (scopes.includes('repo')) {
      return 'write';
    }
    if (scopes.includes('write:discussion')) {
      return 'triage';
    }
    return 'read';
  }

  formatDate(dateString: string): string {
    const date = new Date(dateString);
    return date.toLocaleDateString('en-US', {
      month: 'short',
      day: 'numeric',
      year: 'numeric',
    });
  }

  formatFileSize(bytes: number): string {
    if (bytes === 0) return '-';
    const units = ['B', 'KB', 'MB', 'GB'];
    let size = bytes;
    let unitIndex = 0;
    while (size >= 1024 && unitIndex < units.length - 1) {
      size /= 1024;
      unitIndex++;
    }
    return `${size.toFixed(1)} ${units[unitIndex]}`;
  }
}

export const githubApi = new GitHubApi();

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
import { openDB, DBSchema, IDBPDatabase } from 'idb';
import { GitHubAccount } from '@/types/github';
import CryptoJS from 'crypto-js';

const DB_NAME = 'github-accounts-db';
const DB_VERSION = 1;
const STORE_NAME = 'accounts';

// Encryption key - in production, use a more secure method
const ENCRYPTION_KEY = import.meta.env.VITE_GITHUB_ENCRYPTION_KEY || 'your-secure-key-here';

interface GitHubDBSchema extends DBSchema {
  accounts: {
    key: string;
    value: {
      id: string;
      encryptedData: string;
      addedAt: number;
    };
  };
}

class GitHubStorage {
  private db: IDBPDatabase<GitHubDBSchema> | null = null;

  async init(): Promise<void> {
    this.db = await openDB<GitHubDBSchema>(DB_NAME, DB_VERSION, {
      upgrade(db) {
        if (!db.objectStoreNames.contains(STORE_NAME)) {
          db.createObjectStore(STORE_NAME, { keyPath: 'id' });
        }
      },
    });
  }

  private encrypt(data: string): string {
    return CryptoJS.AES.encrypt(data, ENCRYPTION_KEY).toString();
  }

  private decrypt(encryptedData: string): string {
    const bytes = CryptoJS.AES.decrypt(encryptedData, ENCRYPTION_KEY);
    return bytes.toString(CryptoJS.enc.Utf8);
  }

  async saveAccount(account: GitHubAccount): Promise<void> {
    if (!this.db) await this.init();

    const dataToEncrypt = JSON.stringify({
      token: account.token,
      avatarUrl: account.avatarUrl,
      permissions: account.permissions,
    });

    await this.db!.put(STORE_NAME, {
      id: account.id,
      encryptedData: this.encrypt(dataToEncrypt),
      addedAt: account.addedAt,
    });
  }

  async getAllAccounts(): Promise<GitHubAccount[]> {
    if (!this.db) await this.init();

    const allData = await this.db!.getAll(STORE_NAME);
    
    return allData.map((item) => {
      try {
        const decrypted = JSON.parse(this.decrypt(item.encryptedData));
        return {
          id: item.id,
          token: decrypted.token,
          avatarUrl: decrypted.avatarUrl,
          permissions: decrypted.permissions,
          addedAt: item.addedAt,
        };
      } catch (e) {
        console.error('Failed to decrypt account:', item.id);
        return null;
      }
    }).filter((acc): acc is GitHubAccount => acc !== null);
  }

  async deleteAccount(username: string): Promise<void> {
    if (!this.db) await this.init();
    await this.db!.delete(STORE_NAME, username);
  }

  async clearAll(): Promise<void> {
    if (!this.db) await this.init();
    await this.db!.clear(STORE_NAME);
  }
}

export const githubStorage = new GitHubStorage();

import { GoogleAccount, DriveFile, DriveFolder } from '@/types/drive';

const DISCOVERY_DOC = 'https://www.googleapis.com/discovery/v1/apis/drive/v3/rest';
const SCOPES = 'https://www.googleapis.com/auth/drive.readonly https://www.googleapis.com/auth/drive.file';

class GoogleDriveApi {
  private gapiInited = false;
  private gsiInited = false;
  private tokenClient: any = null;

  async initialize(gapi: any, tokenClient: any): Promise<void> {
    this.tokenClient = tokenClient;
    this.gsiInited = true;
    this.gapiInited = true;
  }

  async listFiles(account: GoogleAccount, folderId: string = 'root'): Promise<DriveFile[]> {
    const response = await fetch(
      `https://www.googleapis.com/drive/v3/files?q='${folderId}'+in+parents+and+trashed=false&fields=files(id,name,mimeType,modifiedTime,size,thumbnailLink,iconLink,webViewLink,parents)&orderBy=name&pageSize=100`,
      {
        headers: {
          'Authorization': `Bearer ${account.accessToken}`,
        },
      }
    );

    if (!response.ok) {
      if (response.status === 401) {
        throw new Error('Token expired');
      }
      throw new Error(`Drive API error: ${response.status}`);
    }

    const data = await response.json();
    return data.files || [];
  }

  async getFileInfo(account: GoogleAccount, fileId: string): Promise<DriveFile> {
    const response = await fetch(
      `https://www.googleapis.com/drive/v3/files/${fileId}?fields=id,name,mimeType,modifiedTime,size,thumbnailLink,iconLink,webViewLink,parents`,
      {
        headers: {
          'Authorization': `Bearer ${account.accessToken}`,
        },
      }
    );

    if (!response.ok) {
      throw new Error(`Failed to get file info: ${response.status}`);
    }

    return response.json();
  }

  isFolder(file: DriveFile): boolean {
    return file.mimeType === 'application/vnd.google-apps.folder';
  }

  formatFileSize(size?: string): string {
    if (!size) return '-';
    const bytes = parseInt(size, 10);
    if (isNaN(bytes)) return '-';
    
    const units = ['B', 'KB', 'MB', 'GB', 'TB'];
    let unitIndex = 0;
    let sizeNum = bytes;
    
    while (sizeNum >= 1024 && unitIndex < units.length - 1) {
      sizeNum /= 1024;
      unitIndex++;
    }
    
    return `${sizeNum.toFixed(1)} ${units[unitIndex]}`;
  }

  formatDate(dateString: string): string {
    const date = new Date(dateString);
    return date.toLocaleDateString('en-US', {
      month: 'short',
      day: 'numeric',
      year: 'numeric',
    });
  }

  getGmailUsername(email: string): string {
    return email.split('@')[0];
  }
}

export const driveApi = new GoogleDriveApi();

FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/prakash-app/src/lib/webcontainerApi.ts
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
import { WebContainer } from '@webcontainer/api';
import { TerminalFileSystemEntry, TerminalDirectory, TerminalFile } from '@/types/terminal';

class WebContainerApi {
  private instance: WebContainer | null = null;
  private isBooting = false;

  async init(onProgress?: (progress: number) => void): Promise<WebContainer> {
    if (this.instance) return this.instance;
    if (this.isBooting) {
      // Wait for existing boot
      while (this.isBooting) {
        await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 100));
      }
      return this.instance!;
    }

    this.isBooting = true;

    try {
      // Boot WebContainer with progress tracking
      this.instance = await WebContainer.boot({
        onProgress: (progress) => {
          onProgress?.(progress);
        },
      });

      this.isBooting = false;
      return this.instance;
    } catch (error) {
      this.isBooting = false;
      throw new Error(`Failed to boot WebContainer: ${(error as Error).message}`);
    }
  }

  getInstance(): WebContainer | null {
    return this.instance;
  }

  async readDirectory(path: string): Promise<TerminalFileSystemEntry[]> {
    if (!this.instance) throw new Error('WebContainer not initialized');

    try {
      // Use WebContainer's fs API to read directory
      const fs = this.instance.fs;
      const entries = await fs.readdir(path, { withFileTypes: true });

      const result: TerminalFileSystemEntry[] = [];

      for (const entry of entries) {
        const fullPath = `${path === '/' ? '' : path}/${entry.name}`;
        
        let type: 'file' | 'directory' | 'symlink' = 'file';
        if (entry.isDirectory()) type = 'directory';
        else if (entry.isSymbolicLink()) type = 'symlink';

        let size = 0;
        let lastModified = new Date();

        try {
          const stats = await fs.stat(fullPath);
          size = stats.size || 0;
          lastModified = new Date(stats.mtime || Date.now());
        } catch (e) {
          // Some entries might not have stats
        }

        result.push({
          name: entry.name,
          type,
          size,
          lastModified,
          permissions: this.formatPermissions(stats),
          path: fullPath,
        });
      }

      return result.sort((a, b) => {
        // Directories first, then files
        if (a.type === 'directory' && b.type !== 'directory') return -1;
        if (a.type !== 'directory' && b.type === 'directory') return 1;
        return a.name.localeCompare(b.name);
      });
    } catch (error) {
      throw new Error(`Failed to read directory: ${(error as Error).message}`);
    }
  }

  async readFile(path: string): Promise<string> {
    if (!this.instance) throw new Error('WebContainer not initialized');

    try {
      const fs = this.instance.fs;
      const content = await fs.readFile(path, 'utf-8');
      return content;
    } catch (error) {
      throw new Error(`Failed to read file: ${(error as Error).message}`);
    }
  }

  async getFileStats(path: string): Promise<any> {
    if (!this.instance) throw new Error('WebContainer not initialized');

    try {
      const fs = this.instance.fs;
      return await fs.stat(path);
    } catch (error) {
      return null;
    }
  }

  formatPermissions(stats: any): string {
    if (!stats) return '---------';
    
    const mode = stats.mode || 0;
    const perms = [
      mode & 0o400 ? 'r' : '-',
      mode & 0o200 ? 'w' : '-',
      mode & 0o100 ? 'x' : '-',
      mode & 0o040 ? 'r' : '-',
      mode & 0o020 ? 'w' : '-',
      mode & 0o010 ? 'x' : '-',
      mode & 0o004 ? 'r' : '-',
      mode & 0o002 ? 'w' : '-',
      mode & 0o001 ? 'x' : '-',
    ];
    
    return perms.join('');
  }

  formatFileSize(bytes: number): string {
    if (bytes === 0) return '-';
    const units = ['B', 'KB', 'MB', 'GB'];
    let size = bytes;
    let unitIndex = 0;
    while (size >= 1024 && unitIndex < units.length - 1) {
      size /= 1024;
      unitIndex++;
    }
    return `${size.toFixed(1)} ${units[unitIndex]}`;
  }

  formatDate(date: Date): string {
    return date.toLocaleDateString('en-US', {
      month: 'short',
      day: 'numeric',
      hour: '2-digit',
      minute: '2-digit',
    });
  }

  isReady(): boolean {
    return this.instance !== null && !this.isBooting;
  }

  async shutdown(): Promise<void> {
    if (this.instance) {
      // WebContainer doesn't have explicit shutdown, but we can clear reference
      this.instance = null;
      this.isBooting = false;
    }
  }
}

export const webcontainerApi = new WebContainerApi();

FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/prakash-app/src/lib/fileSystemBackend.t
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
// src/lib/fileSystemBackend.ts

export const fileSystemBackend = {
  async createDirectory(parentHandle: any, name: string) {
    try {
      if (!parentHandle || !parentHandle.getDirectoryHandle) {
        throw new Error('Invalid directory handle');
      }

      await parentHandle.getDirectoryHandle(name, { create: true });
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('createDirectory failed:', error);
      throw error;
    }
  },

  async deleteEntry(parentHandle: any, name: string) {
    try {
      await parentHandle.removeEntry(name, { recursive: true });
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('deleteEntry failed:', error);
      throw error;
    }
  },

  async renameEntry(parentHandle: any, oldName: string, newName: string) {
    try {
      const entry = await parentHandle.getFileHandle(oldName).catch(() =>
        parentHandle.getDirectoryHandle(oldName)
      );

      const file = await entry.getFile();
      const newHandle = await parentHandle.getFileHandle(newName, { create: true });
      const writable = await newHandle.createWritable();

      await writable.write(file);
      await writable.close();

      await parentHandle.removeEntry(oldName, { recursive: true });
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('renameEntry failed:', error);
      throw error;
    }
  }
};

FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/prakash-app/src/stores/logStore.ts
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
import { create } from 'zustand';
import { persist } from 'zustand/middleware';
import { v4 as uuidv4 } from 'uuid';

export type LogLevel = 'debug' | 'info' | 'warn' | 'error';
export type LogCategory = 'auth' | 'file' | 'system' | 'network' | 'ui';

interface LogEntry {
  id: string;
  timestamp: number;
  level: LogLevel;
  category: LogCategory;
  action: string;
  details: Record<string, any>;
  userId: string;
  sessionId: string;
  panelId?: string;
  sourceType?: string;
  duration?: number;
}

interface Notification {
  id: string;
  type: 'info' | 'success' | 'warning' | 'error';
  title: string;
  message: string;
  timestamp: number;
  read: boolean;
  action?: { label: string; onClick: () => void };
}

interface LogState {
  logs: LogEntry[];
  isLiveLogOpen: boolean;
  notifications: Notification[];
  unreadCount: number;
  logLevel: LogLevel;
  logCategories: LogCategory[];
  // actions
  logAction: (action: string, details?: any, category?: LogCategory, level?: LogLevel) => void;
  toggleLiveLog: () => void;
  clearLogs: () => void;
  exportLogs: () => Promise<Blob>;
  setLogLevel: (level: LogLevel) => void;
  toggleCategory: (category: LogCategory) => void;
  addNotification: (notif: Omit<Notification, 'id' | 'timestamp' | 'read'>) => void;
  markNotificationRead: (id: string) => void;
  markAllRead: () => void;
  dismissNotification: (id: string) => void;
  startBackgroundChecks: () => void;
  stopBackgroundChecks: () => void;
}

export const useLogStore = create<LogState>()(
  persist(
    (set, get) => ({
      logs: [],
      isLiveLogOpen: false,
      notifications: [],
      unreadCount: 0,
      logLevel: 'info',
      logCategories: ['auth', 'file', 'system', 'network', 'ui'],

      logAction: (action, details = {}, category = 'system', level = 'info') => {
        const entry: LogEntry = {
          id: uuidv4(),
          timestamp: Date.now(),
          level,
          category,
          action,
          details,
          userId: 'system',
          sessionId: 'session',
        };
        set((state) => ({
          logs: [...state.logs.slice(-999), entry],
        }));
        // Also create notification for errors/warnings
        if (level === 'error') {
          get().addNotification({
            type: 'error',
            title: action,
            message: details.message || details.error || 'An error occurred',
          });
        } else if (level === 'warn') {
          get().addNotification({
            type: 'warning',
            title: action,
            message: details.message || 'Warning',
          });
        }
      },

      toggleLiveLog: () => set((state) => ({ isLiveLogOpen: !state.isLiveLogOpen })),

      clearLogs: () => set({ logs: [] }),

      exportLogs: async () => {
        const { logs } = get();
        return new Blob([JSON.stringify(logs, null, 2)], { type: 'application/json' });
      },

      setLogLevel: (level) => set({ logLevel: level }),

      toggleCategory: (category) => {
        set((state) => {
          const cats = state.logCategories.includes(category)
            ? state.logCategories.filter(c => c !== category)
            : [...state.logCategories, category];
          return { logCategories: cats };
        });
      },

      addNotification: (notif) => {
        const id = uuidv4();
        set((state) => ({
          notifications: [{ ...notif, id, timestamp: Date.now(), read: false }, ...state.notifications],
          unreadCount: state.unreadCount + 1,
        }));
        // auto-dismiss after 5 seconds
        setTimeout(() => {
          get().dismissNotification(id);
        }, 5000);
      },

      markNotificationRead: (id) => {
        set((state) => {
          const notif = state.notifications.find(n => n.id === id);
          if (notif && !notif.read) {
            return {
              notifications: state.notifications.map(n => n.id === id ? { ...n, read: true } : n),
              unreadCount: state.unreadCount - 1,
            };
          }
          return state;
        });
      },

      markAllRead: () => {
        set((state) => ({
          notifications: state.notifications.map(n => ({ ...n, read: true })),
          unreadCount: 0,
        }));
      },

      dismissNotification: (id) => {
        set((state) => {
          const notif = state.notifications.find(n => n.id === id);
          const newUnread = notif && !notif.read ? state.unreadCount - 1 : state.unreadCount;
          return {
            notifications: state.notifications.filter(n => n.id !== id),
            unreadCount: Math.max(0, newUnread),
          };
        });
      },

      startBackgroundChecks: () => {
        // Placeholder – implement periodic checks if needed
      },

      stopBackgroundChecks: () => {
        // Placeholder
      },
    }),
    { name: 'log-store' }
  )
);

// Selectors (required by other components)
export const useLogFilteredLogs = () => {
  const logs = useLogStore((s) => s.logs);
  const level = useLogStore((s) => s.logLevel);
  const categories = useLogStore((s) => s.logCategories);
  const levelOrder = { debug: 0, info: 1, warn: 2, error: 3 };
  return logs.filter(log => levelOrder[log.level] >= levelOrder[level] && categories.includes(log.category));
};
export const useLogIsLiveLogOpen = () => useLogStore((s) => s.isLiveLogOpen);
export const useLogNotifications = () => useLogStore((s) => s.notifications);
export const useLogUnreadCount = () => useLogStore((s) => s.unreadCount);

FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/prakash-app/src/stores/authStore.ts
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
import { create } from 'zustand';
import { immer } from 'zustand/middleware/immer';
import CryptoJS from 'crypto-js';
import { User, Session, ActionPassword, TokenExpiry } from '@/types/auth';
import { openDB } from 'idb';

const ADMIN_PASSWORD_HASH = '5e884898da28047151d0e56f8dc6292773603d0d6aabbdd62a11ef721d1542d8'; // "password"

interface AuthState {
  currentUser: User | null;
  currentSession: Session | null;
  isAuthenticated: boolean;
  users: User[];
  actionPasswords: ActionPassword[];
  tokenExpiries: TokenExpiry[];
  isAdminRoute: boolean;
}

interface AuthActions {
  // Auth
  login: (username: string, password: string) => Promise<boolean>;
  logout: () => Promise<void>;
  adminLogin: (password: string) => boolean;
  adminLogout: () => void;
  
  // Users
  createUser: (username: string, password: string, role?: 'admin' | 'user') => Promise<void>;
  updateUser: (userId: string, updates: Partial<User>) => Promise<void>;
  deleteUser: (userId: string) => Promise<void>;
  getUsers: () => User[];
  
  // Action passwords
  setActionPassword: (action: string, password: string, required: boolean) => void;
  verifyActionPassword: (action: string, password: string) => boolean;
  
  // Token expiry
  addTokenExpiry: (expiry: TokenExpiry) => void;
  removeTokenExpiry: (accountId: string) => void;
  checkTokenExpiries: () => TokenExpiry[];
  
  // Session
  getSessionLogs: () => LogEntry[];
  exportSession: () => Promise<Blob>;
  
  // Admin check
  checkIsAdmin: () => boolean;
}

const hashPassword = (password: string): string => {
  return CryptoJS.SHA256(password).toString();
};

const DB_NAME = 'auth-db';
const DB_VERSION = 1;

export const useAuthStore = create<AuthState & AuthActions>()(
  immer((set, get) => ({
    // State
    currentUser: null,
    currentSession: null,
    isAuthenticated: false,
    users: [],
    actionPasswords: [],
    tokenExpiries: [],
    isAdminRoute: false,

    // Auth
    login: async (username, password) => {
      const db = await openDB(DB_NAME, DB_VERSION);
      const user = await db.get('users', username);
      
      if (!user || !user.isActive) return false;
      
      const passwordHash = hashPassword(password);
      if (user.passwordHash !== passwordHash) return false;
      
      // Create session
      const session: Session = {
        id: `session-${Date.now()}`,
        userId: user.id,
        username: user.username,
        startTime: new Date(),
        logs: [],
      };
      
      // Update last login
      user.lastLogin = new Date();
      await db.put('users', user);
      
      set((state) => {
        state.currentUser = user;
        state.currentSession = session;
        state.isAuthenticated = true;
      });
      
      return true;
    },

    logout: async () => {
      const { currentSession, currentUser } = get();
      
      if (currentSession && currentUser) {
        // Save session logs
        const db = await openDB(DB_NAME, DB_VERSION);
        currentSession.endTime = new Date();
        await db.add('sessions', currentSession);
      }
      
      set((state) => {
        state.currentUser = null;
        state.currentSession = null;
        state.isAuthenticated = false;
      });
    },

    adminLogin: (password) => {
      const hash = hashPassword(password);
      if (hash === ADMIN_PASSWORD_HASH) {
        set((state) => {
          state.isAdminRoute = true;
        });
        return true;
      }
      return false;
    },

    adminLogout: () => {
      set((state) => {
        state.isAdminRoute = false;
      });
    },

    // Users
    createUser: async (username, password, role = 'user') => {
      const db = await openDB(DB_NAME, DB_VERSION);
      
      const existing = await db.get('users', username);
      if (existing) throw new Error('Username already exists');
      
      const user: User = {
        id: `user-${Date.now()}`,
        username,
        passwordHash: hashPassword(password),
        role,
        createdAt: new Date(),
        isActive: true,
      };
      
      await db.put('users', user);
      
      set((state) => {
        state.users.push(user);
      });
    },

    updateUser: async (userId, updates) => {
      const db = await openDB(DB_NAME, DB_VERSION);
      const tx = db.transaction('users', 'readwrite');
      const store = tx.objectStore('users');
      
      const users = await store.getAll();
      const user = users.find(u => u.id === userId);
      if (!user) throw new Error('User not found');
      
      Object.assign(user, updates);
      if (updates.password) {
        user.passwordHash = hashPassword(updates.password);
      }
      
      await store.put(user);
      await tx.done;
    },

    deleteUser: async (userId) => {
      const db = await openDB(DB_NAME, DB_VERSION);
      const tx = db.transaction('users', 'readwrite');
      const store = tx.objectStore('users');
      
      const users = await store.getAll();
      const user = users.find(u => u.id === userId);
      if (user) {
        user.isActive = false;
        await store.put(user);
      }
      
      await tx.done;
    },

    getUsers: () => {
      return get().users;
    },

    // Action passwords
    setActionPassword: (action, password, required) => {
      set((state) => {
        const existing = state.actionPasswords.find(p => p.action === action);
        if (existing) {
          existing.passwordHash = hashPassword(password);
          existing.required = required;
        } else {
          state.actionPasswords.push({
            action: action as any,
            passwordHash: hashPassword(password),
            required,
          });
        }
      });
    },

    verifyActionPassword: (action, password) => {
      const { actionPasswords } = get();
      const config = actionPasswords.find(p => p.action === action);
      
      if (!config || !config.required) return true;
      
      return config.passwordHash === hashPassword(password);
    },

    // Token expiry
    addTokenExpiry: (expiry) => {
      set((state) => {
        const existing = state.tokenExpiries.find(e => e.accountId === expiry.accountId);
        if (existing) {
          Object.assign(existing, expiry);
        } else {
          state.tokenExpiries.push(expiry);
        }
      });
    },

    removeTokenExpiry: (accountId) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.tokenExpiries = state.tokenExpiries.filter(e => e.accountId !== accountId);
      });
    },

    checkTokenExpiries: () => {
      const now = new Date();
      const tenDaysFromNow = new Date(now.getTime() + 10 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000);
      
      return get().tokenExpiries.filter(e => {
        return e.expiresAt <= tenDaysFromNow && !e.warned;
      });
    },

    // Session
    getSessionLogs: () => {
      return get().currentSession?.logs || [];
    },

    exportSession: async () => {
      const { currentSession, currentUser } = get();
      if (!currentSession || !currentUser) throw new Error('No active session');
      
      const exportData = {
        session: currentSession,
        user: {
          id: currentUser.id,
          username: currentUser.username,
          role: currentUser.role,
        },
        exportedAt: new Date(),
      };
      
      return new Blob([JSON.stringify(exportData, null, 2)], { type: 'application/json' });
    },

    checkIsAdmin: () => {
      const { currentUser, isAdminRoute } = get();
      return isAdminRoute || currentUser?.role === 'admin';
    },
  }))
);

// Initialize DB
const initAuthDB = async () => {
  const db = await openDB(DB_NAME, DB_VERSION, {
    upgrade(db) {
      db.createObjectStore('users', { keyPath: 'username' });
      db.createObjectStore('sessions', { keyPath: 'id' });
      db.createObjectStore('logs', { keyPath: 'id' });
    },
  });
  
  // Create default admin if none exists
  const users = await db.getAll('users');
  if (users.length === 0) {
    await db.put('users', {
      id: 'admin-1',
      username: 'admin',
      passwordHash: ADMIN_PASSWORD_HASH,
      role: 'admin',
      createdAt: new Date(),
      isActive: true,
    });
  }
  
  return db;
};

initAuthDB();
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/prakash-app/src/stores/dfolStore.ts
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
import { create } from 'zustand';
import { immer } from 'zustand/middleware/immer';
import { DEFAULT_PROFILES, DFOLItem, DFOLMode, DFOLOperation, DFOLProfile, DFOLState } from '@/types/dfol';

interface DFOLStore extends DFOLState {
  enterDFOLMode: () => void;
  exitDFOLMode: () => void;
  selectItem: (item: DFOLItem, operations: DFOLMode[]) => void;
  deselectItem: (itemId: string) => void;
  clearSelection: () => void;
  setActiveProfile: (profileId: string) => void;
  addCustomProfile: (profile: DFOLProfile) => void;
  removeCustomProfile: (profileId: string) => void;
  openProfilePanel: () => void;
  closeProfilePanel: () => void;
  openExecutePanel: () => void;
  closeExecutePanel: () => void;
  executeOperations: () => Promise<void>;
  updateOperationStatus: (id: string, status: DFOLOperation['status'], progress?: number, message?: string) => void;
  completeOperation: (id: string, result: any) => void;
  failOperation: (id: string, error: string) => void;
  addNotification: (notif: any) => void;
  dismissNotification: (id: string) => void;
  getOperationStats: () => { total: number; pending: number; running: number; completed: number; failed: number };
}

const generateTimestamp = () => new Date().toISOString().replace(/[:.]/g, '-').slice(0, 19);

export const useDFOLStore = create<DFOLStore>()(
  immer((set, get) => ({
    isDFOLMode: false,
    selectedItems: [],
    operations: [],
    activeProfile: DEFAULT_PROFILES[0].id,
    customProfiles: [],
    outputDirectory: `/DFOL/${generateTimestamp()}`,
    isExecuting: false,
    showProfilePanel: false,
    showExecutePanel: false,
    globalProgress: 0,
    notifications: [],

    enterDFOLMode: () => set((state) => { state.isDFOLMode = true; state.selectedItems = []; state.operations = []; state.outputDirectory = `/DFOL/${generateTimestamp()}`; }),
    exitDFOLMode: () => set((state) => { state.isDFOLMode = false; state.selectedItems = []; state.showProfilePanel = false; state.showExecutePanel = false; if (!state.isExecuting) state.operations = []; }),
    selectItem: (item, operations) => set((state) => { const idx = state.selectedItems.findIndex(i => i.id === item.id); if (idx >= 0) state.selectedItems[idx].operations = operations; else state.selectedItems.push({ ...item, operations }); }),
    deselectItem: (itemId) => set((state) => { state.selectedItems = state.selectedItems.filter(i => i.id !== itemId); }),
    clearSelection: () => set((state) => { state.selectedItems = []; }),
    setActiveProfile: (profileId) => set((state) => { state.activeProfile = profileId; }),
    addCustomProfile: (profile) => set((state) => { state.customProfiles.push(profile); }),
    removeCustomProfile: (profileId) => set((state) => { state.customProfiles = state.customProfiles.filter(p => p.id !== profileId); }),
    openProfilePanel: () => set((state) => { state.showProfilePanel = true; }),
    closeProfilePanel: () => set((state) => { state.showProfilePanel = false; }),
    openExecutePanel: () => set((state) => { state.showExecutePanel = true; }),
    closeExecutePanel: () => set((state) => { state.showExecutePanel = false; }),
    executeOperations: async () => {
      const { selectedItems, outputDirectory } = get();
      const ops: DFOLOperation[] = [];
      selectedItems.forEach(item => {
        item.operations.forEach(mode => {
          ops.push({ id: `${item.id}-${mode}-${Date.now()}`, itemId: item.id, mode, status: 'pending', progress: 0, message: 'Waiting...' });
        });
      });
      set((state) => { state.operations = ops; state.isExecuting = true; state.showExecutePanel = true; });
      for (const op of ops) {
        get().updateOperationStatus(op.id, 'running', 0, 'Starting...');
        await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 500));
        get().completeOperation(op.id, { outputPath: `${outputDirectory}/${op.mode}_${op.itemId}`, size: 1024 });
      }
      set((state) => { state.isExecuting = false; state.globalProgress = 100; });
      get().addNotification({ type: 'success', message: `DFOL completed. Output: ${outputDirectory}`, autoDismiss: true });
    },
    updateOperationStatus: (id, status, progress, message) => set((state) => {
      const op = state.operations.find(o => o.id === id);
      if (op) { op.status = status; if (progress !== undefined) op.progress = progress; if (message) op.message = message; }
      const total = state.operations.length;
      const completed = state.operations.filter(o => o.status === 'completed').length;
      const runningProgress = state.operations.filter(o => o.status === 'running').reduce((sum, o) => sum + o.progress, 0) / (state.operations.filter(o => o.status === 'running').length || 1);
      state.globalProgress = ((completed + runningProgress / 100) / total) * 100;
    }),
    completeOperation: (id, result) => set((state) => { const op = state.operations.find(o => o.id === id); if (op) { op.status = 'completed'; op.progress = 100; op.message = 'Completed'; op.result = result; } }),
    failOperation: (id, error) => set((state) => { const op = state.operations.find(o => o.id === id); if (op) { op.status = 'failed'; op.message = 'Failed'; op.error = error; } get().addNotification({ type: 'error', message: error, operationId: id }); }),
    addNotification: (notif) => set((state) => { state.notifications.push({ ...notif, id: `notif-${Date.now()}`, timestamp: Date.now() }); if (notif.autoDismiss) setTimeout(() => get().dismissNotification(notif.id), 5000); }),
    dismissNotification: (id) => set((state) => { state.notifications = state.notifications.filter(n => n.id !== id); }),
    getOperationStats: () => {
      const ops = get().operations;
      return { total: ops.length, pending: ops.filter(o => o.status === 'pending').length, running: ops.filter(o => o.status === 'running').length, completed: ops.filter(o => o.status === 'completed').length, failed: ops.filter(o => o.status === 'failed').length };
    },
  }))
);

export const useIsDFOLMode = () => useDFOLStore((s) => s.isDFOLMode);
export const useDFOLSelectedItems = () => useDFOLStore((s) => s.selectedItems);
export const useDFOLOperations = () => useDFOLStore((s) => s.operations);
export const useDFOLGlobalProgress = () => useDFOLStore((s) => s.globalProgress);
export const useDFOLIsExecuting = () => useDFOLStore((s) => s.isExecuting);
export const useDFOLNotifications = () => useDFOLStore((s) => s.notifications);
export const useDFOLProfiles = () => useDFOLStore((s) => [...DEFAULT_PROFILES, ...s.customProfiles]);
export const useDFOLActiveProfile = () => useDFOLStore((s) => s.activeProfile);

FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/prakash-app/src/stores/dragDropStore.ts
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
import { create } from 'zustand';
import { immer } from 'zustand/middleware/immer';
import { DragDropState, DragDropActions, SelectedItem } from '@/types/dragDrop';

interface DragDropStore extends DragDropState, DragDropActions {}

export const useDragDropStore = create<DragDropStore>()(
  immer((set, get) => ({
    // State
    isDragging: false,
    isDragMode: false,
    selectedItems: [],
    dragSourcePanel: null,
    dragImagePosition: null,
    pendingOperation: null,
    targetPanel: null,
    showConfirmDialog: false,

    // Actions
    enterDragMode: (panelId) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.isDragMode = true;
        state.dragSourcePanel = panelId;
        state.selectedItems = [];
      });
    },

    exitDragMode: () => {
      set((state) => {
        state.isDragMode = false;
        state.isDragging = false;
        state.selectedItems = [];
        state.dragSourcePanel = null;
        state.dragImagePosition = null;
        state.pendingOperation = null;
        state.targetPanel = null;
        state.showConfirmDialog = false;
      });
    },

    toggleSelection: (item) => {
      set((state) => {
        const existingIndex = state.selectedItems.findIndex(
          (i) => i.id === item.id && i.panelId === item.panelId
        );
        
        if (existingIndex >= 0) {
          state.selectedItems.splice(existingIndex, 1);
        } else {
          state.selectedItems.push(item);
        }
      });
    },

    clearSelection: () => {
      set((state) => {
        state.selectedItems = [];
      });
    },

    selectAll: (items) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.selectedItems = items;
      });
    },

    startDrag: (panelId, position) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.isDragging = true;
        state.dragSourcePanel = panelId;
        state.dragImagePosition = position;
      });
    },

    endDrag: () => {
      set((state) => {
        state.isDragging = false;
        state.dragImagePosition = null;
      });
    },

    setDragImagePosition: (position) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.dragImagePosition = position;
      });
    },

    setTargetPanel: (panelId) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.targetPanel = panelId;
      });
    },

    showConfirm: (operation) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.pendingOperation = operation;
        state.showConfirmDialog = true;
      });
    },

    hideConfirm: () => {
      set((state) => {
        state.showConfirmDialog = false;
        state.pendingOperation = null;
      });
    },

    confirmOperation: () => {
      // This will be handled by the panel that receives the drop
      set((state) => {
        state.showConfirmDialog = false;
      });
    },

    cancelOperation: () => {
      set((state) => {
        state.isDragging = false;
        state.pendingOperation = null;
        state.targetPanel = null;
        state.showConfirmDialog = false;
        state.dragImagePosition = null;
      });
    },
  }))
);

// Selectors
export const useIsDragMode = () => useDragDropStore((s) => s.isDragMode);
export const useIsDragging = () => useDragDropStore((s) => s.isDragging);
export const useSelectedItems = () => useDragDropStore((s) => s.selectedItems);
export const useDragSourcePanel = () => useDragDropStore((s) => s.dragSourcePanel);
export const useDragImagePosition = () => useDragDropStore((s) => s.dragImagePosition);
export const usePendingOperation = () => useDragDropStore((s) => s.pendingOperation);
export const useTargetPanel = () => useDragDropStore((s) => s.targetPanel);
export const useShowConfirmDialog = () => useDragDropStore((s) => s.showConfirmDialog);

FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/prakash-app/src/stores/driveStore.ts
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
import { create } from 'zustand';
import { immer } from 'zustand/middleware/immer';
import { 
  GoogleAccount, 
  DriveFile, 
  DriveFolder,
  DriveViewMode,
  DriveSortBy,
  DrivePanelState 
} from '@/types/drive';
import { driveApi } from '@/lib/googleDriveApi';

interface DriveStore extends DrivePanelState {
  // Actions
  addAccount: (account: GoogleAccount) => void;
  removeAccount: (id: string) => void;
  setActiveAccount: (id: string | null) => void;
  setCurrentFolder: (folderId: string, folderName?: string) => Promise<void>;
  navigateToFolder: (file: DriveFile) => Promise<void>;
  navigateBack: () => Promise<void>;
  navigateToRoot: () => void;
  setViewMode: (mode: DriveViewMode) => void;
  setSortBy: (sort: DriveSortBy) => void;
  refreshCurrent: () => Promise<void>;
  logout: () => void;
  
  // Getters
  getActiveAccount: () => GoogleAccount | undefined;
  getSortedFiles: () => DriveFile[];
  getCurrentFolderName: () => string;
}

const createInitialState = (): DrivePanelState => ({
  accounts: [],
  activeAccountId: null,
  currentFolderId: 'root',
  currentPath: [],
  files: [],
  viewMode: 'list',
  sortBy: 'name-asc',
  isLoading: false,
  error: null,
});

export const useDriveStore = create<DriveStore>()(
  immer((set, get) => ({
    ...createInitialState(),

    addAccount: (account) => {
      set((state) => {
        // Check if account already exists
        const existingIndex = state.accounts.findIndex(a => a.id === account.id);
        if (existingIndex >= 0) {
          // Update existing account with new token
          state.accounts[existingIndex] = account;
        } else {
          state.accounts.push(account);
        }
        // Set as active if no active account
        if (!state.activeAccountId) {
          state.activeAccountId = account.id;
        }
      });
      // Load root files for new account
      get().setCurrentFolder('root', 'My Drive');
    },

    removeAccount: (id) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.accounts = state.accounts.filter(a => a.id !== id);
        if (state.activeAccountId === id) {
          state.activeAccountId = state.accounts[0]?.id || null;
        }
      });
    },

    setActiveAccount: (id) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.activeAccountId = id;
        state.currentFolderId = 'root';
        state.currentPath = [];
        state.files = [];
      });
      if (id) {
        get().setCurrentFolder('root', 'My Drive');
      }
    },

    setCurrentFolder: async (folderId, folderName) => {
      const { activeAccountId, accounts } = get();
      if (!activeAccountId) return;

      const account = accounts.find(a => a.id === activeAccountId);
      if (!account) return;

      set((state) => {
        state.isLoading = true;
        state.error = null;
      });

      try {
        const files = await driveApi.listFiles(account, folderId);
        set((state) => {
          state.currentFolderId = folderId;
          state.files = files;
          state.isLoading = false;
        });
      } catch (err) {
        set((state) => {
          state.error = (err as Error).message;
          state.isLoading = false;
        });
      }
    },

    navigateToFolder: async (file) => {
      if (!driveApi.isFolder(file)) return;
      
      const { currentPath } = get();
      
      set((state) => {
        state.currentPath.push({ id: state.currentFolderId, name: state.currentPath.length === 0 ? 'My Drive' : file.name });
      });
      
      await get().setCurrentFolder(file.id, file.name);
    },

    navigateBack: async () => {
      const { currentPath } = get();
      if (currentPath.length === 0) return;

      const parent = currentPath[currentPath.length - 1];
      set((state) => {
        state.currentPath.pop();
      });
      
      await get().setCurrentFolder(parent.id, parent.name);
    },

    navigateToRoot: () => {
      set((state) => {
        state.currentFolderId = 'root';
        state.currentPath = [];
      });
      get().setCurrentFolder('root', 'My Drive');
    },

    setViewMode: (mode) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.viewMode = mode;
      });
    },

    setSortBy: (sort) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.sortBy = sort;
      });
    },

    refreshCurrent: async () => {
      const { currentFolderId } = get();
      await get().setCurrentFolder(currentFolderId);
    },

    logout: () => {
      set(createInitialState());
    },

    getActiveAccount: () => {
      const { accounts, activeAccountId } = get();
      return accounts.find(a => a.id === activeAccountId);
    },

    getSortedFiles: () => {
      const { files, sortBy } = get();
      const sorted = [...files];
      
      switch (sortBy) {
        case 'name-asc':
          return sorted.sort((a, b) => a.name.localeCompare(b.name));
        case 'name-desc':
          return sorted.sort((a, b) => b.name.localeCompare(a.name));
        case 'modifiedTime':
          return sorted.sort((a, b) => new Date(b.modifiedTime).getTime() - new Date(a.modifiedTime).getTime());
        case 'size':
          return sorted.sort((a, b) => {
            const sizeA = parseInt(a.size || '0', 10);
            const sizeB = parseInt(b.size || '0', 10);
            return sizeB - sizeA;
          });
        default:
          return sorted;
      }
    },

    getCurrentFolderName: () => {
      const { currentPath, currentFolderId } = get();
      if (currentFolderId === 'root') return 'My Drive';
      const current = currentPath[currentPath.length - 1];
      return current?.name || 'My Drive';
    },
  }))
);

// Selectors
export const useDriveAccounts = () => useDriveStore((s) => s.accounts);
export const useDriveActiveAccount = () => useDriveStore((s) => s.getActiveAccount());
export const useDriveFiles = () => useDriveStore((s) => s.getSortedFiles());
export const useDriveViewMode = () => useDriveStore((s) => s.viewMode);
export const useDriveSortBy = () => useDriveStore((s) => s.sortBy);
export const useDriveCurrentPath = () => useDriveStore((s) => s.currentPath);
export const useDriveIsLoading = () => useDriveStore((s) => s.isLoading);
export const useDriveError = () => useDriveStore((s) => s.error);
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/prakash-app/src/stores/fileSystemStore.ts
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
import { create } from 'zustand';
import { 
  FileSystemEntry, 
  FileSystemDirectoryEntry,
  ViewMode, 
  SortBy,
  MountPoint 
} from '@/types/filesystem';
import { fileSystemBackend } from '@/lib/fileSystemBackend';

interface NavigationHistory {
  handle: FileSystemDirectoryHandle;
  name: string;
}

interface FileSystemState {
  // Current state
  currentPath: string;
  currentHandle: FileSystemDirectoryHandle | null;
  entries: FileSystemEntry[];
  viewMode: ViewMode;
  sortBy: SortBy;
  isLoading: boolean;
  error: string | null;
  
  // History for back navigation
  history: NavigationHistory[];
  
  // Mount points (fake root)
  mountPoints: MountPoint[];
  
  // Actions
  setViewMode: (mode: ViewMode) => void;
  setSortBy: (sort: SortBy) => void;
  pickDirectory: () => Promise<void>;
  navigateTo: (entry: FileSystemDirectoryEntry) => Promise<void>;
  navigateBack: () => Promise<void>;
  navigateToRoot: () => void;
  refreshCurrent: () => Promise<void>;
  createFolder: (name: string) => Promise<void>;
  initMountPoints: () => void;
  selectMountPoint: (mountId: string) => Promise<void>;
  
  // Computed
  getSortedEntries: () => FileSystemEntry[];
}

const createFakeMountPoints = (): MountPoint[] => [
  {
    id: 'internal',
    name: 'Internal Storage',
    icon: 'hard-drive',
    handle: null,
    isFake: true,
  },
  {
    id: 'sd-card',
    name: 'SD Card',
    icon: 'sd-card',
    handle: null,
    isFake: true,
  },
];

export const useFileSystemStore = create<FileSystemState>((set, get) => ({
  currentPath: '/',
  currentHandle: null,
  entries: [],
  viewMode: 'list',
  sortBy: 'name-asc',
  isLoading: false,
  error: null,
  history: [],
  mountPoints: createFakeMountPoints(),

  setViewMode: (mode) => set({ viewMode: mode }),
  
  setSortBy: (sort) => set({ sortBy: sort }),

  pickDirectory: async () => {
    set({ isLoading: true, error: null });
    try {
      const handle = await fileSystemBackend.pickDirectory();
      if (handle) {
        const entries = await fileSystemBackend.readDirectory(handle);
        set({ 
          currentHandle: handle,
          currentPath: `/${handle.name}`,
          entries,
          history: [],
          isLoading: false 
        });
      } else {
        set({ isLoading: false });
      }
    } catch (err) {
      set({ error: (err as Error).message, isLoading: false });
    }
  },

  navigateTo: async (entry) => {
    const { currentHandle, history, currentPath } = get();
    if (!currentHandle || entry.kind !== 'directory') return;

    set({ isLoading: true, error: null });
    try {
      const newEntries = await fileSystemBackend.readDirectory(entry.handle as FileSystemDirectoryHandle);
      set({
        currentHandle: entry.handle as FileSystemDirectoryHandle,
        currentPath: `${currentPath}/${entry.name}`,
        entries: newEntries,
        history: [...history, { handle: currentHandle, name: currentPath.split('/').pop() || 'root' }],
        isLoading: false,
      });
    } catch (err) {
      set({ error: (err as Error).message, isLoading: false });
    }
  },

  navigateBack: async () => {
    const { history } = get();
    if (history.length === 0) {
      get().navigateToRoot();
      return;
    }

    const previous = history[history.length - 1];
    set({ isLoading: true, error: null });
    
    try {
      const entries = await fileSystemBackend.readDirectory(previous.handle);
      set({
        currentHandle: previous.handle,
        currentPath: history.length === 1 ? '/' : `/${previous.name}`,
        entries,
        history: history.slice(0, -1),
        isLoading: false,
      });
    } catch (err) {
      set({ error: (err as Error).message, isLoading: false });
    }
  },

  navigateToRoot: () => {
    set({
      currentPath: '/',
      currentHandle: null,
      entries: [],
      history: [],
    });
  },

  refreshCurrent: async () => {
    const { currentHandle } = get();
    if (!currentHandle) return;

    set({ isLoading: true, error: null });
    try {
      const entries = await fileSystemBackend.readDirectory(currentHandle);
      set({ entries, isLoading: false });
    } catch (err) {
      set({ error: (err as Error).message, isLoading: false });
    }
  },

  createFolder: async (name) => {
    const { currentHandle } = get();
    if (!currentHandle) return;

    set({ isLoading: true, error: null });
    try {
      await fileSystemBackend.createDirectory(currentHandle, name);
      await get().refreshCurrent();
    } catch (err) {
      set({ error: (err as Error).message, isLoading: false });
    }
  },

  initMountPoints: () => {
    set({ mountPoints: createFakeMountPoints() });
  },

  selectMountPoint: async (mountId) => {
    const { mountPoints } = get();
    const mount = mountPoints.find(m => m.id === mountId);
    
    if (!mount) return;
    
    // If mount has no handle yet, open picker
    if (!mount.handle) {
      const handle = await fileSystemBackend.pickDirectory();
      if (handle) {
        // Update mount point with handle
        const updatedMounts = mountPoints.map(m => 
          m.id === mountId ? { ...m, handle, isFake: false } : m
        );
        const entries = await fileSystemBackend.readDirectory(handle);
        set({
          mountPoints: updatedMounts,
          currentHandle: handle,
          currentPath: `/${mount.name}`,
          entries,
          history: [],
        });
      }
    } else {
      // Use existing handle
      const entries = await fileSystemBackend.readDirectory(mount.handle);
      set({
        currentHandle: mount.handle,
        currentPath: `/${mount.name}`,
        entries,
        history: [],
      });
    }
  },

  getSortedEntries: () => {
    const { entries, sortBy } = get();
    const sorted = [...entries];
    
    switch (sortBy) {
      case 'name-asc':
        return sorted.sort((a, b) => a.name.localeCompare(b.name));
      case 'name-desc':
        return sorted.sort((a, b) => b.name.localeCompare(a.name));
      case 'date':
        return sorted.sort((a, b) => b.lastModified.getTime() - a.lastModified.getTime());
      case 'size':
        return sorted.sort((a, b) => b.size - a.size);
      default:
        return sorted;
    }
  },
}));

// Selectors
export const useCurrentPath = () => useFileSystemStore((s) => s.currentPath);
export const useCurrentHandle = () => useFileSystemStore((s) => s.currentHandle);
export const useEntries = () => useFileSystemStore((s) => s.getSortedEntries());
export const useViewMode = () => useFileSystemStore((s) => s.viewMode);
export const useSortBy = () => useFileSystemStore((s) => s.sortBy);
export const useIsLoading = () => useFileSystemStore((s) => s.isLoading);
export const useHistory = () => useFileSystemStore((s) => s.history);
export const useMountPoints = () => useFileSystemStore((s) => s.mountPoints);
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/prakash-app/src/stores/githubStore.ts
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
import { create } from 'zustand';
import { immer } from 'zustand/middleware/immer';
import { 
  GitHubAccount, 
  GitHubRepository, 
  GitHubContent,
  GitHubViewMode,
  GitHubSortBy,
  GitHubPanelState,
  GitHubPermission 
} from '@/types/github';
import { githubApi } from '@/lib/githubApi';
import { githubStorage } from '@/lib/githubStorage';

interface GitHubStore extends GitHubPanelState {
  // Actions
  loadAccounts: () => Promise<void>;
  addAccount: (username: string, token: string) => Promise<void>;
  removeAccount: (id: string) => Promise<void>;
  setActiveAccount: (id: string | null) => void;
  loadRepositories: () => Promise<void>;
  selectRepository: (repo: GitHubRepository) => Promise<void>;
  navigateToPath: (path: string) => Promise<void>;
  navigateBack: () => Promise<void>;
  navigateToRoot: () => void;
  openFile: (file: GitHubContent) => Promise<void>;
  closeFile: () => void;
  setViewMode: (mode: GitHubViewMode) => void;
  setSortBy: (sort: GitHubSortBy) => void;
  refreshCurrent: () => Promise<void>;
  logout: () => void;
  
  // Getters
  getActiveAccount: () => GitHubAccount | undefined;
  getSortedRepositories: () => GitHubRepository[];
  getSortedContents: () => GitHubContent[];
  getCurrentBreadcrumb: () => string[];
  canGoBack: () => boolean;
}

const createInitialState = (): GitHubPanelState => ({
  accounts: [],
  activeAccountId: null,
  currentRepository: null,
  currentPath: '',
  pathHistory: [],
  repositories: [],
  contents: [],
  viewMode: 'list',
  sortBy: 'updated',
  isLoading: false,
  error: null,
  fileContent: null,
  fileName: null,
});

export const useGitHubStore = create<GitHubStore>()(
  immer((set, get) => ({
    ...createInitialState(),

    loadAccounts: async () => {
      const accounts = await githubStorage.getAllAccounts();
      set((state) => {
        state.accounts = accounts;
      });
    },

    addAccount: async (username, token) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.isLoading = true;
        state.error = null;
      });

      try {
        // Validate token and get user info
        const userInfo = await githubApi.authenticate(token);
        
        // Check if account already exists
        const existing = get().accounts.find(a => a.id === userInfo.username);
        if (existing) {
          throw new Error('Account already exists');
        }

        const account: GitHubAccount = {
          id: userInfo.username,
          token,
          avatarUrl: userInfo.avatarUrl,
          permissions: 'read', // Will be updated based on token scopes
          addedAt: Date.now(),
        };

        // Save to encrypted storage
        await githubStorage.saveAccount(account);

        set((state) => {
          state.accounts.push(account);
          state.activeAccountId = account.id;
          state.isLoading = false;
        });

        // Load repositories for new account
        await get().loadRepositories();
      } catch (err) {
        set((state) => {
          state.error = (err as Error).message;
          state.isLoading = false;
        });
        throw err;
      }
    },

    removeAccount: async (id) => {
      await githubStorage.deleteAccount(id);
      set((state) => {
        state.accounts = state.accounts.filter(a => a.id !== id);
        if (state.activeAccountId === id) {
          state.activeAccountId = null;
          state.currentRepository = null;
          state.currentPath = '';
          state.pathHistory = [];
          state.repositories = [];
          state.contents = [];
        }
      });
    },

    setActiveAccount: (id) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.activeAccountId = id;
        state.currentRepository = null;
        state.currentPath = '';
        state.pathHistory = [];
        state.contents = [];
        state.fileContent = null;
        state.fileName = null;
      });
      
      if (id) {
        get().loadRepositories();
      }
    },

    loadRepositories: async () => {
      const { activeAccountId, accounts } = get();
      if (!activeAccountId) return;

      const account = accounts.find(a => a.id === activeAccountId);
      if (!account) return;

      set((state) => {
        state.isLoading = true;
        state.error = null;
      });

      try {
        githubApi.setToken(account.token);
        const repos = await githubApi.listRepositories(account.id);
        set((state) => {
          state.repositories = repos;
          state.isLoading = false;
        });
      } catch (err) {
        set((state) => {
          state.error = (err as Error).message;
          state.isLoading = false;
        });
      }
    },

    selectRepository: async (repo) => {
      const { activeAccountId, accounts } = get();
      if (!activeAccountId) return;

      const account = accounts.find(a => a.id === activeAccountId);
      if (!account) return;

      set((state) => {
        state.isLoading = true;
        state.error = null;
        state.currentRepository = repo.name;
        state.currentPath = '';
        state.pathHistory = [];
        state.fileContent = null;
        state.fileName = null;
      });

      try {
        githubApi.setToken(account.token);
        const contents = await githubApi.getRepositoryContents(account.id, repo.name, '');
        set((state) => {
          state.contents = contents;
          state.isLoading = false;
        });
      } catch (err) {
        set((state) => {
          state.error = (err as Error).message;
          state.isLoading = false;
        });
      }
    },

    navigateToPath: async (path) => {
      const { activeAccountId, accounts, currentRepository, currentPath } = get();
      if (!activeAccountId || !currentRepository) return;

      const account = accounts.find(a => a.id === activeAccountId);
      if (!account) return;

      set((state) => {
        state.isLoading = true;
        state.error = null;
        state.pathHistory.push(currentPath);
        state.currentPath = path;
        state.fileContent = null;
        state.fileName = null;
      });

      try {
        githubApi.setToken(account.token);
        const contents = await githubApi.getRepositoryContents(account.id, currentRepository, path);
        set((state) => {
          state.contents = contents;
          state.isLoading = false;
        });
      } catch (err) {
        set((state) => {
          state.error = (err as Error).message;
          state.isLoading = false;
        });
      }
    },

    navigateBack: async () => {
      const { pathHistory, activeAccountId, accounts, currentRepository } = get();
      if (pathHistory.length === 0 || !activeAccountId || !currentRepository) {
        // Go back to repository root
        set((state) => {
          state.currentPath = '';
          state.pathHistory = [];
          state.fileContent = null;
          state.fileName = null;
        });
        await get().refreshCurrent();
        return;
      }

      const account = accounts.find(a => a.id === activeAccountId);
      if (!account) return;

      const previousPath = pathHistory[pathHistory.length - 1];

      set((state) => {
        state.isLoading = true;
        state.error = null;
        state.pathHistory.pop();
        state.currentPath = previousPath;
        state.fileContent = null;
        state.fileName = null;
      });

      try {
        githubApi.setToken(account.token);
        const contents = await githubApi.getRepositoryContents(account.id, currentRepository, previousPath);
        set((state) => {
          state.contents = contents;
          state.isLoading = false;
        });
      } catch (err) {
        set((state) => {
          state.error = (err as Error).message;
          state.isLoading = false;
        });
      }
    },

    navigateToRoot: () => {
      set((state) => {
        state.currentRepository = null;
        state.currentPath = '';
        state.pathHistory = [];
        state.contents = [];
        state.fileContent = null;
        state.fileName = null;
      });
    },

    openFile: async (file) => {
      const { activeAccountId, accounts, currentRepository } = get();
      if (!activeAccountId || !currentRepository || file.type !== 'file') return;

      const account = accounts.find(a => a.id === activeAccountId);
      if (!account) return;

      set((state) => {
        state.isLoading = true;
        state.error = null;
      });

      try {
        githubApi.setToken(account.token);
        const fileData = await githubApi.getFileContent(account.id, currentRepository, file.path);
        set((state) => {
          state.fileContent = fileData.content;
          state.fileName = fileData.name;
          state.isLoading = false;
        });
      } catch (err) {
        set((state) => {
          state.error = (err as Error).message;
          state.isLoading = false;
        });
      }
    },

    closeFile: () => {
      set((state) => {
        state.fileContent = null;
        state.fileName = null;
      });
    },

    setViewMode: (mode) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.viewMode = mode;
      });
    },

    setSortBy: (sort) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.sortBy = sort;
      });
    },

    refreshCurrent: async () => {
      const { currentRepository, currentPath, activeAccountId, accounts } = get();
      if (!activeAccountId || !currentRepository) {
        await get().loadRepositories();
        return;
      }

      const account = accounts.find(a => a.id === activeAccountId);
      if (!account) return;

      set((state) => {
        state.isLoading = true;
        state.error = null;
      });

      try {
        githubApi.setToken(account.token);
        const contents = await githubApi.getRepositoryContents(account.id, currentRepository, currentPath);
        set((state) => {
          state.contents = contents;
          state.isLoading = false;
        });
      } catch (err) {
        set((state) => {
          state.error = (err as Error).message;
          state.isLoading = false;
        });
      }
    },

    logout: () => {
      set(createInitialState());
    },

    getActiveAccount: () => {
      const { accounts, activeAccountId } = get();
      return accounts.find(a => a.id === activeAccountId);
    },

    getSortedRepositories: () => {
      const { repositories, sortBy } = get();
      const sorted = [...repositories];
      
      switch (sortBy) {
        case 'name-asc':
          return sorted.sort((a, b) => a.name.localeCompare(b.name));
        case 'name-desc':
          return sorted.sort((a, b) => b.name.localeCompare(a.name));
        case 'updated':
          return sorted.sort((a, b) => new Date(b.pushed_at).getTime() - new Date(a.pushed_at).getTime());
        case 'stars':
          return sorted.sort((a, b) => b.stargazers_count - a.stargazers_count);
        default:
          return sorted;
      }
    },

    getSortedContents: () => {
      const { contents, sortBy } = get();
      const sorted = [...contents];
      
      // Always show folders first, then files
      const folders = sorted.filter(c => c.type === 'dir');
      const files = sorted.filter(c => c.type === 'file');
      
      const sortFn = (a: GitHubContent, b: GitHubContent) => {
        switch (sortBy) {
          case 'name-asc':
            return a.name.localeCompare(b.name);
          case 'name-desc':
            return b.name.localeCompare(a.name);
          case 'size':
            return (b.size || 0) - (a.size || 0);
          default:
            return a.name.localeCompare(b.name);
        }
      };
      
      return [...folders.sort(sortFn), ...files.sort(sortFn)];
    },

    getCurrentBreadcrumb: () => {
      const { currentPath } = get();
      if (!currentPath) return [];
      return currentPath.split('/').filter(Boolean);
    },

    canGoBack: () => {
      const { currentRepository, currentPath } = get();
      return !!currentRepository && (currentPath !== '' || true); // Can always go back to repo list
    },
  }))
);

// Selectors
export const useGitHubAccounts = () => useGitHubStore((s) => s.accounts);
export const useGitHubActiveAccount = () => useGitHubStore((s) => s.getActiveAccount());
export const useGitHubRepositories = () => useGitHubStore((s) => s.getSortedRepositories());
export const useGitHubContents = () => useGitHubStore((s) => s.getSortedContents());
export const useGitHubViewMode = () => useGitHubStore((s) => s.viewMode);
export const useGitHubSortBy = () => useGitHubStore((s) => s.sortBy);
export const useGitHubCurrentRepo = () => useGitHubStore((s) => s.currentRepository);
export const useGitHubFileContent = () => useGitHubStore((s) => s.fileContent);
export const useGitHubFileName = () => useGitHubStore((s) => s.fileName);
export const useGitHubIsLoading = () => useGitHubStore((s) => s.isLoading);
export const useGitHubError = () => useGitHubStore((s) => s.error);
