import { create } from 'zustand';
import { immer } from 'zustand/middleware/immer';
import { 
  PanelState, 
  PanelLayout, 
  createDefaultPanel,
  MIN_PANEL_WIDTH,
  MAX_PANELS 
} from '@/types/panel';
import { SourceType } from './appStore';
import { ViewMode, SortBy } from '@/types/filesystem';
import { fileSystemBackend } from '@/lib/fileSystemBackend';

interface PanelStore extends PanelLayout {
  // Actions
  addPanel: () => void;
  removePanel: (id: string) => void;
  setActivePanel: (id: string) => void;
  
  // Panel-specific actions
  setPanelSource: (id: string, source: SourceType) => void;
  setPanelPath: (id: string, path: string) => void;
  setPanelHandle: (id: string, handle: FileSystemDirectoryHandle | null) => void;
  navigatePanelForward: (id: string, handle: FileSystemDirectoryHandle, name: string) => void;
  navigatePanelBack: (id: string) => void;
  setPanelViewMode: (id: string, mode: ViewMode) => void;
  setPanelSortBy: (id: string, sort: SortBy) => void;
  setPanelWidth: (id: string, width: number) => void;
  togglePanelMinimize: (id: string) => void;
  
  // Storage operations
  pickDirectoryForPanel: (id: string) => Promise<void>;
  refreshPanelDirectory: (id: string) => Promise<void>;
  
  // Getters
  getPanel: (id: string) => PanelState | undefined;
  getPanelEntries: (id: string) => Promise<FileSystemEntry[]>;
}

import { FileSystemEntry } from '@/types/filesystem';

export const usePanelStore = create<PanelStore>()(
  immer((set, get) => ({
    panels: [
      createDefaultPanel('panel-1', 0),
      createDefaultPanel('panel-2', 1),
    ],
    activePanelId: 'panel-1',

    addPanel: () => {
      const { panels } = get();
      if (panels.length >= MAX_PANELS) return;
      
      const newId = `panel-${panels.length + 1}`;
      set((state) => {
        state.panels.push(createDefaultPanel(newId, panels.length));
        state.activePanelId = newId;
      });
    },

    removePanel: (id) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.panels = state.panels.filter((p) => p.id !== id);
        if (state.activePanelId === id) {
          state.activePanelId = state.panels[0]?.id || null;
        }
      });
    },

    setActivePanel: (id) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.activePanelId = id;
      });
    },

    setPanelSource: (id, source) => {
      set((state) => {
        const panel = state.panels.find((p) => p.id === id);
        if (panel) {
          panel.source = source;
          // Reset path-specific state when source changes
          panel.path = '/';
          panel.handle = null;
          panel.history = [];
        }
      });
    },

    setPanelPath: (id, path) => {
      set((state) => {
        const panel = state.panels.find((p) => p.id === id);
        if (panel) panel.path = path;
      });
    },

    setPanelHandle: (id, handle) => {
      set((state) => {
        const panel = state.panels.find((p) => p.id === id);
        if (panel) panel.handle = handle;
      });
    },

    navigatePanelForward: (id, handle, name) => {
      set((state) => {
        const panel = state.panels.find((p) => p.id === id);
        if (panel && panel.handle) {
          panel.history.push({ handle: panel.handle, name: panel.path.split('/').pop() || 'root' });
          panel.handle = handle;
          panel.path = `${panel.path}/${name}`.replace('//', '/');
        }
      });
    },

    navigatePanelBack: (id) => {
      set((state) => {
        const panel = state.panels.find((p) => p.id === id);
        if (panel && panel.history.length > 0) {
          const previous = panel.history.pop()!;
          panel.handle = previous.handle;
          panel.path = panel.history.length === 0 ? '/' : `/${previous.name}`;
        }
      });
    },

    setPanelViewMode: (id, mode) => {
      set((state) => {
        const panel = state.panels.find((p) => p.id === id);
        if (panel) panel.viewMode = mode;
      });
    },

    setPanelSortBy: (id, sort) => {
      set((state) => {
        const panel = state.panels.find((p) => p.id === id);
        if (panel) panel.sortBy = sort;
      });
    },

    setPanelWidth: (id, width) => {
      set((state) => {
        const panel = state.panels.find((p) => p.id === id);
        if (panel) {
          panel.width = Math.max(MIN_PANEL_WIDTH, width);
        }
      });
    },

    togglePanelMinimize: (id) => {
      set((state) => {
        const panel = state.panels.find((p) => p.id === id);
        if (panel) panel.isMinimized = !panel.isMinimized;
      });
    },

    pickDirectoryForPanel: async (id) => {
      const handle = await fileSystemBackend.pickDirectory();
      if (handle) {
        set((state) => {
          const panel = state.panels.find((p) => p.id === id);
          if (panel) {
            panel.handle = handle;
            panel.path = `/${handle.name}`;
            panel.history = [];
          }
        });
      }
    },

    refreshPanelDirectory: async (id) => {
      // Trigger re-render by updating a timestamp or similar
      // Actual refresh happens in component via useEffect
    },

    getPanel: (id) => {
      return get().panels.find((p) => p.id === id);
    },

    getPanelEntries: async (id) => {
      const panel = get().getPanel(id);
      if (!panel?.handle) return [];
      return fileSystemBackend.readDirectory(panel.handle);
    },
  }))
);

// Selectors
export const usePanels = () => usePanelStore((s) => s.panels);
export const useActivePanelId = () => usePanelStore((s) => s.activePanelId);
export const usePanel = (id: string) => usePanelStore((s) => s.getPanel(id));
export const usePanelCount = () => usePanelStore((s) => s.panels.length);

FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/prakash-app/src/stores/promptStore.ts
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
import { create } from 'zustand';
import { immer } from 'zustand/middleware/immer';
import { v4 as uuidv4 } from 'uuid';
import { PromptSession, PromptNote, PromptFile, PromptFolder, PromptManagerState } from '@/types/prompt';
import { openDB } from 'idb';

interface PromptStore extends PromptManagerState {
  // Session management
  createSession: (name: string) => PromptSession;
  loadSession: (id: string) => void;
  saveSession: () => Promise<void>;
  deleteSession: (id: string) => Promise<void>;
  duplicateSession: (id: string) => PromptSession;
  renameSession: (id: string, newName: string) => void;
  
  // Prompt operations
  updatePromptText: (text: string) => void;
  
  // Note operations
  addNote: (title: string, content: string) => void;
  updateNote: (id: string, updates: Partial<PromptNote>) => void;
  deleteNote: (id: string) => void;
  toggleNoteAttachment: (id: string) => void;
  
  // File operations
  addFile: (file: Omit<PromptFile, 'id'>, folderPath?: string) => void;
  moveFile: (fileId: string, newFolderPath: string) => void;
  renameFile: (fileId: string, newName: string) => void;
  deleteFile: (fileId: string) => void;
  createFolder: (name: string, parentPath: string) => void;
  renameFolder: (folderId: string, newName: string) => void;
  deleteFolder: (folderId: string) => void;
  compressFile: (fileId: string, profileId: string) => void;
  
  // Drag-drop from main app
  addDragDropFile: (fileData: any, sourcePanelId: string) => void;
  
  // Upload
  completeAndUpload: () => Promise<{ shareLink: string }>;
  setUploadProvider: (provider: 'drive' | 'github') => void;
  
  // UI
  openPromptManager: () => void;
  closePromptManager: () => void;
  togglePromptManager: () => void;
  
  // Getters
  getSessionFiles: () => PromptFile[];
  getFolderStructure: () => PromptFolder;
  getTotalSize: () => number;
  getAttachedNotes: () => PromptNote[];
}

const DB_NAME = 'prompt-manager-db';
const DB_VERSION = 1;

const createDefaultFolder = (): PromptFolder => ({
  id: 'root',
  name: 'root',
  path: '/',
  children: [],
});

const createEmptySession = (name: string): PromptSession => ({
  id: `session-${uuidv4()}`,
  name,
  createdAt: new Date(),
  updatedAt: new Date(),
  promptText: '',
  notes: [],
  files: [],
  folderStructure: createDefaultFolder(),
  isCompleted: false,
});

export const usePromptStore = create<PromptStore>()(
  immer((set, get) => ({
    // State
    sessions: [],
    currentSession: null,
    isPromptManagerOpen: false,
    selectedUploadProvider: 'drive',
    isUploading: false,
    uploadProgress: 0,

    // Session management
    createSession: (name) => {
      const session = createEmptySession(name);
      set((state) => {
        state.sessions.push(session);
        state.currentSession = session;
      });
      return session;
    },

    loadSession: (id) => {
      const session = get().sessions.find(s => s.id === id);
      if (session) {
        set((state) => {
          state.currentSession = session;
        });
      }
    },

    saveSession: async () => {
      const { currentSession } = get();
      if (!currentSession) return;

      currentSession.updatedAt = new Date();

      const db = await openDB(DB_NAME, DB_VERSION);
      await db.put('sessions', currentSession);

      set((state) => {
        const index = state.sessions.findIndex(s => s.id === currentSession.id);
        if (index >= 0) {
          state.sessions[index] = currentSession;
        }
      });
    },

    deleteSession: async (id) => {
      const db = await openDB(DB_NAME, DB_VERSION);
      await db.delete('sessions', id);

      set((state) => {
        state.sessions = state.sessions.filter(s => s.id !== id);
        if (state.currentSession?.id === id) {
          state.currentSession = null;
        }
      });
    },

    duplicateSession: (id) => {
      const original = get().sessions.find(s => s.id === id);
      if (!original) throw new Error('Session not found');

      const copy: PromptSession = {
        ...original,
        id: `session-${uuidv4()}`,
        name: `${original.name} (Copy)`,
        createdAt: new Date(),
        updatedAt: new Date(),
        isCompleted: false,
        uploadResult: undefined,
      };

      set((state) => {
        state.sessions.push(copy);
      });

      return copy;
    },

    renameSession: (id, newName) => {
      set((state) => {
        const session = state.sessions.find(s => s.id === id);
        if (session) {
          session.name = newName;
          session.updatedAt = new Date();
        }
      });
    },

    // Prompt operations
    updatePromptText: (text) => {
      set((state) => {
        if (state.currentSession) {
          state.currentSession.promptText = text;
          state.currentSession.updatedAt = new Date();
        }
      });
    },

    // Note operations
    addNote: (title, content) => {
      const note: PromptNote = {
        id: `note-${uuidv4()}`,
        title,
        content,
        createdAt: new Date(),
        attachedToLink: false,
      };

      set((state) => {
        if (state.currentSession) {
          state.currentSession.notes.push(note);
          state.currentSession.updatedAt = new Date();
        }
      });
    },

    updateNote: (id, updates) => {
      set((state) => {
        if (state.currentSession) {
          const note = state.currentSession.notes.find(n => n.id === id);
          if (note) {
            Object.assign(note, updates);
            state.currentSession.updatedAt = new Date();
          }
        }
      });
    },

    deleteNote: (id) => {
      set((state) => {
        if (state.currentSession) {
          state.currentSession.notes = state.currentSession.notes.filter(n => n.id !== id);
          state.currentSession.updatedAt = new Date();
        }
      });
    },

    toggleNoteAttachment: (id) => {
      set((state) => {
        if (state.currentSession) {
          const note = state.currentSession.notes.find(n => n.id === id);
          if (note) {
            note.attachedToLink = !note.attachedToLink;
          }
        }
      });
    },

    // File operations
    addFile: (fileData, folderPath = '/') => {
      const file: PromptFile = {
        id: `file-${uuidv4()}`,
        ...fileData,
        folderPath,
      };

      set((state) => {
        if (state.currentSession) {
          state.currentSession.files.push(file);
          addFileToFolder(state.currentSession.folderStructure, file, folderPath);
          state.currentSession.updatedAt = new Date();
        }
      });
    },

    moveFile: (fileId, newFolderPath) => {
      set((state) => {
        if (state.currentSession) {
          const file = state.currentSession.files.find(f => f.id === fileId);
          if (file) {
            // Remove from old location
            removeFromFolder(state.currentSession.folderStructure, fileId);
            // Add to new location
            file.folderPath = newFolderPath;
            addFileToFolder(state.currentSession.folderStructure, file, newFolderPath);
            state.currentSession.updatedAt = new Date();
          }
        }
      });
    },

    renameFile: (fileId, newName) => {
      set((state) => {
        if (state.currentSession) {
          const file = state.currentSession.files.find(f => f.id === fileId);
          if (file) {
            file.name = newName;
            updateInFolder(state.currentSession.folderStructure, fileId, { name: newName });
            state.currentSession.updatedAt = new Date();
          }
        }
      });
    },

    deleteFile: (fileId) => {
      set((state) => {
        if (state.currentSession) {
          state.currentSession.files = state.currentSession.files.filter(f => f.id !== fileId);
          removeFromFolder(state.currentSession.folderStructure, fileId);
          state.currentSession.updatedAt = new Date();
        }
      });
    },

    createFolder: (name, parentPath) => {
      const folder: PromptFolder = {
        id: `folder-${uuidv4()}`,
        name,
        path: `${parentPath === '/' ? '' : parentPath}/${name}`,
        children: [],
      };

      set((state) => {
        if (state.currentSession) {
          addFolderToFolder(state.currentSession.folderStructure, folder, parentPath);
          state.currentSession.updatedAt = new Date();
        }
      });
    },

    renameFolder: (folderId, newName) => {
      set((state) => {
        if (state.currentSession) {
          updateFolderInFolder(state.currentSession.folderStructure, folderId, { name: newName });
          state.currentSession.updatedAt = new Date();
        }
      });
    },

    deleteFolder: (folderId) => {
      set((state) => {
        if (state.currentSession) {
          // Remove files in folder
          const folderPath = getFolderPath(state.currentSession.folderStructure, folderId);
          if (folderPath) {
            state.currentSession.files = state.currentSession.files.filter(f => !f.folderPath.startsWith(folderPath));
          }
          removeFolderFromFolder(state.currentSession.folderStructure, folderId);
          state.currentSession.updatedAt = new Date();
        }
      });
    },

    compressFile: (fileId, profileId) => {
      set((state) => {
        if (state.currentSession) {
          const file = state.currentSession.files.find(f => f.id === fileId);
          if (file) {
            file.isCompressed = true;
            file.compressionProfile = profileId;
            state.currentSession.updatedAt = new Date();
          }
        }
      });
    },

    // Drag-drop from main app
    addDragDropFile: (fileData, sourcePanelId) => {
      const file: PromptFile = {
        id: `file-${uuidv4()}`,
        name: fileData.name,
        size: fileData.size,
        type: fileData.type || 'application/octet-stream',
        source: 'drag-drop',
        sourcePath: fileData.path,
        sourcePanelId,
        folderPath: '/',
        isCompressed: false,
      };

      set((state) => {
        if (state.currentSession) {
          state.currentSession.files.push(file);
          addFileToFolder(state.currentSession.folderStructure, file, '/');
          state.currentSession.updatedAt = new Date();
        }
      });
    },

    // Upload
    completeAndUpload: async () => {
      const { currentSession, selectedUploadProvider } = get();
      if (!currentSession) throw new Error('No active session');

      set((state) => {
        state.isUploading = true;
        state.uploadProgress = 0;
      });

      try {
        // Generate upload structure
        const uploadData = await prepareUploadData(currentSession);
        
        // Upload to selected provider
        let result;
        if (selectedUploadProvider === 'drive') {
          result = await uploadToDrive(uploadData, currentSession.name, (progress) => {
            set((state) => { state.uploadProgress = progress; });
          });
        } else {
          result = await uploadToGitHub(uploadData, currentSession.name, (progress) => {
            set((state) => { state.uploadProgress = progress; });
          });
        }

        // Update session
        set((state) => {
          if (state.currentSession) {
            state.currentSession.isCompleted = true;
            state.currentSession.uploadResult = {
              provider: selectedUploadProvider,
              folderPath: result.folderPath,
              shareLink: result.shareLink,
              rawLink: result.rawLink,
              uploadedAt: new Date(),
            };
          }
          state.isUploading = false;
        });

        return { shareLink: result.shareLink };
      } catch (error) {
        set((state) => {
          state.isUploading = false;
        });
        throw error;
      }
    },

    setUploadProvider: (provider) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.selectedUploadProvider = provider;
      });
    },

    // UI
    openPromptManager: () => {
      set((state) => {
        state.isPromptManagerOpen = true;
        if (!state.currentSession) {
          state.currentSession = createEmptySession('Untitled Session');
          state.sessions.push(state.currentSession);
        }
      });
    },

    closePromptManager: () => {
      set((state) => {
        state.isPromptManagerOpen = false;
      });
    },

    togglePromptManager: () => {
      set((state) => {
        state.isPromptManagerOpen = !state.isPromptManagerOpen;
        if (state.isPromptManagerOpen && !state.currentSession) {
          state.currentSession = createEmptySession('Untitled Session');
          state.sessions.push(state.currentSession);
        }
      });
    },

    // Getters
    getSessionFiles: () => get().currentSession?.files || [],
    getFolderStructure: () => get().currentSession?.folderStructure || createDefaultFolder(),
    getTotalSize: () => {
      return get().currentSession?.files.reduce((sum, f) => sum + f.size, 0) || 0;
    },
    getAttachedNotes: () => {
      return get().currentSession?.notes.filter(n => n.attachedToLink) || [];
    },
  }))
);

// Helper functions for folder operations
function addFileToFolder(root: PromptFolder, file: PromptFile, path: string) {
  if (path === '/' || path === '') {
    root.children.push(file);
    return;
  }

  const parts = path.split('/').filter(Boolean);
  let current = root;

  for (const part of parts) {
    const folder = current.children.find(c => 'children' in c && c.name === part) as PromptFolder;
    if (folder) {
      current = folder;
    }
  }

  current.children.push(file);
}

function addFolderToFolder(root: PromptFolder, folder: PromptFolder, parentPath: string) {
  if (parentPath === '/' || parentPath === '') {
    root.children.push(folder);
    return;
  }

  const parts = parentPath.split('/').filter(Boolean);
  let current = root;

  for (const part of parts) {
    const found = current.children.find(c => 'children' in c && c.name === part) as PromptFolder;
    if (found) {
      current = found;
    }
  }

  current.children.push(folder);
}

function removeFromFolder(root: PromptFolder, fileId: string): boolean {
  const index = root.children.findIndex(c => !('children' in c) && c.id === fileId);
  if (index >= 0) {
    root.children.splice(index, 1);
    return true;
  }

  for (const child of root.children) {
    if ('children' in child) {
      if (removeFromFolder(child, fileId)) return true;
    }
  }

  return false;
}

function removeFolderFromFolder(root: PromptFolder, folderId: string): boolean {
  const index = root.children.findIndex(c => 'children' in c && c.id === folderId);
  if (index >= 0) {
    root.children.splice(index, 1);
    return true;
  }

  for (const child of root.children) {
    if ('children' in child) {
      if (removeFolderFromFolder(child, folderId)) return true;
    }
  }

  return false;
}

function updateInFolder(root: PromptFolder, fileId: string, updates: Partial<PromptFile>) {
  const file = root.children.find(c => !('children' in c) && c.id === fileId) as PromptFile;
  if (file) {
    Object.assign(file, updates);
    return;
  }

  for (const child of root.children) {
    if ('children' in child) {
      updateInFolder(child, fileId, updates);
    }
  }
}

function updateFolderInFolder(root: PromptFolder, folderId: string, updates: Partial<PromptFolder>) {
  const folder = root.children.find(c => 'children' in c && c.id === folderId) as PromptFolder;
  if (folder) {
    Object.assign(folder, updates);
    return;
  }

  for (const child of root.children) {
    if ('children' in child) {
      updateFolderInFolder(child, folderId, updates);
    }
  }
}

function getFolderPath(root: PromptFolder, folderId: string): string | null {
  if (root.id === folderId) return root.path;

  for (const child of root.children) {
    if ('children' in child) {
      const found = getFolderPath(child, folderId);
      if (found) return found;
    }
  }

  return null;
}

async function prepareUploadData(session: PromptSession): Promise<FormData> {
  const formData = new FormData();

  // Add prompt.txt
  const promptBlob = new Blob([session.promptText], { type: 'text/plain' });
  formData.append('prompt.txt', promptBlob, 'prompt.txt');

  // Add links.txt with notes
  const linksContent = generateLinksContent(session);
  const linksBlob = new Blob([linksContent], { type: 'text/plain' });
  formData.append('links.txt', linksBlob, 'links.txt');

  // Add files
  for (const file of session.files) {
    if (file.content) {
      formData.append(file.name, file.content, file.name);
    } else {
      // Placeholder for referenced files
      const placeholder = new Blob([`Reference: ${file.sourcePath || file.name}`], { type: 'text/plain' });
      formData.append(file.name, placeholder, file.name);
    }
  }

  return formData;
}

function generateLinksContent(session: PromptSession): string {
  let content = `Session: ${session.name}\n`;
  content += `Created: ${session.createdAt.toISOString()}\n`;
  content += `Files: ${session.files.length}\n\n`;
  
  content += `Attached Notes:\n`;
  for (const note of session.notes.filter(n => n.attachedToLink)) {
    content += `\n--- ${note.title} ---\n`;
    content += `${note.content}\n`;
  }

  content += `\nFile List:\n`;
  for (const file of session.files) {
    content += `- ${file.name} (${file.size} bytes) [${file.source}]\n`;
  }

  return content;
}

  data: FormData, 
  sessionName: string,
  onProgress: (progress: number) => void
): Promise<{ folderPath: string; shareLink: string; rawLink?: string }> {
  // Implementation using Google Drive API

  // Upload all files

  onProgress(50);
  
  // Mock implementation

    folderPath: `Pro-MNT/${sessionName}`,
    shareLink: `https://drive.google.com/drive/folders/mock-folder-id`,
  };
}

  onProgress: (progress: number) => void
): Promise<{ folderPath: string; shareLink: string; rawLink: string }> {

FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/prakash-app/src/stores/renameStore.ts
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
import { create } from 'zustand';
import { immer } from 'zustand/middleware/immer';
import { RenameState } from '@/types/rename';
import { getEngineForConversion, needsConversion, getExtension } from '@/lib/conversionEngines';

interface RenameStore extends RenameState {
  // Actions
  startRename: (item: RenameState['renamingItem']) => void;
  updateNewName: (name: string) => void;
  cancelRename: () => void;
  confirmRename: () => Promise<void>;
  setConversionProgress: (progress: number) => void;
  openKeepReplaceDialog: (result: RenameState['pendingConversion']) => void;
  keepBoth: () => Promise<void>;
  replaceOriginal: () => Promise<void>;
  skipConversion: () => Promise<void>;
}

export const useRenameStore = create<RenameStore>()(
  immer((set, get) => ({
    renamingItem: null,
    newName: '',
    isConverting: false,
    conversionProgress: 0,
    conversionResult: null,
    showKeepReplaceDialog: false,
    pendingConversion: null,

    startRename: (item) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.renamingItem = item;
        state.newName = item.name;
        state.isConverting = false;
        state.conversionProgress = 0;
        state.conversionResult = null;
        state.showKeepReplaceDialog = false;
        state.pendingConversion = null;
      });
    },

    updateNewName: (name) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.newName = name;
      });
    },

    cancelRename: () => {
      set((state) => {
        state.renamingItem = null;
        state.newName = '';
        state.isConverting = false;
        state.conversionProgress = 0;
        state.conversionResult = null;
        state.showKeepReplaceDialog = false;
        state.pendingConversion = null;
      });
    },

    confirmRename: async () => {
      const { renamingItem, newName } = get();
      if (!renamingItem) return;

      const oldExt = getExtension(renamingItem.name);
      const newExt = getExtension(newName);

      if (oldExt !== newExt && needsConversion(renamingItem.name, newName)) {
        set((state) => {
          state.isConverting = true;
          state.conversionProgress = 0;
        });

        try {
          const engine = getEngineForConversion(oldExt, newExt);
          if (!engine) {
            throw new Error('Conversion not supported');
          }

          if (!engine.isReady) {
            await engine.init();
          }

          const originalBlob = await getOriginalFileBlob(renamingItem);
          
          const convertedBlob = await engine.convert(
            originalBlob,
            oldExt,
            newExt,
            (progress) => {
              set((state) => {
                state.conversionProgress = progress;
              });
            }
          );

          set((state) => {
            state.isConverting = false;
            state.pendingConversion = {
              originalName: renamingItem.name,
              newName,
              originalBlob,
              convertedBlob,
            };
            state.showKeepReplaceDialog = true;
          });

        } catch (error) {
          set((state) => {
            state.isConverting = false;
            state.conversionResult = {
              success: false,
              message: (error as Error).message,
            };
          });
        }
      } else {
        await performSimpleRename(renamingItem, newName);
        get().cancelRename();
      }
    },

    setConversionProgress: (progress) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.conversionProgress = progress;
      });
    },

    openKeepReplaceDialog: (result) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.pendingConversion = result;
        state.showKeepReplaceDialog = true;
      });
    },

    keepBoth: async () => {
      const { pendingConversion, renamingItem } = get();
      if (!pendingConversion || !renamingItem) return;

      await saveFile(pendingConversion.originalBlob, pendingConversion.originalName, renamingItem);
      await saveFile(pendingConversion.convertedBlob, pendingConversion.newName, renamingItem);
      
      get().cancelRename();
    },

    replaceOriginal: async () => {
      const { pendingConversion, renamingItem } = get();
      if (!pendingConversion || !renamingItem) return;

      await deleteFile(renamingItem);
      await saveFile(pendingConversion.convertedBlob, pendingConversion.newName, renamingItem);
      
      get().cancelRename();
    },

    skipConversion: async () => {
      const { renamingItem, newName } = get();
      if (!renamingItem) return;

      await performSimpleRename(renamingItem, newName);
      get().cancelRename();
    },
  }))
);

async function getOriginalFileBlob(item: any): Promise<Blob> {
  switch (item.sourceType) {
    case 'storage':
      if (item.handle) {
        const file = await item.handle.getFile();
        return file;
      }
      break;
    case 'drive':
      break;
    case 'github':
      break;
    case 'terminal':
      break;
  }
  throw new Error('Cannot read file from source');
}

async function saveFile(blob: Blob, name: string, context: any): Promise<void> {
  console.log('Saving file:', name, 'Size:', blob.size);
}

async function deleteFile(item: any): Promise<void> {
  console.log('Deleting file:', item.name);
}

async function performSimpleRename(item: any, newName: string): Promise<void> {
  console.log('Renaming', item.name, 'to', newName);
}

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/prakash-app/src/stores/searchStore.ts
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
import { create } from 'zustand';
import { immer } from 'zustand/middleware/immer';
import Fuse from 'fuse.js';
import MiniSearch from 'minisearch';
import { openDB } from 'idb';
import {
  SearchState,
  SearchFilter,
  SearchResult,
  SearchIndexEntry,
  ExtensionStats,
  SearchEngineConfig,
} from '@/types/search';

interface SearchStore extends SearchState {
  // Fuse instance
  fuse: Fuse<SearchIndexEntry> | null;
  miniSearch: MiniSearch | null;
  
  // Actions
  initializeSearch: () => Promise<void>;
  setQuery: (query: string) => void;
  executeSearch: () => void;
  toggleFilterPanel: () => void;
  setFilters: (filters: Partial<SearchFilter>) => void;
  resetFilters: () => void;
  toggleGlobalMode: () => void;
  
  // Index management
  addToIndex: (entries: SearchIndexEntry[]) => Promise<void>;
  removeFromIndex: (ids: string[]) => Promise<void>;
  clearIndex: () => Promise<void>;
  scanSourceForExtensions: (sourceType: string, accountId: string, items: any[]) => Promise<void>;
  
  // Recent searches
  addRecentSearch: (query: string) => void;
  clearRecentSearches: () => void;
  
  // Getters
  getFilteredResults: () => SearchResult[];
  getExtensionSuggestions: (query: string) => ExtensionStats[];
  getTopExtensions: (limit?: number) => ExtensionStats[];
}

const DEFAULT_FILTERS: SearchFilter = {
  sources: ['storage', 'drive', 'github', 'terminal'],
  accounts: [],
  extensions: [],
  type: 'all',
  includeHidden: false,
};

const FUSE_CONFIG: Fuse.IFuseOptions<SearchIndexEntry> = {
  keys: [
    { name: 'name', weight: 0.5 },
    { name: 'path', weight: 0.3 },
    { name: 'extension', weight: 0.2 },
  ],
  threshold: 0.3,
  distance: 100,
  includeScore: true,
  includeMatches: true,
  minMatchCharLength: 2,
  useExtendedSearch: true,
};

const MINI_SEARCH_CONFIG = {
  fields: ['name', 'path', 'extension'],
  storeFields: ['id', 'name', 'path', 'sourceType', 'accountId', 'type', 'size', 'lastModified', 'extension'],
  searchOptions: {
    boost: { name: 2, path: 1.5, extension: 1 },
    fuzzy: 0.3,
    prefix: true,
  },
};

// IndexedDB for persistent index
const DB_NAME = 'search-index-db';
const DB_VERSION = 1;

export const useSearchStore = create<SearchStore>()(
  immer((set, get) => ({
    // State
    query: '',
    isSearching: false,
    results: [],
    filters: { ...DEFAULT_FILTERS },
    isFilterPanelOpen: false,
    availableExtensions: [],
    availableAccounts: [],
    recentSearches: [],
    searchHistory: [],
    isGlobalMode: true,
    indexedCount: 0,
    lastIndexUpdate: null,
    fuse: null,
    miniSearch: null,

    initializeSearch: async () => {
      // Initialize MiniSearch for fast prefix matching
      const miniSearch = new MiniSearch(MINI_SEARCH_CONFIG);
      
      // Load existing index from IndexedDB
      try {
        const db = await openDB(DB_NAME, DB_VERSION, {
          upgrade(db) {
            db.createObjectStore('entries', { keyPath: 'id' });
            db.createObjectStore('extensions', { keyPath: 'extension' });
            db.createObjectStore('accounts', { keyPath: 'id' });
            db.createObjectStore('metadata', { keyPath: 'key' });
          },
        });

        const entries = await db.getAll('entries');
        if (entries.length > 0) {
          miniSearch.addAll(entries);
          
          const extensions = await db.getAll('extensions');
          const accounts = await db.getAll('accounts');
          
          // Rebuild Fuse index
          const fuse = new Fuse(entries, FUSE_CONFIG);
          
          set((state) => {
            state.fuse = fuse;
            state.miniSearch = miniSearch;
            state.availableExtensions = extensions;
            state.availableAccounts = accounts;
            state.indexedCount = entries.length;
            state.lastIndexUpdate = new Date();
          });
        } else {
          set((state) => {
            state.miniSearch = miniSearch;
          });
        }
      } catch (error) {
        console.error('Failed to initialize search:', error);
        set((state) => {
          state.miniSearch = miniSearch;
        });
      }
    },

    setQuery: (query) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.query = query;
      });
      
      // Debounced search
      const { executeSearch } = get();
      clearTimeout((window as any).searchTimeout);
      (window as any).searchTimeout = setTimeout(() => {
        executeSearch();
      }, 150);
    },

    executeSearch: () => {
      const { query, fuse, miniSearch, filters, isGlobalMode } = get();
      
      if (!query.trim() || (!fuse && !miniSearch)) {
        set((state) => {
          state.results = [];
          state.isSearching = false;
        });
        return;
      }

      set((state) => {
        state.isSearching = true;
      });

      let results: SearchResult[] = [];

      // Use MiniSearch for fast prefix/fuzzy matching
      if (miniSearch) {
        const miniResults = miniSearch.search(query, {
          boost: { name: 2, path: 1.5 },
          fuzzy: 0.2,
          prefix: true,
        });

        results = miniResults.map((r: any) => ({
          item: r as SearchIndexEntry,
          score: r.score,
          matches: [],
        }));
      }

      // Use Fuse for advanced fuzzy matching if MiniSearch results are insufficient
      if (fuse && results.length < 20) {
        const fuseResults = fuse.search(query);
        
        // Merge and deduplicate
        const existingIds = new Set(results.map(r => r.item.id));
        const additionalResults = fuseResults
          .filter(r => !existingIds.has(r.item.id))
          .map(r => ({
            item: r.item,
            score: r.score || 0,
            matches: (r.matches || []).map((m: any) => ({
              key: m.key,
              value: m.value,
              indices: m.indices,
            })),
          }));
        
        results = [...results, ...additionalResults];
      }

      // Apply filters
      results = results.filter(r => {
        const item = r.item;
        
        // Source filter
        if (!filters.sources.includes(item.sourceType)) return false;
        
        // Account filter
        if (filters.accounts.length > 0 && !filters.accounts.includes(item.accountId)) return false;
        
        // Extension filter
        if (filters.extensions.length > 0 && !filters.extensions.includes(item.extension)) return false;
        
        // Type filter
        if (filters.type !== 'all' && item.type !== filters.type) return false;
        
        // Size filter
        if (filters.minSize !== undefined && item.size < filters.minSize) return false;
        if (filters.maxSize !== undefined && item.size > filters.maxSize) return false;
        
        // Date filter
        if (filters.dateFrom && item.lastModified < filters.dateFrom) return false;
        if (filters.dateTo && item.lastModified > filters.dateTo) return false;
        
        // Hidden filter
        if (!filters.includeHidden && item.metadata.isHidden) return false;
        
        return true;
      });

      // Sort by score
      results.sort((a, b) => a.score - b.score);

      set((state) => {
        state.results = results.slice(0, 100); // Limit to top 100
        state.isSearching = false;
      });
    },

    toggleFilterPanel: () => {
      set((state) => {
        state.isFilterPanelOpen = !state.isFilterPanelOpen;
      });
    },

    setFilters: (newFilters) => {
      set((state) => {
        Object.assign(state.filters, newFilters);
      });
      get().executeSearch();
    },

    resetFilters: () => {
      set((state) => {
        state.filters = { ...DEFAULT_FILTERS };
      });
      get().executeSearch();
    },

    toggleGlobalMode: () => {
      set((state) => {
        state.isGlobalMode = !state.isGlobalMode;
        if (state.isGlobalMode) {
          state.filters.sources = ['storage', 'drive', 'github', 'terminal'];
          state.filters.accounts = [];
        }
      });
      get().executeSearch();
    },

    addToIndex: async (entries) => {
      const { miniSearch, fuse } = get();
      
      // Add to search engines
      miniSearch?.addAll(entries);
      
      // Rebuild Fuse index
      const allEntries = miniSearch ? (miniSearch as any).documentCount : 0;
      const newFuse = new Fuse(
        miniSearch ? Array.from((miniSearch as any).documentStore.docs.values()) : entries,
        FUSE_CONFIG
      );

      // Persist to IndexedDB
      const db = await openDB(DB_NAME, DB_VERSION);
      const tx = db.transaction('entries', 'readwrite');
      const store = tx.objectStore('entries');
      
      for (const entry of entries) {
        await store.put(entry);
      }
      
      await tx.done;

      // Update extension stats
      await get().updateExtensionStats(entries);

      set((state) => {
        state.fuse = newFuse;
        state.indexedCount += entries.length;
        state.lastIndexUpdate = new Date();
      });
    },

    removeFromIndex: async (ids) => {
      const { miniSearch } = get();
      
      ids.forEach(id => miniSearch?.remove({ id }));
      
      const db = await openDB(DB_NAME, DB_VERSION);
      const tx = db.transaction('entries', 'readwrite');
      const store = tx.objectStore('entries');
      
      for (const id of ids) {
        await store.delete(id);
      }
      
      await tx.done;

      set((state) => {
        state.indexedCount -= ids.length;
      });
    },

    clearIndex: async () => {
      const db = await openDB(DB_NAME, DB_VERSION);
      
      await db.clear('entries');
      await db.clear('extensions');
      await db.clear('accounts');
      
      set((state) => {
        state.fuse = null;
        state.miniSearch = null;
        state.availableExtensions = [];
        state.availableAccounts = [];
        state.indexedCount = 0;
        state.results = [];
      });
    },

    scanSourceForExtensions: async (sourceType, accountId, items) => {
      const extensionMap = new Map<string, ExtensionStats>();
      const accountSet = new Set<string>();

      const processItem = (item: any, path: string = '') => {
        const ext = item.name?.includes('.') 
          ? item.name.slice(item.name.lastIndexOf('.')).toLowerCase()
          : '';
        
        if (ext) {
          const existing = extensionMap.get(ext);
          if (existing) {
            existing.count++;
            existing.totalSize += item.size || 0;
            existing.sources.add(sourceType);
            existing.accounts.add(accountId);
          } else {
            extensionMap.set(ext, {
              extension: ext,
              count: 1,
              totalSize: item.size || 0,
              sources: new Set([sourceType]),
              accounts: new Set([accountId]),
            });
          }
        }

        accountSet.add(accountId);

        // Process children
        if (item.children) {
          item.children.forEach((child: any) => 
            processItem(child, `${path}/${item.name}`)
          );
        }
      };

      items.forEach((item: any) => processItem(item));

      // Update store
      const extensions = Array.from(extensionMap.values());
      
      const db = await openDB(DB_NAME, DB_VERSION);
      const tx = db.transaction(['extensions', 'accounts'], 'readwrite');
      
      for (const ext of extensions) {
        const existing = await tx.objectStore('extensions').get(ext.extension);
        if (existing) {
          existing.count += ext.count;
          existing.totalSize += ext.totalSize;
          ext.sources.forEach(s => existing.sources.add(s));
          ext.accounts.forEach(a => existing.accounts.add(a));
          await tx.objectStore('extensions').put(existing);
        } else {
          await tx.objectStore('extensions').put({
            ...ext,
            sources: Array.from(ext.sources),
            accounts: Array.from(ext.accounts),
          });
        }
      }

      // Add account
      await tx.objectStore('accounts').put({
        id: accountId,
        sourceType,
        name: accountId,
      });

      await tx.done;

      // Reload from DB
      const allExtensions = await db.getAll('extensions');
      const allAccounts = await db.getAll('accounts');

      set((state) => {
        state.availableExtensions = allExtensions.map(e => ({
          ...e,
          sources: new Set(e.sources),
          accounts: new Set(e.accounts),
        }));
        state.availableAccounts = allAccounts;
      });
    },

    updateExtensionStats: async (entries: SearchIndexEntry[]) => {
      const extensionMap = new Map<string, ExtensionStats>();

      entries.forEach(entry => {
        if (entry.extension) {
          const existing = extensionMap.get(entry.extension);
          if (existing) {
            existing.count++;
            existing.totalSize += entry.size;
            existing.sources.add(entry.sourceType);
            existing.accounts.add(entry.accountId);
          } else {
            extensionMap.set(entry.extension, {
              extension: entry.extension,
              count: 1,
              totalSize: entry.size,
              sources: new Set([entry.sourceType]),
              accounts: new Set([entry.accountId]),
            });
          }
        }
      });

      const db = await openDB(DB_NAME, DB_VERSION);
      const tx = db.transaction('extensions', 'readwrite');

      for (const [ext, stats] of extensionMap) {
        const existing = await tx.store.get(ext);
        if (existing) {
          existing.count += stats.count;
          existing.totalSize += stats.totalSize;
          stats.sources.forEach(s => existing.sources.add(s));
          stats.accounts.forEach(a => existing.accounts.add(a));
          await tx.store.put(existing);
        } else {
          await tx.store.put({
            ...stats,
            sources: Array.from(stats.sources),
            accounts: Array.from(stats.accounts),
          });
        }
      }

      await tx.done;
    },

    addRecentSearch: (query) => {
      if (!query.trim()) return;
      
      set((state) => {
        state.recentSearches = [
          query,
          ...state.recentSearches.filter(s => s !== query),
        ].slice(0, 10);
      });
    },

    clearRecentSearches: () => {
      set((state) => {
        state.recentSearches = [];
      });
    },

    getFilteredResults: () => {
      return get().results;
    },

    getExtensionSuggestions: (query) => {
      const { availableExtensions } = get();
      if (!query) return [];
      
      return availableExtensions.filter(e => 
        e.extension.toLowerCase().includes(query.toLowerCase())
      ).sort((a, b) => b.count - a.count);
    },

    getTopExtensions: (limit = 20) => {
      return get().availableExtensions
        .sort((a, b) => b.count - a.count)
        .slice(0, limit);
    },
  }))
);

// Selectors
export const useSearchQuery = () => useSearchStore((s) => s.query);
export const useSearchResults = () => useSearchStore((s) => s.results);
export const useIsSearching = () => useSearchStore((s) => s.isSearching);
export const useSearchFilters = () => useSearchStore((s) => s.filters);
export const useIsFilterPanelOpen = () => useSearchStore((s) => s.isFilterPanelOpen);
export const useAvailableExtensions = () => useSearchStore((s) => s.availableExtensions);
export const useAvailableAccounts = () => useSearchStore((s) => s.availableAccounts);
export const useIsGlobalMode = () => useSearchStore((s) => s.isGlobalMode);
export const useRecentSearches = () => useSearchStore((s) => s.recentSearches);
export const useIndexedCount = () => useSearchStore((s) => s.indexedCount);

FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/prakash-app/src/stores/terminalStore.ts
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
import { create } from 'zustand';
import { immer } from 'zustand/middleware/immer';
import { 
  TerminalFileSystemEntry, 
  TerminalFile,
  TerminalViewMode,
  TerminalSortBy,
  TerminalPanelState 
} from '@/types/terminal';
import { webcontainerApi } from '@/lib/webcontainerApi';

interface TerminalStore extends TerminalPanelState {
  // Actions
  initialize: () => Promise<void>;
  shutdown: () => Promise<void>;
  navigateTo: (path: string) => Promise<void>;
  navigateBack: () => Promise<void>;
  navigateToRoot: () => Promise<void>;
  selectFile: (file: TerminalFile | null) => Promise<void>;
  refreshCurrent: () => Promise<void>;
  setViewMode: (mode: TerminalViewMode) => void;
  setSortBy: (sort: TerminalSortBy) => void;
  
  // Getters
  getSortedEntries: () => TerminalFileSystemEntry[];
  getBreadcrumb: () => string[];
  canGoBack: () => boolean;
}

const createInitialState = (): TerminalPanelState => ({
  isInitialized: false,
  isBooting: false,
  bootProgress: 0,
  currentPath: '/',
  pathHistory: [],
  entries: [],
  viewMode: 'list',
  sortBy: 'name-asc',
  selectedFile: null,
  error: null,
  webcontainerInstance: null,
});

export const useTerminalStore = create<TerminalStore>()(
  immer((set, get) => ({
    ...createInitialState(),

    initialize: async () => {
      const { isInitialized, isBooting } = get();
      if (isInitialized || isBooting) return;

      set((state) => {
        state.isBooting = true;
        state.bootProgress = 0;
        state.error = null;
      });

      try {
        const instance = await webcontainerApi.init((progress) => {
          set((state) => {
            state.bootProgress = Math.round(progress * 100);
          });
        });

        set((state) => {
          state.isInitialized = true;
          state.isBooting = false;
          state.bootProgress = 100;
          state.webcontainerInstance = instance;
        });

        // Load root directory
        await get().navigateTo('/');
      } catch (err) {
        set((state) => {
          state.error = (err as Error).message;
          state.isBooting = false;
          state.bootProgress = 0;
        });
      }
    },

    shutdown: async () => {
      await webcontainerApi.shutdown();
      set(createInitialState());
    },

    navigateTo: async (path) => {
      const { currentPath, pathHistory } = get();
      
      set((state) => {
        state.isBooting = true;
        state.error = null;
        state.selectedFile = null;
      });

      try {
        const entries = await webcontainerApi.readDirectory(path);
        
        set((state) => {
          if (path !== currentPath) {
            state.pathHistory.push(currentPath);
          }
          state.currentPath = path;
          state.entries = entries;
          state.isBooting = false;
        });
      } catch (err) {
        set((state) => {
          state.error = (err as Error).message;
          state.isBooting = false;
        });
      }
    },

    navigateBack: async () => {
      const { pathHistory } = get();
      if (pathHistory.length === 0) {
        await get().navigateToRoot();
        return;
      }

      const previousPath = pathHistory[pathHistory.length - 1];
      
      set((state) => {
        state.pathHistory.pop();
        state.selectedFile = null;
      });

      await get().navigateTo(previousPath);
    },

    navigateToRoot: async () => {
      set((state) => {
        state.pathHistory = [];
        state.selectedFile = null;
      });
      await get().navigateTo('/');
    },

    selectFile: async (file) => {
      if (!file) {
        set((state) => {
          state.selectedFile = null;
        });
        return;
      }

      if (file.type === 'directory') {
        await get().navigateTo(file.path);
      } else {
        // Read file content
        set((state) => {
          state.isBooting = true;
        });

        try {
          const content = await webcontainerApi.readFile(file.path);
          set((state) => {
            state.selectedFile = { ...file, content };
            state.isBooting = false;
          });
        } catch (err) {
          set((state) => {
            state.error = (err as Error).message;
            state.isBooting = false;
          });
        }
      }
    },

    refreshCurrent: async () => {
      const { currentPath } = get();
      await get().navigateTo(currentPath);
    },

    setViewMode: (mode) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.viewMode = mode;
      });
    },

    setSortBy: (sort) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.sortBy = sort;
      });
    },

    getSortedEntries: () => {
      const { entries, sortBy } = get();
      const sorted = [...entries];
      
      switch (sortBy) {
        case 'name-asc':
          return sorted.sort((a, b) => a.name.localeCompare(b.name));
        case 'name-desc':
          return sorted.sort((a, b) => b.name.localeCompare(a.name));
        case 'date':
          return sorted.sort((a, b) => b.lastModified.getTime() - a.lastModified.getTime());
        case 'size':
          return sorted.sort((a, b) => b.size - a.size);
        default:
          return sorted;
      }
    },

    getBreadcrumb: () => {
      const { currentPath } = get();
      if (currentPath === '/') return ['root'];
      return ['root', ...currentPath.split('/').filter(Boolean)];
    },

    canGoBack: () => {
      const { pathHistory, currentPath } = get();
      return pathHistory.length > 0 || currentPath !== '/';
    },
  }))
);

// Selectors
export const useTerminalInitialized = () => useTerminalStore((s) => s.isInitialized);
export const useTerminalBooting = () => useTerminalStore((s) => s.isBooting);
export const useTerminalBootProgress = () => useTerminalStore((s) => s.bootProgress);
export const useTerminalCurrentPath = () => useTerminalStore((s) => s.currentPath);
export const useTerminalEntries = () => useTerminalStore((s) => s.getSortedEntries());
export const useTerminalViewMode = () => useTerminalStore((s) => s.viewMode);
export const useTerminalSortBy = () => useTerminalStore((s) => s.sortBy);
export const useTerminalSelectedFile = () => useTerminalStore((s) => s.selectedFile);
export const useTerminalError = () => useTerminalStore((s) => s.error);

FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/prakash-app/src/stores/treeStore.ts
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
import { create } from 'zustand';
import { immer } from 'zustand/middleware/immer';
import { TreeViewState, TreeNode, TreeStats, NodeProperties } from '@/types/tree';

interface TreeStore extends TreeViewState {
  // Actions
  openTree: (node: TreeNode) => void;
  closeTree: () => void;
  toggleNode: (nodeId: string) => void;
  expandAll: () => void;
  collapseAll: () => void;
  expandToNode: (nodeId: string) => void;
  setViewMode: (mode: TreeViewState['viewMode']) => void;
  setSearchQuery: (query: string) => void;
  updateNodeProperties: (nodeId: string, properties: Partial<NodeProperties>) => void;
  selectNode: (node: TreeNode) => void;
  calculateStats: () => TreeStats;
  exportToTxt: () => string;
  exportToPdf: () => Promise<Blob>;
  copyToClipboard: (type: 'properties' | 'tree' | 'both') => Promise<void>;
}

const createInitialState = (): TreeViewState => ({
  isOpen: false,
  selectedNode: null,
  rootNode: null,
  expandedNodes: new Set(),
  viewMode: 'hierarchy',
  searchQuery: '',
  isLoading: false,
  error: null,
  exportFormat: null,
});

export const useTreeStore = create<TreeStore>()(
  immer((set, get) => ({
    ...createInitialState(),

    openTree: (node) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.isOpen = true;
        state.selectedNode = node;
        state.rootNode = node;
        state.expandedNodes = new Set([node.id]);
      });
    },

    closeTree: () => {
      set(createInitialState());
    },

    toggleNode: (nodeId) => {
      set((state) => {
        if (state.expandedNodes.has(nodeId)) {
          state.expandedNodes.delete(nodeId);
        } else {
          state.expandedNodes.add(nodeId);
        }
      });
    },

    expandAll: () => {
      const { rootNode } = get();
      if (!rootNode) return;

      const allIds = new Set<string>();
      const collectIds = (node: TreeNode) => {
        allIds.add(node.id);
        node.children?.forEach(collectIds);
      };
      collectIds(rootNode);

      set((state) => {
        state.expandedNodes = allIds;
      });
    },

    collapseAll: () => {
      const { rootNode } = get();
      if (!rootNode) return;

      set((state) => {
        state.expandedNodes = new Set([rootNode.id]);
      });
    },

    expandToNode: (nodeId) => {
      set((state) => {
        // Expand all parents of the target node
        let current = state.selectedNode;
        while (current?.parent) {
          state.expandedNodes.add(current.parent.id);
          current = current.parent;
        }
        state.expandedNodes.add(nodeId);
      });
    },

    setViewMode: (mode) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.viewMode = mode;
      });
    },

    setSearchQuery: (query) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.searchQuery = query;
      });
    },

    updateNodeProperties: (nodeId, properties) => {
      set((state) => {
        const updateNode = (node: TreeNode): boolean => {
          if (node.id === nodeId) {
            node.properties = { ...node.properties, ...properties };
            return true;
          }
          return node.children?.some(updateNode) || false;
        };
        if (state.rootNode) updateNode(state.rootNode);
      });
    },

    selectNode: (node) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.selectedNode = node;
      });
    },

    calculateStats: () => {
      const { rootNode } = get();
      if (!rootNode) {
        return {
          totalFiles: 0,
          totalDirectories: 0,
          totalSize: 0,
          maxDepth: 0,
          averageFileSize: 0,
        };
      }

      let totalFiles = 0;
      let totalDirectories = 0;
      let totalSize = 0;
      let maxDepth = 0;
      const fileSizes: number[] = [];

      const traverse = (node: TreeNode, depth: number) => {
        maxDepth = Math.max(maxDepth, depth);
        
        if (node.type === 'file') {
          totalFiles++;
          totalSize += node.size;
          fileSizes.push(node.size);
        } else if (node.type === 'directory') {
          totalDirectories++;
        }

        node.children?.forEach(child => traverse(child, depth + 1));
      };

      traverse(rootNode, 0);

      return {
        totalFiles,
        totalDirectories,
        totalSize,
        maxDepth,
        averageFileSize: fileSizes.length > 0 
          ? fileSizes.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0) / fileSizes.length 
          : 0,
      };
    },

    exportToTxt: () => {
      const { rootNode, selectedNode } = get();
      const targetNode = selectedNode || rootNode;
      if (!targetNode) return '';

      let output = '';
      output += `TREE STRUCTURE REPORT\n`;
      output += `=====================\n\n`;
      output += `Generated: ${new Date().toLocaleString()}\n`;
      output += `Root: ${targetNode.name}\n`;
      output += `Path: ${targetNode.path}\n\n`;

      const buildTree = (node: TreeNode, prefix: string, isLast: boolean) => {
        const connector = isLast ? '└── ' : '├── ';
        const line = prefix + connector + node.name;
        output += line + '\n';

        if (node.children) {
          const newPrefix = prefix + (isLast ? '    ' : '│   ');
          node.children.forEach((child, index) => {
            buildTree(child, newPrefix, index === node.children!.length - 1);
          });
        }
      };

      if (targetNode.children) {
        targetNode.children.forEach((child, index) => {
          buildTree(child, '', index === targetNode.children!.length - 1);
        });
      }

      // Add properties section
      output += `\n\nPROPERTIES\n`;
      output += `==========\n`;
      output += formatProperties(targetNode.properties);

      return output;
    },

    exportToPdf: async () => {
      const { jsPDF } = await import('jspdf');
      const { rootNode, selectedNode } = get();
      const targetNode = selectedNode || rootNode;
      
      if (!targetNode) throw new Error('No node selected');

      const doc = new jsPDF();
      
      // Title
      doc.setFontSize(20);
      doc.text('Tree Structure Report', 14, 20);
      
      // Metadata
      doc.setFontSize(10);
      doc.text(`Generated: ${new Date().toLocaleString()}`, 14, 30);
      doc.text(`Root: ${targetNode.name}`, 14, 36);
      doc.text(`Path: ${targetNode.path}`, 14, 42);

      // Tree table
      const tableData: string[][] = [];
      const buildTableData = (node: TreeNode, depth: number) => {
        const indent = '  '.repeat(depth);
        tableData.push([
          indent + node.name,
          node.type,
          formatBytes(node.size),
          node.lastModified.toLocaleDateString(),
        ]);

        node.children?.forEach(child => buildTableData(child, depth + 1));
      };

      if (targetNode.children) {
        targetNode.children.forEach(child => buildTableData(child, 0));
      }

      // @ts-ignore - jspdf-autotable
      doc.autoTable({
        startY: 50,
        head: [['Name', 'Type', 'Size', 'Modified']],
        body: tableData,
        styles: { fontSize: 8, cellPadding: 2 },
        headStyles: { fillColor: [66, 139, 202] },
      });

      // Properties section
      const finalY = (doc as any).lastAutoTable?.finalY || 50;
      doc.setFontSize(12);
      doc.text('Properties', 14, finalY + 10);

      const props = formatPropertiesForPdf(targetNode.properties);
      // @ts-ignore
      doc.autoTable({
        startY: finalY + 15,
        body: props,
        styles: { fontSize: 8 },
      });

      return doc.output('blob');
    },

    copyToClipboard: async (type) => {
      const { exportToTxt, selectedNode, rootNode } = get();
      const targetNode = selectedNode || rootNode;
      if (!targetNode) return;

      let text = '';

      switch (type) {
        case 'properties':
          text = formatProperties(targetNode.properties);
          break;
        case 'tree':
          text = exportToTxt();
          break;
        case 'both':
          text = exportToTxt();
          break;
      }

      await navigator.clipboard.writeText(text);
    },
  }))
);

// Helper functions
function formatBytes(bytes: number): string {
  if (bytes === 0) return '-';
  const units = ['B', 'KB', 'MB', 'GB', 'TB'];
  let size = bytes;
  let unitIndex = 0;
  while (size >= 1024 && unitIndex < units.length - 1) {
    size /= 1024;
    unitIndex++;
  }
  return `${size.toFixed(1)} ${units[unitIndex]}`;
}

function formatProperties(props: NodeProperties): string {
  let output = '';
  if (props.mountPath) output += `Mount Path: ${props.mountPath}\n`;
  if (props.usedSpace !== undefined) output += `Used Space: ${formatBytes(props.usedSpace)}\n`;
  if (props.freeSpace !== undefined) output += `Free Space: ${formatBytes(props.freeSpace)}\n`;
  if (props.totalSpace !== undefined) output += `Total Space: ${formatBytes(props.totalSpace)}\n`;
  if (props.fileSystemType) output += `File System: ${props.fileSystemType}\n`;
  if (props.label) output += `Label: ${props.label}\n`;
  if (props.createdAt) output += `Created: ${props.createdAt.toLocaleString()}\n`;
  if (props.modifiedAt) output += `Modified: ${props.modifiedAt.toLocaleString()}\n`;
  if (props.accessedAt) output += `Accessed: ${props.accessedAt.toLocaleString()}\n`;
  if (props.permissions) output += `Permissions: ${props.permissions}\n`;
  if (props.owner) output += `Owner: ${props.owner}\n`;
  if (props.group) output += `Group: ${props.group}\n`;
  if (props.mimeType) output += `MIME Type: ${props.mimeType}\n`;
  if (props.isHidden !== undefined) output += `Hidden: ${props.isHidden}\n`;
  if (props.isReadOnly !== undefined) output += `Read Only: ${props.isReadOnly}\n`;
  if (props.isSystem !== undefined) output += `System: ${props.isSystem}\n`;
  if (props.linkTarget) output += `Link Target: ${props.linkTarget}\n`;
  if (props.checksum) output += `Checksum: ${props.checksum}\n`;
  if (props.version) output += `Version: ${props.version}\n`;
  if (props.tags?.length) output += `Tags: ${props.tags.join(', ')}\n`;
  return output;
}

function formatPropertiesForPdf(props: NodeProperties): string[][] {
  const result: string[][] = [];
  if (props.mountPath) result.push(['Mount Path', props.mountPath]);
  if (props.usedSpace !== undefined) result.push(['Used Space', formatBytes(props.usedSpace)]);
  if (props.freeSpace !== undefined) result.push(['Free Space', formatBytes(props.freeSpace)]);
  if (props.totalSpace !== undefined) result.push(['Total Space', formatBytes(props.totalSpace)]);
  if (props.fileSystemType) result.push(['File System', props.fileSystemType]);
  if (props.label) result.push(['Label', props.label]);
  if (props.createdAt) result.push(['Created', props.createdAt.toLocaleString()]);
  if (props.modifiedAt) result.push(['Modified', props.modifiedAt.toLocaleString()]);
  if (props.permissions) result.push(['Permissions', props.permissions]);
  if (props.owner) result.push(['Owner', props.owner]);
  return result;
}
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/prakash-app/src/stores/dfolStore.t
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
import { create } from 'zustand';
import { immer } from 'zustand/middleware/immer';
import { DFOLState, DFOLItem, DFOLMode, DFOLProfile, DFOLOperation, DFOLNotification, DEFAULT_PROFILES } from '@/types/dfol';

interface DFOLStore extends DFOLState {
  // Actions
  enterDFOLMode: () => void;
  exitDFOLMode: () => void;
  toggleItemSelection: (item: DFOLItem) => void;
  selectItem: (item: DFOLItem, operations: DFOLMode[]) => void;
  deselectItem: (itemId: string) => void;
  clearSelection: () => void;
  setItemOperations: (itemId: string, operations: DFOLMode[]) => void;
  setItemProfile: (itemId: string, profileId: string) => void;
  setActiveProfile: (profileId: string) => void;
  addCustomProfile: (profile: DFOLProfile) => void;
  removeCustomProfile: (profileId: string) => void;
  openProfilePanel: () => void;
  closeProfilePanel: () => void;
  openExecutePanel: () => void;
  closeExecutePanel: () => void;
  executeOperations: () => Promise<void>;
  updateOperationStatus: (operationId: string, status: DFOLOperation['status'], progress?: number, message?: string) => void;
  completeOperation: (operationId: string, result: DFOLOperation['result']) => void;
  failOperation: (operationId: string, error: string) => void;
  addNotification: (notification: Omit<DFOLNotification, 'id' | 'timestamp'>) => void;
  dismissNotification: (id: string) => void;
  clearNotifications: () => void;

  // Getters
  getPendingOperations: () => DFOLOperation[];
  getOperationStats: () => { total: number; pending: number; running: number; completed: number; failed: number };
}

const generateTimestamp = () => {
  const now = new Date();
  return now.toISOString().replace(/[:.]/g, '-').slice(0, 19);
};

export const useDFOLStore = create<DFOLStore>()(
  immer((set, get) => ({
    isDFOLMode: false,
    selectedItems: [],
    operations: [],
    activeProfile: DEFAULT_PROFILES[0].id,
    customProfiles: [],
    outputDirectory: `/DFOL/${generateTimestamp()}`,
    isExecuting: false,
    isProfilePanelOpen: false,
    isExecutePanelOpen: false,
    globalProgress: 0,
    notifications: [],

    enterDFOLMode: () => {
      set((state) => {
        state.isDFOLMode = true;
        state.selectedItems = [];
        state.operations = [];
        state.outputDirectory = `/DFOL/${generateTimestamp()}`;
      });
    },

    exitDFOLMode: () => {
      set((state) => {
        state.isDFOLMode = false;
        state.selectedItems = [];
        state.isProfilePanelOpen = false;
        state.isExecutePanelOpen = false;
        if (!state.isExecuting) {
          state.operations = [];
        }
      });
    },

    toggleItemSelection: (item) => {
      set((state) => {
        const existingIndex = state.selectedItems.findIndex(i => i.id === item.id);
        if (existingIndex >= 0) {
          state.selectedItems.splice(existingIndex, 1);
        } else {
          state.selectedItems.push({ ...item, operations: ['folder'] });
        }
      });
    },

    selectItem: (item, operations) => {
      set((state) => {
        const existingIndex = state.selectedItems.findIndex(i => i.id === item.id);
        if (existingIndex >= 0) {
          state.selectedItems[existingIndex].operations = operations;
        } else {
          state.selectedItems.push({ ...item, operations });
        }
      });
    },

    deselectItem: (itemId) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.selectedItems = state.selectedItems.filter(i => i.id !== itemId);
      });
    },

    clearSelection: () => {
      set((state) => {
        state.selectedItems = [];
      });
    },

    setItemOperations: (itemId, operations) => {
      set((state) => {
        const item = state.selectedItems.find(i => i.id === itemId);
        if (item) {
          item.operations = operations;
        }
      });
    },

    setItemProfile: (itemId, profileId) => {
      set((state) => {
        const item = state.selectedItems.find(i => i.id === itemId);
        if (item) {
          item.selectedProfile = profileId;
        }
      });
    },

    setActiveProfile: (profileId) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.activeProfile = profileId;
      });
    },

    addCustomProfile: (profile) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.customProfiles.push(profile);
      });
    },

    removeCustomProfile: (profileId) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.customProfiles = state.customProfiles.filter(p => p.id !== profileId);
      });
    },

    openProfilePanel: () => {
      set((state) => {
        state.isProfilePanelOpen = true;
      });
    },

    closeProfilePanel: () => {
      set((state) => {
        state.isProfilePanelOpen = false;
      });
    },

    openExecutePanel: () => {
      set((state) => {
        state.isExecutePanelOpen = true;
      });
    },

    closeExecutePanel: () => {
      set((state) => {
        state.isExecutePanelOpen = false;
      });
    },

    executeOperations: async () => {
      const { selectedItems, outputDirectory, activeProfile } = get();

      // Generate operations
      const operations: DFOLOperation[] = [];
      selectedItems.forEach(item => {
        item.operations.forEach(mode => {
          operations.push({
            id: `${item.id}-${mode}-${Date.now()}`,
            itemId: item.id,
            mode,
            status: 'pending',
            progress: 0,
            message: 'Waiting...',
          });
        });
      });

      set((state) => {
        state.operations = operations;
        state.isExecuting = true;
        state.isExecutePanelOpen = true;
      });

      // Execute operations sequentially or in parallel
      for (const operation of operations) {
        const item = selectedItems.find(i => i.id === operation.itemId);
        if (!item) continue;

        set((state) => {
          const op = state.operations.find(o => o.id === operation.id);
          if (op) {
            op.status = 'running';
            op.message = 'Starting...';
          }
        });

        try {
          await executeSingleOperation(operation, item, outputDirectory, activeProfile);
        } catch (error) {
          get().failOperation(operation.id, (error as Error).message);
        }
      }

      set((state) => {
        state.isExecuting = false;
        state.globalProgress = 100;
      });

      get().addNotification({
        type: 'success',
        message: `DFOL operations completed. Output: ${outputDirectory}`,
        autoDismiss: true,
      });
    },

    updateOperationStatus: (operationId, status, progress, message) => {
      set((state) => {
        const op = state.operations.find(o => o.id === operationId);
        if (op) {
          op.status = status;
          if (progress !== undefined) op.progress = progress;
          if (message !== undefined) op.message = message;
        }

        // Update global progress
        const totalOps = state.operations.length;
        const completedOps = state.operations.filter(o => o.status === 'completed').length;
        const runningOps = state.operations.filter(o => o.status === 'running');
        const runningProgress = runningOps.reduce((sum, o) => sum + o.progress, 0) / (runningOps.length || 1);
        state.globalProgress = ((completedOps + runningProgress / 100) / totalOps) * 100;
      });
    },

    completeOperation: (operationId, result) => {
      set((state) => {
        const op = state.operations.find(o => o.id === operationId);
        if (op) {
          op.status = 'completed';
          op.progress = 100;
          op.message = 'Completed';
          op.result = result;
        }
      });
    },

    failOperation: (operationId, error) => {
      set((state) => {
        const op = state.operations.find(o => o.id === operationId);
        if (op) {
          op.status = 'failed';
          op.message = 'Failed';
          op.error = error;
        }
      });

      get().addNotification({
        type: 'error',
        message: `Operation failed: ${error}`,
        operationId,
      });
    },

    addNotification: (notification) => {
      const id = `notif-${Date.now()}`;
      set((state) => {
        state.notifications.push({
          ...notification,
          id,
          timestamp: Date.now(),
        });
      });

      // Auto dismiss after 5 seconds
      if (notification.autoDismiss) {
        setTimeout(() => {
          get().dismissNotification(id);
        }, 5000);
      }
    },

    dismissNotification: (id) => {
      set((state) => {
        state.notifications = state.notifications.filter(n => n.id !== id);
      });
    },

    clearNotifications: () => {
      set((state) => {
        state.notifications = [];
      });
    },

    getPendingOperations: () => {
      return get().operations.filter(o => o.status === 'pending' || o.status === 'running');
    },

    getOperationStats: () => {
      const ops = get().operations;
      return {
        total: ops.length,
        pending: ops.filter(o => o.status === 'pending').length,
        running: ops.filter(o => o.status === 'running').length,
        completed: ops.filter(o => o.status === 'completed').length,
        failed: ops.filter(o => o.status === 'failed').length,
      };
    },
  }))
);

// Execute single operation
async function executeSingleOperation(
  operation: DFOLOperation,
  item: DFOLItem,
  outputDirectory: string,
  defaultProfile: string
): Promise<void> {
  const store = useDFOLStore.getState();

  switch (operation.mode) {
    case 'folder':
      await executeFolderDump(operation, item, outputDirectory, store);
      break;
    case 'txt':
      await executeTXTDump(operation, item, outputDirectory, store);
      break;
    case 'pdf':
      await executePDFDump(operation, item, outputDirectory, store);
      break;
    case 'compress':
      await executeCompress(operation, item, outputDirectory, item.selectedProfile || defaultProfile, store);
      break;
  }
}

async function executeFolderDump(
  operation: DFOLOperation,
  item: DFOLItem,
  outputDir: string,
  store: any
): Promise<void> {
  store.updateOperationStatus(operation.id, 'running', 0, 'Copying folder structure...');

  // Implementation depends on source type
  // For storage: use File System Access API
  // For Drive/GitHub: use respective APIs

  // Simulate progress
  for (let i = 0; i <= 100; i += 10) {
    await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 100));
    store.updateOperationStatus(operation.id, 'running', i, `Copying... ${i}%`);
  }

  store.completeOperation(operation.id, {
    outputPath: `${outputDir}/${item.name}_dump/`,
    size: item.size,
  });
}

async function executeTXTDump(
  operation: DFOLOperation,
  item: DFOLItem,
  outputDir: string,
  store: any
): Promise<void> {
  store.updateOperationStatus(operation.id, 'running', 0, 'Generating text dump...');

  // Traverse and generate text content
  let content = `DFOL TEXT DUMP\n==============\n\n`;
  content += `Source: ${item.name}\n`;
  content += `Type: ${item.type}\n`;
  content += `Date: ${new Date().toISOString()}\n\n`;

  // Add tree structure and file contents
  // ... traverse implementation ...

  content += `\n\nEND OF DUMP`;

  // Save to file
  const blob = new Blob([content], { type: 'text/plain' });
  const outputPath = `${outputDir}/${item.name}.txt`;

  // Save using appropriate API

  store.completeOperation(operation.id, {
    outputPath,
    size: blob.size,
  });
}

async function executePDFDump(
  operation: DFOLOperation,
  item: DFOLItem,
  outputDir: string,
  store: any
): Promise<void> {
  store.updateOperationStatus(operation.id, 'running', 0, 'Generating PDF dump...');

  const { jsPDF } = await import('jspdf');
  const doc = new jsPDF();

  // Add content to PDF
  doc.setFontSize(20);
  doc.text('DFOL PDF DUMP', 14, 20);

  doc.setFontSize(10);
  doc.text(`Source: ${item.name}`, 14, 30);
  doc.text(`Date: ${new Date().toLocaleString()}`, 14, 36);

  // Add tree and content tables
  // ...

  const pdfBlob = doc.output('blob');
  const outputPath = `${outputDir}/${item.name}.pdf`;

  store.completeOperation(operation.id, {
    outputPath,
    size: pdfBlob.size,
  });
}

async function executeCompress(
  operation: DFOLOperation,
  item: DFOLItem,
  outputDir: string,
  profileId: string,
  store: any
): Promise<void> {
  const profile = [...DEFAULT_PROFILES, ...useDFOLStore.getState().customProfiles]
    .find(p => p.id === profileId);

  if (!profile) throw new Error('Profile not found');

  store.updateOperationStatus(operation.id, 'running', 0, `Compressing with ${profile.name}...`);

  // Use Web Worker for compression
  const worker = new Worker(new URL('../workers/compression.worker.ts', import.meta.url));

  return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
    worker.onmessage = (e) => {
      const { type, progress, result, error } = e.data;

      if (type === 'progress') {
        store.updateOperationStatus(operation.id, 'running', progress, `Compressing... ${progress}%`);
      } else if (type === 'complete') {
        store.completeOperation(operation.id, {
          outputPath: `${outputDir}/${item.name}.${profile.format}`,
          size: result.size,
          checksum: result.checksum,
        });
        worker.terminate();
        resolve();
      } else if (type === 'error') {
        worker.terminate();
        reject(new Error(error));
      }
    };

    worker.postMessage({
      item,
      profile,
      outputDir,
    });
  });
}

import { SourceType } from '@/stores/appStore';

  // Storage-specific state
  path: string;

  history: { handle: FileSystemDirectoryHandle; name: string }[];
  viewMode: ViewMode;
  sortBy: SortBy;
  // Account/GitHub-specific state (for future)
  accountId: string | null;
  // UI state
  width: number; // in pixels
  isMinimized: boolean;
