FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/prakash-app/src/workers/extensionScanner.worker.ts
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
import { expose } from 'comlink';

interface ScanResult {
  extensions: Map<string, { count: number; totalSize: number }>;
  totalFiles: number;
  totalSize: number;
}

class ExtensionScanner {
  async scan(items: any[]): Promise<ScanResult> {
    const extensions = new Map<string, { count: number; totalSize: number }>();
    let totalFiles = 0;
    let totalSize = 0;

    const processItem = (item: any) => {
      const ext = this.getExtension(item.name);
      
      if (item.type === 'file' || item.kind === 'file') {
        totalFiles++;
        totalSize += item.size || 0;

        if (ext) {
          const existing = extensions.get(ext);
          if (existing) {
            existing.count++;
            existing.totalSize += item.size || 0;
          } else {
            extensions.set(ext, {
              count: 1,
              totalSize: item.size || 0,
            });
          }
        }
      }

      // Recursively process children
      if (item.children) {
        item.children.forEach(processItem);
      }
    };

    items.forEach(processItem);

    return {
      extensions,
      totalFiles,
      totalSize,
    };
  }

  private getExtension(filename: string): string | null {
    if (!filename || !filename.includes('.')) return null;
    const ext = filename.slice(filename.lastIndexOf('.')).toLowerCase();
    return ext.length > 1 ? ext : null;
  }

  async incrementalScan(
    existingExtensions: Map<string, { count: number; totalSize: number }>,
    newItems: any[]
  ): Promise<ScanResult> {
    const result = await this.scan(newItems);
    
    // Merge with existing
    for (const [ext, stats] of result.extensions) {
      const existing = existingExtensions.get(ext);
      if (existing) {
        existing.count += stats.count;
        existing.totalSize += stats.totalSize;
      } else {
        existingExtensions.set(ext, stats);
      }
    }

    return {
      extensions: existingExtensions,
      totalFiles: result.totalFiles,
      totalSize: result.totalSize,
    };
  }
}

expose(ExtensionScanner);
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/prakash-app/src/workers/compression.worker.ts
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
import { expose } from 'comlink';
import { ZipWriter, BlobWriter, BlobReader } from '@zip.js/zip.js';
import * as fflate from 'fflate';

interface CompressionTask {
  item: any;
  profile: {
    format: string;
    compressionLevel: string;
    password?: string;
  };
  outputDir: string;
}

async function compress(task: CompressionTask, onProgress: (progress: number) => void): Promise<{ size: number; checksum: string }> {
  const { item, profile } = task;
  
  // Initialize based on format
  switch (profile.format) {
    case 'zip':
      return await compressZip(item, profile, onProgress);
    case 'tar.gz':
    case 'tar.bz2':
      return await compressTar(item, profile, onProgress);
    default:
      throw new Error(`Format ${profile.format} not yet supported`);
  }
}

async function compressZip(
  item: any, 
  profile: any, 
  onProgress: (p: number) => void
): Promise<{ size: number; checksum: string }> {
  const zipWriter = new ZipWriter(new BlobWriter('application/zip'), {
    level: getCompressionLevel(profile.compressionLevel),
    password: profile.password,
  });

  // Add files to zip
  // This is a simplified version - actual implementation would traverse and add all files
  
  const blob = await zipWriter.close();
  const arrayBuffer = await blob.arrayBuffer();
  
  // Calculate checksum
  const checksum = await calculateChecksum(arrayBuffer);
  
  onProgress(100);
  
  return {
    size: blob.size,
    checksum,
  };
}

async function compressTar(
  item: any,
  profile: any,
  onProgress: (p: number) => void
): Promise<{ size: number; checksum: string }> {
  // Use fflate for gzip/bzip2 compression
  const compression = profile.format === 'tar.gz' ? fflate.gzipSync : fflate.strToU8;
  const level = getCompressionLevel(profile.compressionLevel);
  
  // Build tar archive then compress
  // Simplified implementation
  
  onProgress(100);
  
  return {
    size: 0,
    checksum: '',
  };
}

function getCompressionLevel(level: string): number {
  switch (level) {
    case 'store': return 0;
    case 'fast': return 3;
    case 'normal': return 6;
    case 'maximum': return 9;
    default: return 6;
  }
}

async function calculateChecksum(data: ArrayBuffer): Promise<string> {
  const hashBuffer = await crypto.subtle.digest('SHA-256', data);
  const hashArray = Array.from(new Uint8Array(hashBuffer));
  return hashArray.map(b => b.toString(16).padStart(2, '0')).join('');
}

// Web Worker message handler
self.onmessage = async (e) => {
  const { item, profile, outputDir } = e.data as CompressionTask;
  
  try {
    const result = await compress(
      { item, profile, outputDir },
      (progress) => {
        self.postMessage({ type: 'progress', progress });
      }
    );
    
    self.postMessage({ type: 'complete', result });
  } catch (error) {
    self.postMessage({ type: 'error', error: (error as Error).message });
  }
};

export {};

FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/prakash-app/src/App.tsx
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
import { BrowserRouter, Routes, Route, Navigate } from 'react-router-dom';
import { useEffect } from 'react';
import { MainApp } from './MainApp';
import { AdminPanel } from './components/Admin/AdminPanel';
import { NotificationBell } from './components/Notification/NotificationBell';
import { LiveLogPanel } from './components/Log/LiveLogPanel';
import { useLogStore } from './stores/logStore';

function App() {
  // Initialize logging
  useEffect(() => {
    const { logAction } = useLogStore.getState();
    
    // Log app start
    logAction('app_start', {
      userAgent: navigator.userAgent,
      platform: navigator.platform,
    }, 'system');

    // Setup global error handler
    window.onerror = (message, source, lineno, colno, error) => {
      logAction('uncaught_error', {
        message,
        source,
        lineno,
        colno,
        stack: error?.stack,
      }, 'system');
      return false;
    };

    // Setup unhandled promise rejection handler
    window.onunhandledrejection = (event) => {
      logAction('unhandled_rejection', {
        reason: event.reason?.toString(),
      }, 'system');
    };
  }, []);

  return (
    <BrowserRouter>
      <Routes>
        <Route path="/" element={<MainApp />} />
        <Route path="/admin" element={<AdminPanel />} />
        <Route path="*" element={<Navigate to="/" replace />} />
      </Routes>
      
      {/* Global overlays */}
      <NotificationBell />
      <LiveLogPanel />
    </BrowserRouter>
  );
}

export default App;

        "accordion-up": "accordion-up 0.2s ease-out",
      },
    },
  },
  plugins: [require("tailwindcss-animate")],
}

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/prakash-app/auto-setup.js
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
// auto-setup.js
import { execSync, spawn } from 'child_process';
import fs from 'fs';
import path from 'path';
import { fileURLToPath } from 'url';

const __dirname = path.dirname(fileURLToPath(import.meta.url));
const packageJsonPath = path.join(__dirname, 'package.json');
const nodeModulesPath = path.join(__dirname, 'node_modules');

// Read package.json
const packageJson = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(packageJsonPath, 'utf8'));
const requiredDeps = {
  ...packageJson.dependencies,
  ...packageJson.devDependencies,
};

// Check which dependencies are missing
const missing = [];
for (const dep in requiredDeps) {
  const depPath = path.join(nodeModulesPath, dep);
  if (!fs.existsSync(depPath)) {
    missing.push(`${dep}@${requiredDeps[dep]}`);
  }
}

if (missing.length > 0) {
  console.log('\x1b[33m%s\x1b[0m', '⚠️  Missing dependencies detected. Installing...');
  console.log('Missing:', missing.map(m => m.split('@')[0]).join(', '));
  try {
    execSync(`npm install ${missing.join(' ')} --legacy-peer-deps`, { stdio: 'inherit' });
    console.log('\x1b[32m%s\x1b[0m', '✅ All dependencies installed successfully.');
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('\x1b[31m%s\x1b[0m', '❌ Failed to install dependencies:', error.message);
    process.exit(1);
  }
} else {
  console.log('\x1b[32m%s\x1b[0m', '✅ All dependencies are already installed.');
}

// Start Vite directly (NOT npm run dev again)
console.log('\x1b[36m%s\x1b[0m', '🚀 Starting development server...');
const vite = spawn('npx', ['vite', '--host', '0.0.0.0'], { 
  stdio: 'inherit', 
  shell: true 
});

vite.on('close', (code) => {
  process.exit(code);
});
